# 股票交易系统详细开发文档
重要提示:此程序是在 MACOS 系统下开发,请使用虚拟环境,先按文档的要求搭建好环境;程序开发结束是要部署到云服务器,系统是 UBUNTU SERVER22+,故程序要有多系统自适应的功能(不用适配 WINDOWS 系统);先开发后端,确保按照 TUSHATE 和 AKSHARE 官方文档要求设计数据库;需要创建一键部署后端和一键部署前端服务的自动化脚本,在 UBUNTU 系统中请使用 SYSTEMCTL 启动后端及前端服务及在虚拟环境下运行股票交易系统;所有测试必须是从数据源获取到的真实数据,不能使用虚拟数据;测试完成后,所有测试文件都必须删除;

## 📋 技术栈选择总结

### 🎯 最终确定的技术栈
- **前端**: **React.js 18+** ✅
- **后端**: **FastAPI** ✅  
- **主数据库**: **PostgreSQL 15** ✅
- **缓存数据库**: **Redis 7** ✅
- **数据源**: **TUshare (历史数据优先) + AKshare (实时数据优先)** ✅
- **WEB端口**: **8080** (固定端口，自动处理占用冲突)
- **后端端口**: **9000** (固定端口，自动处理占用冲突)

## 1. 项目概述

### 1.1 项目简介
基于 TUshare 和 AKshare API 的股票交易系统，提供实时行情数据、技术分析、自选股管理、九转系列选股等功能。

### 1.2 系统部署环境

#### 1.2.1 生产环境配置
- **部署平台**: 云服务器 (腾讯云)
- **操作系统**: **Ubuntu Server 22.04 LTS** 及以上版本
- **运行模式**: **24小时不间断运行**
- **服务架构**: 微服务架构，支持水平扩展
- **容器化**: Docker + Docker Compose 部署

#### 1.2.2 系统运行时间表

**A股交易日运行逻辑：**

```
09:30 - 开始实时数据同步
├── 实时行情数据获取 (AKShare)
├── 数据缓存到 Redis
├── 实时技术指标计算
└── WebSocket 推送到前端

15:00 - 交易结束后数据处理
├── 停止实时数据获取
├── Redis → PostgreSQL 数据迁移
├── 历史数据完整性检查
└── 触发九转选股算法

16:00 - 九转系列选股执行
├── 获取当日完整数据
├── 计算九转买入/卖出信号
├── 更新选股结果表
└── 生成选股报告

17:00 - 数据清理与维护
├── 清理Redis临时数据
├── 数据库索引优化
├── 日志文件归档
└── 系统健康检查

非交易时间 (17:00-次日09:30)
├── 系统监控与维护
├── 数据备份
├── 财务数据更新
└── 系统性能优化
```

#### 1.2.3 数据流转策略

**实时数据处理流程：**
```
AKShare API → Redis缓存 → WebSocket推送 → 前端展示
     ↓
PostgreSQL历史存储 (交易结束后)
```

**数据迁移策略对比：**

| 方案 | 优势 | 劣势 | 推荐度 |
|------|------|------|--------|
| **Redis→PostgreSQL直接迁移** | 速度快、数据一致性好 | Redis内存占用高 | ⭐⭐⭐⭐⭐ |
| **清空Redis重新获取** | 内存占用低、数据最新 | 网络请求多、耗时长 | ⭐⭐⭐ |

**最优方案选择：Redis→PostgreSQL直接迁移**
- 交易结束后立即将Redis中的实时数据批量写入PostgreSQL
- 数据写入完成后清空Redis当日数据
- 保留最近3个交易日的Redis数据作为快速查询缓存

#### 1.2.4 系统监控与告警

**24小时监控指标：**
- 系统CPU、内存、磁盘使用率
- 数据库连接数和查询性能
- Redis缓存命中率和内存使用
- API响应时间和错误率
- 数据获取成功率和延迟

**自动告警机制：**
- 系统资源使用超过80%时告警
- 数据获取失败率超过5%时告警
- API响应时间超过3秒时告警
- 数据库连接异常时立即告警

### 1.3 技术栈选择

#### 1.3.1 最优技术栈组合
经过综合评估性能、开发效率、生态完整性和维护成本，确定使用以下技术栈：

- **前端**: **React.js** (选择理由：生态丰富、性能优秀、社区活跃、组件化程度高)
- **后端**: **FastAPI** (选择理由：高性能、自动API文档、类型提示、异步支持)
- **主数据库**: **PostgreSQL** (选择理由：功能强大、JSON支持、扩展性好、数据一致性强)
- **缓存数据库**: **Redis** (选择理由：高性能、丰富数据结构、集群支持、持久化选项)
- **数据源策略**: 
  - **历史数据优先**: **TUshare** (数据质量高、覆盖全面、接口稳定)
  - **实时数据优先**: **AKshare** (更新频率高、延迟低、免费使用)
  - **容错机制**: 主数据源失败时自动切换到备用数据源

#### 1.3.2 技术栈对比分析

**前端框架对比：**
| 特性 | React.js ✅ | Vue.js |
|------|-------------|---------|
| 学习曲线 | 中等 | 较低 |
| 性能 | 优秀 | 优秀 |
| 生态系统 | 非常丰富 | 丰富 |
| 企业采用度 | 很高 | 高 |
| 组件复用性 | 很好 | 好 |

**后端框架对比：**
| 特性 | FastAPI ✅ | Flask | Django | Node.js |
|------|------------|-------|---------|---------|
| 性能 | 很高 | 中等 | 中等 | 高 |
| 开发效率 | 高 | 高 | 很高 | 中等 |
| API文档 | 自动生成 | 手动 | 手动 | 手动 |
| 异步支持 | 原生 | 扩展 | 扩展 | 原生 |
| 类型安全 | 很好 | 一般 | 一般 | TypeScript |

**数据库对比：**
| 特性 | PostgreSQL ✅ | MySQL |
|------|---------------|--------|
| JSON支持 | 原生优秀 | 基础 |
| 扩展性 | 很好 | 好 |
| 数据一致性 | 很强 | 强 |
| 复杂查询 | 很好 | 好 |
| 维护成本 | 低 | 低 |

**数据源对比：**
| 特性 | TUshare | AKshare |
|------|---------|---------|
| 历史数据质量 | ✅ 很高 | 高 |
| 实时数据延迟 | 中等 | ✅ 很低 |
| 数据覆盖范围 | ✅ 很全面 | 全面 |
| 接口稳定性 | ✅ 很稳定 | 稳定 |
| 使用成本 | 付费 | ✅ 免费 |
| API限制 | 有限制 | ✅ 较宽松 |
| **使用策略** | **历史数据优先** | **实时数据优先** |

### 1.4 系统配置

#### 1.4.1 端口配置
- **WEB服务端口**: 固定使用 **8080** 端口
- **端口占用处理**: 如果8080端口被占用，系统将自动终结占用进程并启动服务
- **后端服务端口**: 固定使用 **9000** 端口
#### 1.4.2 端口占用检测与处理脚本
```bash
#!/bin/bash
# scripts/check_port.sh

PORT=8080
echo "检查端口 $PORT 是否被占用..."

# 检查端口占用
PID=$(lsof -ti:$PORT)

if [ ! -z "$PID" ]; then
    echo "端口 $PORT 被进程 $PID 占用，正在终结进程..."
    kill -9 $PID
    sleep 2
    
    # 再次检查
    PID=$(lsof -ti:$PORT)
    if [ ! -z "$PID" ]; then
        echo "强制终结进程 $PID..."
        sudo kill -9 $PID
    fi
    
    echo "端口 $PORT 已释放"
else
    echo "端口 $PORT 未被占用"
fi

echo "启动服务在端口 $PORT..."
```

#### 1.4.3 Python端口处理
```python
# utils/port_manager.py
import os
import signal
import psutil
import socket

class PortManager:
    def __init__(self, port=8080):
        self.port = port
    
    def is_port_in_use(self):
        """检查端口是否被占用"""
        with socket.socket(socket.AF_INET, socket.SOCK_STREAM) as s:
            return s.connect_ex(('localhost', self.port)) == 0
    
    def kill_process_on_port(self):
        """终结占用端口的进程"""
        for proc in psutil.process_iter(['pid', 'name', 'connections']):
            try:
                for conn in proc.info['connections'] or []:
                    if conn.laddr.port == self.port:
                        print(f"终结进程 {proc.info['pid']} ({proc.info['name']})")
                        proc.kill()
                        return True
            except (psutil.NoSuchProcess, psutil.AccessDenied):
                continue
        return False
    
    def ensure_port_available(self):
        """确保端口可用"""
        if self.is_port_in_use():
            print(f"端口 {self.port} 被占用，正在释放...")
            if self.kill_process_on_port():
                print(f"端口 {self.port} 已释放")
            else:
                raise Exception(f"无法释放端口 {self.port}")
        else:
            print(f"端口 {self.port} 可用")
```

## 2. 系统架构

### 2.1 整体架构图
```
┌─────────────────┐    ┌─────────────────┐    ┌─────────────────┐
│   前端应用      │    │   后端API服务   │    │   数据获取服务  │
│   React.js      │◄──►│   FastAPI       │◄──►│   TUshare       │
│   Port: 8080    │    │   Port: 9000    │    │   AKshare       │
└─────────────────┘    └─────────────────┘    └─────────────────┘
                              │
                              ▼
                    ┌─────────────────┐
                    │   数据存储层    │
                    │   PostgreSQL    │
                    │   Redis         │
                    │   Port: 5432    │
                    │   Port: 6379    │
                    └─────────────────┘
```

### 2.2 服务模块划分
- **数据获取模块**: 负责从 TUshare 和 AKshare 获取数据
- **数据处理模块**: 数据清洗、计算技术指标
- **缓存模块**: Redis实时数据缓存
- **API服务模块**: 提供RESTful API接口
- **前端展示模块**: 用户界面和交互

## 3. 数据库设计

### 3.1 主数据库表结构 (PostgreSQL/MySQL)

#### 3.1.1 股票基础信息表 (stocks)
```sql
CREATE TABLE stocks (
    id SERIAL PRIMARY KEY,
    stock_code VARCHAR(10) NOT NULL UNIQUE,
    stock_name VARCHAR(50) NOT NULL,
    market VARCHAR(10) NOT NULL, -- SH, SZ, HK, US
    industry VARCHAR(50),
    concept VARCHAR(200),
    region VARCHAR(50),
    list_date DATE,
    created_at TIMESTAMP DEFAULT CURRENT_TIMESTAMP,
    updated_at TIMESTAMP DEFAULT CURRENT_TIMESTAMP
);
```

#### 3.1.2 历史行情数据表 (stock_daily)
```sql
CREATE TABLE stock_daily (
    id SERIAL PRIMARY KEY,
    stock_code VARCHAR(10) NOT NULL,
    trade_date DATE NOT NULL,
    open_price DECIMAL(10,3),
    high_price DECIMAL(10,3),
    low_price DECIMAL(10,3),
    close_price DECIMAL(10,3),
    volume BIGINT,
    amount DECIMAL(15,2),
    turnover_rate DECIMAL(8,4),
    pe_ratio DECIMAL(8,2),
    pb_ratio DECIMAL(8,2),
    market_cap DECIMAL(15,2),
    created_at TIMESTAMP DEFAULT CURRENT_TIMESTAMP,
    UNIQUE(stock_code, trade_date)
);
```

#### 3.1.3 技术指标表 (technical_indicators)
```sql
CREATE TABLE technical_indicators (
    id SERIAL PRIMARY KEY,
    stock_code VARCHAR(10) NOT NULL,
    trade_date DATE NOT NULL,
    macd_dif DECIMAL(8,4),
    macd_dea DECIMAL(8,4),
    macd_histogram DECIMAL(8,4),
    kdj_k DECIMAL(8,4),
    kdj_d DECIMAL(8,4),
    kdj_j DECIMAL(8,4),
    rsi_6 DECIMAL(8,4),
    rsi_12 DECIMAL(8,4),
    rsi_24 DECIMAL(8,4),
    ma_5 DECIMAL(10,3),
    ma_10 DECIMAL(10,3),
    ma_20 DECIMAL(10,3),
    ma_60 DECIMAL(10,3),
    created_at TIMESTAMP DEFAULT CURRENT_TIMESTAMP,
    UNIQUE(stock_code, trade_date)
);
```

#### 3.1.4 用户表 (users)
```sql
CREATE TABLE users (
    id SERIAL PRIMARY KEY,
    username VARCHAR(50) NOT NULL UNIQUE,
    email VARCHAR(100) NOT NULL UNIQUE,
    password_hash VARCHAR(255) NOT NULL,
    created_at TIMESTAMP DEFAULT CURRENT_TIMESTAMP,
    updated_at TIMESTAMP DEFAULT CURRENT_TIMESTAMP
);
```

#### 3.1.5 自选股表 (user_favorites)
```sql
CREATE TABLE user_favorites (
    id SERIAL PRIMARY KEY,
    user_id INTEGER REFERENCES users(id),
    stock_code VARCHAR(10) NOT NULL,
    note TEXT,
    created_at TIMESTAMP DEFAULT CURRENT_TIMESTAMP,
    UNIQUE(user_id, stock_code)
);
```

#### 3.1.6 九转选股结果表 (nine_turn_signals)
```sql
CREATE TABLE nine_turn_signals (
    id SERIAL PRIMARY KEY,
    stock_code VARCHAR(10) NOT NULL,
    signal_date DATE NOT NULL,
    signal_type VARCHAR(20) NOT NULL, -- buy_setup, sell_setup, buy_countdown, sell_countdown
    signal_value INTEGER,
    price DECIMAL(10,3),
    created_at TIMESTAMP DEFAULT CURRENT_TIMESTAMP,
    UNIQUE(stock_code, signal_date, signal_type)
);
```

#### 3.1.7 每日基本面数据表 (daily_basic)
```sql
CREATE TABLE daily_basic (
    id SERIAL PRIMARY KEY,
    stock_code VARCHAR(10) NOT NULL,
    trade_date DATE NOT NULL,
    close_price DECIMAL(10,3),
    turnover_rate DECIMAL(8,4),
    turnover_rate_f DECIMAL(8,4),
    volume_ratio DECIMAL(8,4),
    pe_ratio DECIMAL(8,2),
    pe_ratio_ttm DECIMAL(8,2),
    pb_ratio DECIMAL(8,2),
    ps_ratio DECIMAL(8,2),
    ps_ratio_ttm DECIMAL(8,2),
    dv_ratio DECIMAL(8,4),
    dv_ttm DECIMAL(8,4),
    total_share DECIMAL(15,2),
    float_share DECIMAL(15,2),
    free_share DECIMAL(15,2),
    total_mv DECIMAL(15,2),
    circ_mv DECIMAL(15,2),
    created_at TIMESTAMP DEFAULT CURRENT_TIMESTAMP,
    UNIQUE(stock_code, trade_date)
);
```

#### 3.1.8 资金流向数据表 (money_flow)
```sql
CREATE TABLE money_flow (
    id SERIAL PRIMARY KEY,
    stock_code VARCHAR(10) NOT NULL,
    trade_date DATE NOT NULL,
    buy_sm_vol DECIMAL(15,2),
    buy_sm_amount DECIMAL(15,2),

    sell_elg_amount DECIMAL(15,2),
    net_mf_vol DECIMAL(15,2),
    net_mf_amount DECIMAL(15,2),
    created_at TIMESTAMP DEFAULT CURRENT_TIMESTAMP,
    UNIQUE(stock_code, trade_date)
);
```

#### 3.1.10 资产负债表数据表 (balance_sheet)
```sql
CREATE TABLE balance_sheet (
    id SERIAL PRIMARY KEY,

    ann_date DATE,
    f_ann_date DATE,
    end_date DATE NOT NULL,

    reinsur_receiv DECIMAL(15,2),
    reinsur_res_receiv DECIMAL(15,2),
    pur_resale_fa DECIMAL(15,2),
    oth_cur_assets DECIMAL(15,2),
    total_nca DECIMAL(15,2),
    fa_avail_for_sale DECIMAL(15,2),
    htm_invest DECIMAL(15,2),
    lt_eqt_invest DECIMAL(15,2),
    invest_real_estate DECIMAL(15,2),
    time_deposits DECIMAL(15,2),
    oth_assets DECIMAL(15,2),
    lt_rec DECIMAL(15,2),
    fix_assets DECIMAL(15,2),
    cip DECIMAL(15,2),

);

    created_at TIMESTAMP DEFAULT CURRENT_TIMESTAMP,

);

#### 3.1.16 龙虎榜数据表 (top_list)

CREATE TABLE top_list (
    id SERIAL PRIMARY KEY,
    trade_date DATE NOT NULL,
    stock_code VARCHAR(10) NOT NULL,
    stock_name VARCHAR(50),

    amount_rate DECIMAL(8,4),
    float_values DECIMAL(15,2),
    reason VARCHAR(200),
    created_at TIMESTAMP DEFAULT CURRENT_TIMESTAMP,
    UNIQUE(trade_date, stock_code)
);
```

#### 3.1.17 大宗交易数据表 (block_trade)

CREATE TABLE block_trade (

    amount DECIMAL(15,2),

    UNIQUE(stock_code, trade_date, buyer, seller)
);
```

#### 3.1.22 板块数据表 (sectors)
```sql
CREATE TABLE sectors (
    id SERIAL PRIMARY KEY,
    sector_code VARCHAR(20) NOT NULL UNIQUE,
    sector_name VARCHAR(50) NOT NULL,
    sector_type VARCHAR(20), -- industry, concept, region

    created_at TIMESTAMP DEFAULT CURRENT_TIMESTAMP,
    updated_at TIMESTAMP DEFAULT CURRENT_TIMESTAMP
);
```

#### 3.1.23 板块成分股数据表 (sector_stocks)
```sql
CREATE TABLE sector_stocks (
    id SERIAL PRIMARY KEY,
    sector_code VARCHAR(20) NOT NULL,
    stock_code VARCHAR(10) NOT NULL,
    in_date DATE,
    out_date DATE,
    is_new VARCHAR(1),
    created_at TIMESTAMP DEFAULT CURRENT_TIMESTAMP,
    UNIQUE(sector_code, stock_code, in_date)
);
```

#### 3.1.24 宏观经济数据表 (macro_data)
```sql
CREATE TABLE macro_data (
    id SERIAL PRIMARY KEY,
    indicator_code VARCHAR(20) NOT NULL,
    indicator_name VARCHAR(50),
    period DATE NOT NULL,
    value DECIMAL(15,4),
    unit VARCHAR(20),
    created_at TIMESTAMP DEFAULT CURRENT_TIMESTAMP,
    UNIQUE(indicator_code, period)
);
```

#### 3.1.25 跨市场数据表 (cross_market)
```sql
CREATE TABLE cross_market (
    id SERIAL PRIMARY KEY,
    market VARCHAR(20) NOT NULL, -- US, HK, CRYPTO
    symbol VARCHAR(20) NOT NULL,
    name VARCHAR(100),
    price DECIMAL(15,6),
    change_pct DECIMAL(8,4),
    volume DECIMAL(20,2),
    market_cap DECIMAL(20,2),
    update_time TIMESTAMP,
    created_at TIMESTAMP DEFAULT CURRENT_TIMESTAMP,
    UNIQUE(market, symbol, DATE(update_time))
);
```

## 4. API 接口设计

### 4.1 数据源说明
- **实时数据**: 全部使用 AKshare 获取，免费且更新频率高
- **历史数据**: 优先使用 TUshare (2000积分内接口)，超出积分限制的接口使用 AKshare
- **概念股数据**: 使用 AKshare 
- **限售股解禁**: 使用 AKshare 

### 4.2 基础配置
- **Base URL**: `http://localhost:9000/api/v1`
- **认证方式**: JWT Token
- **数据格式**: JSON
- **端口**: 9000 (固定端口，自动处理占用冲突)


### 4.4 股票数据接口

#### 4.4.1 获取股票列表
```
GET /stocks?page=1&size=20&market=SH&keyword=平安

Response:
{
    "code": 200,
    "message": "获取成功",
    "data": {
        "total": 4500,
        "page": 1,
        "size": 20,
        "stocks": [
            {
                "code": "000001",
                "name": "平安银行",
                "market": "SZ",
                "industry": "银行",
                "price": 12.34,
                "change_pct": 0.98
            }
        ]
    }
}
```

#### 4.4.2 获取股票详情
```
GET /stocks/{stock_code}

Response:
{
    "code": 200,
    "message": "获取成功",
    "data": {
        "code": "000001",
        "name": "平安银行",
        "market": "SZ",
        "industry": "银行",
        "concept": "银行概念,金融科技",
        "region": "广东",
        "list_date": "1991-04-03",
        "realtime": {
            "price": 12.34,
            "change": 0.12,
            "change_pct": 0.98,
            "volume": 1234567,
            "amount": 15234567.89,
            "turnover_rate": 1.23,
            "pe_ratio": 5.67,
            "pb_ratio": 0.89,
            "market_cap": 2345678901.23
        }
    }
}
```

#### 4.4.3 获取K线数据
```
GET /stocks/{stock_code}/kline?period=daily&start_date=2024-01-01&end_date=2024-01-31

Response:
{
    "code": 200,
    "message": "获取成功",
    "data": [
        {
            "date": "2024-01-15",
            "open": 12.20,
            "high": 12.45,
            "low": 12.10,
            "close": 12.34,
            "volume": 1234567,
            "amount": 15234567.89
        }
    ]
}
```

#### 4.4.4 获取技术指标
```
GET /stocks/{stock_code}/indicators?start_date=2024-01-01&end_date=2024-01-31

Response:
{
    "code": 200,
    "message": "获取成功",
    "data": [
        {
            "date": "2024-01-15",
            "macd": {
                "dif": 0.12,
                "dea": 0.08,
                "histogram": 0.04
            },

                "k": 65.23,
                "d": 62.45,
                "j": 70.79
            },
            "rsi": {
                "rsi_6": 58.23,

                "rsi_24": 52.34
            }
        }
    ]
}
```

### 4.5 自选股接口

#### 4.5.1 获取自选股列表
```
GET /favorites
Authorization: Bearer {token}

Response:
{
    "code": 200,
    "message": "获取成功",
    "data": [
        {
            "id": 1,
            "stock_code": "000001",
            "stock_name": "平安银行",
            "note": "关注银行板块",
            "price": 12.34,
            "change_pct": 0.98,
            "created_at": "2024-01-15 10:30:00"
        }
    ]
}
```

#### 4.5.2 添加自选股
```
POST /favorites
Authorization: Bearer {token}
Content-Type: application/json

Request:
{
    "stock_code": "000001",
    "note": "关注银行板块"
}

Response:
{
    "code": 200,
    "message": "添加成功",
    "data": {
        "id": 1
    }
}
```

### 4.6 九转选股接口

#### 4.6.1 获取九转信号

GET /nine-turn/signals?signal_type=buy_setup&date=2024-01-15

{
    "code": 200,
    "message": "获取成功",
    "data": [
        {
            "stock_code": "000001",

            "signal_value": 9,

            "signal_date": "2024-01-15"

    ]
}
```

## 5. 前端页面设计 (React.js)

### 5.1 技术栈详细配置
- **框架**: React.js 18+
- **状态管理**: Redux Toolkit
- **路由**: React Router v6
- **UI组件库**: Ant Design / Material-UI
- **图表库**: ECharts / Chart.js
- **HTTP客户端**: Axios
- **WebSocket**: Socket.io-client
- **构建工具**: Vite / Create React App
- **开发端口**: 3000

### 5.2 项目结构
```
src/
├── components/          # 公共组件
│   ├── Header/         # 头部导航
│   ├── Sidebar/        # 侧边栏
│   ├── StockCard/      # 股票卡片
│   ├── Chart/          # 图表组件
│   └── Table/          # 表格组件
├── pages/              # 页面组件
│   ├── Home/           # 首页
│   ├── StockDetail/    # 股票详情页
│   ├── Favorites/      # 自选股页
│   ├── Trading/        # 交易页
│   └── NineTurn/       # 九转选股页
├── services/           # API服务
├── utils/              # 工具函数
└── styles/             # 样式文件
```

### 5.2 首页设计 (Home)

#### 5.2.1 组件结构
```jsx
// Home.jsx
import React, { useState, useEffect } from 'react';
import Header from '../components/Header';
import IndexPanel from '../components/IndexPanel';
import StockList from '../components/StockList';
import MarketOverview from '../components/MarketOverview';

const Home = () => {
    const [indices, setIndices] = useState([]);
    const [stocks, setStocks] = useState([]);
    
    useEffect(() => {
        fetchIndices();
        fetchStocks();
    }, []);
    
    return (
        <div className="home-container">
            <Header />
            <div className="main-content">
                <IndexPanel indices={indices} />
                <MarketOverview />
                <StockList stocks={stocks} />
            </div>
        </div>
    );
};
```

#### 5.2.2 功能模块
- **指数面板**: 显示上证指数、深证成指、创业板指等
- **市场概览**: A股、港股、美股市场状态
- **股票列表**: 支持搜索、筛选、排序
- **实时更新**: WebSocket 连接实时数据

### 5.3 股票详情页设计 (StockDetail)

#### 5.3.1 组件结构
```jsx
// StockDetail.jsx
import React, { useState, useEffect } from 'react';
import { useParams } from 'react-router-dom';
import StockInfo from '../components/StockInfo';
import KLineChart from '../components/KLineChart';
import TechnicalIndicators from '../components/TechnicalIndicators';
import NewsPanel from '../components/NewsPanel';

const StockDetail = () => {
    const { stockCode } = useParams();
    const [stockData, setStockData] = useState(null);
    const [klineData, setKlineData] = useState([]);
    
    return (
        <div className="stock-detail-container">
            <StockInfo data={stockData} />
            <div className="chart-section">
                <KLineChart data={klineData} />
                <TechnicalIndicators stockCode={stockCode} />
            </div>
            <NewsPanel stockCode={stockCode} />
        </div>
    );
};
```

#### 5.3.2 功能模块
- **股票基本信息**: 代码、名称、行业、概念等
- **实时行情**: 价格、涨跌幅、成交量等
- **K线图表**: 支持日K、周K、月K切换
- **技术指标**: MACD、KDJ、RSI等
- **分时图**: 实时分时走势
- **资金流向**: 主力资金流入流出

#### 5.4.1 功能特性
- 自选股列表展示
- 添加/删除自选股

- 实时价格更新
- 涨跌幅排序

### 5.5 九转选股页设计 (NineTurn)

#### 5.4.1 功能特性
- 九转买入信号股票列表

- 信号强度显示
- 历史信号回测
- 一键添加到自选股

## 6. 数据获取与处理

### 6.1 数据源策略设计

#### 6.1.1 数据源优先级策略
```
历史数据获取策略：
TUshare (主，2000积分限制) → AKshare (备用) → 缓存数据 (兜底)

实时数据获取策略：
AKshare (主，免费无限制) → 缓存数据 (兜底)

特殊数据获取策略：
- 概念股数据：AKshare (TUshare concept 接口需要5000积分)
- 限售股解禁：AKshare (TUshare share_float 接口需要3000积分)
- 所有实时行情：AKshare (免费且更新频率高)
```

#### 6.1.2 数据源选择原则
- **历史数据**: TUshare 优先 (2000积分内接口)
  - 数据质量更高，经过专业清洗
  - 历史数据完整性好
  - 财务数据准确性高
  - 注意：超出2000积分的接口改用 AKshare
  
- **实时数据**: AKshare 优先 (全部使用)
  - 更新频率更高，延迟更低
  - 免费使用，无API调用限制
  - 实时行情数据丰富
  - 避免 TUshare 积分消耗

- **概念股数据**: AKshare 独有
  - TUshare concept/concept_detail 接口需要5000积分
  - AKshare 提供免费的概念板块数据
  
- **限售股解禁**: AKshare 独有
  - TUshare share_float 接口需要3000积分
  - AKshare 提供免费的限售股解禁数据

#### 6.1.3 容错与重试机制
```python
# services/data_source_manager.py
import asyncio
import logging
from typing import Optional, Dict, Any
from enum import Enum

class DataSourceType(Enum):
    TUSHARE = "tushare"
    AKSHARE = "akshare"

class DataType(Enum):
    HISTORICAL = "historical"
    REALTIME = "realtime"

class DataSourceManager:
    def __init__(self):
        self.retry_count = 3
        self.retry_delay = 1  # 秒
        
    async def get_data_with_fallback(self, data_type: DataType, **kwargs) -> Optional[Dict[Any, Any]]:
        """
        根据数据类型选择主数据源，失败时自动切换到备用数据源
        """
        if data_type == DataType.HISTORICAL:
            primary_source = DataSourceType.TUSHARE
            fallback_source = DataSourceType.AKSHARE
        else:  # REALTIME
            primary_source = DataSourceType.AKSHARE
            fallback_source = DataSourceType.TUSHARE
        
        # 尝试主数据源
        data = await self._fetch_with_retry(primary_source, **kwargs)
        if data is not None:
            logging.info(f"成功从主数据源 {primary_source.value} 获取数据")
            return data
        
        # 主数据源失败，尝试备用数据源
        logging.warning(f"主数据源 {primary_source.value} 失败，切换到备用数据源 {fallback_source.value}")
        data = await self._fetch_with_retry(fallback_source, **kwargs)
        if data is not None:
            logging.info(f"成功从备用数据源 {fallback_source.value} 获取数据")
            return data
        
        # 所有数据源都失败
        logging.error("所有数据源都失败，尝试从缓存获取数据")
        return await self._get_cached_data(**kwargs)
    
    async def _fetch_with_retry(self, source: DataSourceType, **kwargs) -> Optional[Dict[Any, Any]]:
        """
        带重试机制的数据获取
        """
        for attempt in range(self.retry_count):
            try:
                if source == DataSourceType.TUSHARE:
                    return await self._fetch_from_tushare(**kwargs)
                else:
                    return await self._fetch_from_akshare(**kwargs)
            except Exception as e:
                logging.warning(f"数据源 {source.value} 第 {attempt + 1} 次尝试失败: {e}")
                if attempt < self.retry_count - 1:
                    await asyncio.sleep(self.retry_delay * (attempt + 1))  # 指数退避
        
        return None
    
    async def _fetch_from_tushare(self, **kwargs) -> Dict[Any, Any]:
        """从TUshare获取数据"""
        # TUshare API调用逻辑
        pass
    
    async def _fetch_from_akshare(self, **kwargs) -> Dict[Any, Any]:
        """从AKshare获取数据"""
        # AKshare API调用逻辑
        pass
    
    async def _get_cached_data(self, **kwargs) -> Optional[Dict[Any, Any]]:
        """从缓存获取数据作为兜底"""
        # 缓存数据获取逻辑
        pass
```

### 6.2 数据源配置

#### 6.2.1 TUshare 配置 (历史数据优先)
```python
# config/tushare_config.py
import tushare as ts
from typing import Optional, Dict, Any, List
import pandas as pd
from datetime import datetime

class TushareConfig:
    def __init__(self, token: str):
        self.token = token
        ts.set_token(token)
        self.pro = ts.pro_api()
    
    def get_stock_basic(self) -> pd.DataFrame:
        """获取股票基础信息 - 包含完整字段"""
        return self.pro.stock_basic(
            exchange='',
            list_status='L',
            fields='ts_code,symbol,name,area,industry,fullname,enname,cnspell,market,exchange,curr_type,list_status,list_date,delist_date,is_hs'
        )
    
    def get_daily_data(self, ts_code: str, start_date: str, end_date: str) -> pd.DataFrame:
        """获取历史日线数据 - 完整字段"""
        return self.pro.daily(
            ts_code=ts_code,
            start_date=start_date,
            end_date=end_date,
            fields='ts_code,trade_date,open,high,low,close,pre_close,change,pct_chg,vol,amount'
        )
    
    def get_daily_basic(self, ts_code: str, start_date: str, end_date: str) -> pd.DataFrame:
        """获取每日基本面数据 - TUshare Pro新增重要接口"""
        return self.pro.daily_basic(
            ts_code=ts_code,
            start_date=start_date,
            end_date=end_date,
            fields='ts_code,trade_date,close,turnover_rate,turnover_rate_f,volume_ratio,pe,pe_ttm,pb,ps,ps_ttm,dv_ratio,dv_ttm,total_share,float_share,free_share,total_mv,circ_mv'
        )
    
    def get_moneyflow(self, ts_code: str, start_date: str, end_date: str) -> pd.DataFrame:
        """获取个股资金流向 - TUshare Pro专业数据"""
        return self.pro.moneyflow(
            ts_code=ts_code,
            start_date=start_date,
            end_date=end_date,
            fields='ts_code,trade_date,buy_sm_vol,buy_sm_amount,sell_sm_vol,sell_sm_amount,buy_md_vol,buy_md_amount,sell_md_vol,sell_md_amount,buy_lg_vol,buy_lg_amount,sell_lg_vol,sell_lg_amount,buy_elg_vol,buy_elg_amount,sell_elg_vol,sell_elg_amount,net_mf_vol,net_mf_amount'
        )
    
    def get_income_statement(self, ts_code: str, period: str) -> pd.DataFrame:
        """获取利润表 - 完整财务数据"""
        return self.pro.income(
            ts_code=ts_code,
            period=period,
            fields='ts_code,ann_date,f_ann_date,end_date,report_type,comp_type,total_revenue,revenue,int_income,prem_earned,comm_income,n_commis_income,n_oth_income,n_oth_b_income,prem_income,out_prem,une_prem_reser,reins_income,n_sec_tb_income,n_sec_uw_income,n_asset_mg_income,oth_b_income,fv_value_chg_gain,invest_income,ass_invest_income,forex_gain,total_cogs,oper_cost,int_exp,comm_exp,biz_tax_surchg,sell_exp,admin_exp,fin_exp,assets_impair_loss,prem_refund,compens_payout,reser_insur_liab,div_payt,reins_exp,oper_exp,compens_payout_refu,insur_reser_refu,reins_cost_refund,other_bus_cost,operate_profit,non_oper_income,non_oper_exp,nca_disploss,total_profit,income_tax,n_income,n_income_attr_p,minority_gain,oth_compr_income,t_compr_income,compr_inc_attr_p,compr_inc_attr_m_s,ebit,ebitda,insurance_exp,undist_profit,distable_profit,basic_eps,diluted_eps'
        )
    
    def get_balance_sheet(self, ts_code: str, period: str) -> pd.DataFrame:
        """获取资产负债表 - 完整财务数据"""
        return self.pro.balancesheet(
            ts_code=ts_code,
            period=period,
            fields='ts_code,ann_date,f_ann_date,end_date,report_type,comp_type,total_share,cap_rese,undistr_porfit,surplus_rese,special_rese,money_cap,trad_asset,notes_receiv,accounts_receiv,oth_receiv,prepayment,div_receiv,int_receiv,inventories,amor_exp,nca_within_1y,sett_rsrv,loanto_oth_bank_fi,premium_receiv,reinsur_receiv,reinsur_res_receiv,pur_resale_fa,oth_cur_assets,total_cur_assets,fa_avail_for_sale,htm_invest,lt_eqt_invest,invest_real_estate,time_deposits,oth_assets,lt_rec,fix_assets,cip,const_materials,fixed_assets_disp,produc_bio_assets,oil_and_gas_assets,intan_assets,r_and_d,goodwill,lt_amor_exp,defer_tax_assets,decr_in_disbur,oth_nca,total_nca,cash_reser_cb,depos_in_oth_bfi,prec_metals,deriv_assets,rr_reinsur_une_prem,rr_reinsur_outstd_cla,rr_reinsur_lins_liab,rr_reinsur_lthins_liab,refund_depos,ph_pledge_loans,refund_cap_depos,indep_acct_assets,client_depos,client_prov,transac_seat_fee,invest_as_receiv,total_assets,st_borr,cb_borr,depos_ib_deposits,loan_oth_bank,trading_fl,notes_payable,acct_payable,adv_receipts,sold_for_repur_fa,comm_payable,payroll_payable,taxes_payable,int_payable,div_payable,oth_payable,acc_exp,deferred_inc,st_bonds_payable,payable_to_reinsurer,rsrv_insur_cont,acting_trading_sec,acting_uw_sec,non_cur_liab_due_1y,oth_cur_liab,total_cur_liab,bond_payable,lt_payable,specific_payables,estimated_liab,defer_tax_liab,defer_inc_non_cur_liab,oth_ncl,total_ncl,depos_oth_bfi,deriv_liab,depos,agency_bus_liab,oth_liab,prem_receiv_adva,depos_received,ph_invest,reser_une_prem,reser_outstd_claims,reser_lins_liab,reser_lthins_liab,indept_acc_liab,pledge_borr,indem_payable,policy_div_payable,total_liab,treasury_share,ordin_risk_reser,forex_differ,invest_loss_unconf,minority_int,total_hldr_eqy_exc_min_int,total_hldr_eqy_inc_min_int,total_liab_hldr_eqy,lt_payroll_payable,oth_comp_income,oth_eqt_tools,oth_eqt_tools_p_shr,lending_funds,acc_receivable,st_fin_payable,payables'
        )
    
    def get_cashflow(self, ts_code: str, period: str) -> pd.DataFrame:
        """获取现金流量表 - 完整财务数据"""
        return self.pro.cashflow(
            ts_code=ts_code,
            period=period,
            fields='ts_code,ann_date,f_ann_date,end_date,report_type,comp_type,net_profit,finan_exp,c_fr_sale_sg,recp_tax_rends,n_depos_incr_fi,n_incr_loans_cb,n_inc_borr_oth_fi,prem_fr_orig_contr,n_incr_insured_dep,n_reinsur_prem,n_incr_disp_tfa,ifc_cash_incr,n_incr_disp_faas,n_incr_loans_oth_bank,n_cap_incr_repur,c_fr_oth_operate_a,c_inf_fr_operate_a,c_paid_goods_s,c_paid_to_for_empl,c_paid_for_taxes,n_incr_clt_loan_adv,n_incr_dep_cbob,c_pay_claims_orig_inco,pay_handling_chrg,pay_comm_insur_plcy,oth_cash_pay_oper_act,st_cash_out_act,n_cashflow_act,oth_recp_ral_inv_act,c_disp_withdrwl_invest,c_recp_return_invest,n_recp_disp_fiolta,n_recp_disp_sobu,stot_inflows_inv_act,c_pay_acq_const_fiolta,c_paid_invest,n_disp_subs_oth_biz,oth_pay_ral_inv_act,n_incr_pledge_loan,stot_out_inv_act,n_cashflow_inv_act,c_recp_borrow,proc_issue_bonds,oth_cash_recp_ral_fnc_act,stot_cash_in_fnc_act,free_cashflow,c_prepay_amt_borr,c_pay_dist_dpcp_int_exp,incl_dvd_profit_paid_sc_ms,oth_cashpay_ral_fnc_act,stot_cashout_fnc_act,n_cash_flows_fnc_act,eff_fx_flu_cash,n_incr_cash_cash_equ,c_cash_equ_beg_period,c_cash_equ_end_period,c_recp_cap_contrib,incl_cash_rec_saims,uncon_invest_loss,prov_depr_assets,depr_fa_coga_dpba,amort_intang_assets,lt_amort_deferred_exp,decr_deferred_exp,incr_acc_exp,loss_disp_fiolta,loss_scr_fa,loss_fv_chg,invest_loss,decr_def_inc_tax_assets,incr_def_inc_tax_liab,decr_inventories,decr_oper_payable,incr_oper_payable,others,im_net_cashflow_oper_act,conv_debt_into_cap,conv_copbonds_due_within_1y,fa_fnc_leases,end_bal_cash,beg_bal_cash,end_bal_cash_equ,beg_bal_cash_equ,im_n_incr_cash_equ'
        )
    
    def get_fina_indicator(self, ts_code: str, period: str) -> pd.DataFrame:
        """获取财务指标数据 - TUshare Pro专业分析数据"""
        return self.pro.fina_indicator(
            ts_code=ts_code,
            period=period,
            fields='ts_code,ann_date,end_date,eps,dt_eps,total_revenue_ps,revenue_ps,capital_rese_ps,surplus_rese_ps,undist_profit_ps,extra_item,profit_dedt,gross_margin,current_ratio,quick_ratio,cash_ratio,invturn_days,arturn_days,inv_turn,ar_turn,ca_turn,fa_turn,assets_turn,op_income,valuechange_income,interst_income,daa,ebit,ebitda,fcff,fcfe,current_exint,noncurrent_exint,interestdebt,netdebt,tangible_asset,working_capital,networking_capital,invest_capital,retained_earnings,diluted2_eps,bps,ocfps,retainedps,cfps,ebit_ps,fcff_ps,fcfe_ps,netprofit_margin,grossprofit_margin,cogs_of_sales,expense_of_sales,profit_to_gr,saleexp_to_gr,adminexp_of_gr,finaexp_of_gr,impai_ttm,gc_of_gr,op_of_gr,ebit_of_gr,roe,roe_waa,roe_dt,roa,npta,roic,roe_yearly,roa_yearly,roe_avg,opincome_of_ebt,investincome_of_ebt,n_op_profit_of_ebt,tax_to_ebt,dtprofit_to_profit,salescash_to_or,ocf_to_or,ocf_to_opincome,capitalized_to_da,debt_to_assets,assets_to_eqt,dp_assets_to_eqt,ca_to_assets,nca_to_assets,tbassets_to_totalassets,int_to_talcap,eqt_to_talcapital,currentdebt_to_debt,longdeb_to_debt,ocf_to_shortdebt,debt_to_eqt,eqt_to_debt,eqt_to_interestdebt,tangibleasset_to_debt,tangasset_to_intdebt,tangibleasset_to_netdebt,ocf_to_debt,ocf_to_interestdebt,ocf_to_netdebt,ebit_to_interest,longdebt_to_workingcapital,ebitda_to_debt,turn_days,roa_yearly,roa_dp,fixed_assets,profit_prefin_exp,non_op_profit,op_to_ebt,nop_to_ebt,ocf_to_profit,cash_to_liqdebt,cash_to_liqdebt_withinterest,op_to_liqdebt,op_to_debt,roic_yearly,total_fa_trun,profit_to_op,q_opincome,q_investincome,q_dtprofit,q_eps,q_netprofit_margin,q_gsprofit_margin,q_exp_to_sales,q_profit_to_gr,q_saleexp_to_gr,q_adminexp_to_gr,q_finaexp_to_gr,q_impair_to_gr_ttm,q_gc_to_gr,q_op_to_gr,q_roe,q_dt_roe,q_npta,q_opincome_to_ebt,q_investincome_to_ebt,q_dtprofit_to_profit,q_salescash_to_or,q_ocf_to_sales,q_ocf_to_or,basic_eps_yoy,dt_eps_yoy,cfps_yoy,op_yoy,ebt_yoy,netprofit_yoy,dt_netprofit_yoy,ocf_yoy,roe_yoy,bps_yoy,assets_yoy,eqt_yoy,tr_yoy,or_yoy,q_gr_yoy,q_gr_qoq,q_sales_yoy,q_sales_qoq,q_op_yoy,q_op_qoq,q_profit_yoy,q_profit_qoq,q_netprofit_yoy,q_netprofit_qoq,equity_yoy,rd_exp,update_flag'
        )
    
    def get_dividend(self, ts_code: str) -> pd.DataFrame:
        """获取分红送股数据"""
        return self.pro.dividend(
            ts_code=ts_code,
            fields='ts_code,end_date,ann_date,div_proc,stk_div,stk_bo_rate,stk_co_rate,cash_div,cash_div_tax,record_date,ex_date,pay_date,div_listdate,imp_ann_date,base_date,base_share'
        )
    
    def get_forecast(self, ts_code: str, period: str) -> pd.DataFrame:
        """获取业绩预告数据"""
        return self.pro.forecast(
            ts_code=ts_code,
            period=period,
            fields='ts_code,ann_date,end_date,type,p_change_min,p_change_max,net_profit_min,net_profit_max,last_parent_net,first_ann_date,summary,change_reason'
        )
    
    def get_express(self, ts_code: str, period: str) -> pd.DataFrame:
        """获取业绩快报数据"""
        return self.pro.express(
            ts_code=ts_code,
            period=period,
            fields='ts_code,ann_date,end_date,revenue,operate_profit,total_profit,n_income,total_assets,total_hldr_eqy_exc_min_int,diluted_eps,diluted_roe,yoy_net_profit,bps,yoy_sales,yoy_op,yoy_tp,yoy_dedu_np,yoy_eps,yoy_roe,growth_assets,yoy_equity,growth_bps,or_last_year,op_last_year,tp_last_year,np_last_year,eps_last_year,open_net_assets,open_bps,perf_summary,is_audit,remark'
        )
    
    def get_top_list(self, trade_date: str) -> pd.DataFrame:
        """获取龙虎榜数据"""
        return self.pro.top_list(
            trade_date=trade_date,
            fields='trade_date,ts_code,name,close,pct_change,turnover_rate,amount,l_sell,l_buy,l_amount,net_amount,net_rate,amount_rate,float_values,reason'
        )
    
    def get_top_inst(self, trade_date: str) -> pd.DataFrame:
        """获取龙虎榜机构交易明细"""
        return self.pro.top_inst(
            trade_date=trade_date,
            fields='trade_date,ts_code,exalter,buy,buy_rate,sell,sell_rate,net_buy'
        )
    
    def get_block_trade(self, ts_code: str, start_date: str, end_date: str) -> pd.DataFrame:
        """获取大宗交易数据"""
        return self.pro.block_trade(
            ts_code=ts_code,
            start_date=start_date,
            end_date=end_date,
            fields='ts_code,trade_date,price,vol,amount,buyer,seller'
        )
    
    def get_stk_holdernumber(self, ts_code: str, end_date: str) -> pd.DataFrame:
        """获取股东人数数据"""
        return self.pro.stk_holdernumber(
            ts_code=ts_code,
            end_date=end_date,
            fields='ts_code,ann_date,end_date,holder_num'
        )
    
    def get_top10_holders(self, ts_code: str, period: str) -> pd.DataFrame:
        """获取前十大股东数据"""
        return self.pro.top10_holders(
            ts_code=ts_code,
            period=period,
            fields='ts_code,ann_date,end_date,holder_name,hold_amount,hold_ratio'
        )
    
    def get_top10_floatholders(self, ts_code: str, period: str) -> pd.DataFrame:
        """获取前十大流通股东数据"""
        return self.pro.top10_floatholders(
            ts_code=ts_code,
            period=period,
            fields='ts_code,ann_date,end_date,holder_name,hold_amount,hold_ratio'
        )
    
    def get_new_share(self, start_date: str, end_date: str) -> pd.DataFrame:
        """获取新股数据"""
        return self.pro.new_share(
            start_date=start_date,
            end_date=end_date,
            fields='ts_code,sub_code,name,ipo_date,issue_date,amount,market_amount,price,pe,limit_amount,funds,ballot'
        )
    
    def get_margin(self, trade_date: str) -> pd.DataFrame:
        """获取融资融券交易汇总数据"""
        return self.pro.margin(
            trade_date=trade_date,
            fields='trade_date,exchange_id,rzye,rqye,rzmre,rqmcl,rzche,rqchl,net_buy_amt,remain_amt'
        )
    
    def get_margin_detail(self, ts_code: str, trade_date: str) -> pd.DataFrame:
        """获取融资融券交易明细数据"""
        return self.pro.margin_detail(
            ts_code=ts_code,
            trade_date=trade_date,
            fields='trade_date,ts_code,rzye,rqye,rzmre,rqmcl,rzche,rqchl'
        )
    
    def get_repurchase(self, ann_date: str) -> pd.DataFrame:
        """获取股票回购数据"""
        return self.pro.repurchase(
            ann_date=ann_date,
            fields='ts_code,ann_date,end_date,proc,exp_date,vol,amount,high_limit,low_limit'
        )
    
    # 注意：concept 和 concept_detail 接口需要5000积分，已移除
    # 改用 AKshare 的概念股接口：
    # - ak.stock_board_concept_name_em() 获取概念板块名称
    # - ak.stock_board_concept_cons_em() 获取概念板块成份股
    
    def get_index_basic(self) -> pd.DataFrame:
        """获取指数基础信息"""
        return self.pro.index_basic(
            market='',
            fields='ts_code,name,fullname,market,publisher,index_type,category,base_date,base_point,list_date,weight_rule,desc,exp_date'
        )
    
    def get_index_daily(self, ts_code: str, start_date: str, end_date: str) -> pd.DataFrame:
        """获取指数日线行情"""
        return self.pro.index_daily(
            ts_code=ts_code,
            start_date=start_date,
            end_date=end_date,
            fields='ts_code,trade_date,close,open,high,low,pre_close,change,pct_chg,vol,amount'
        )
    
    def get_index_weight(self, index_code: str, trade_date: str) -> pd.DataFrame:
        """获取指数成份和权重"""
        return self.pro.index_weight(
            index_code=index_code,
            trade_date=trade_date,
            fields='index_code,con_code,trade_date,weight'
        )

#### 6.2.2 AKshare 配置 (实时数据优先)

# config/akshare_config.py
import akshare as ak

class AkshareConfig:
    def __init__(self):
        """AKshare无需token，直接使用"""
        pass
    
    def get_stock_zh_a_spot_em(self) -> pd.DataFrame:
        """获取A股实时行情数据 - 东方财富"""
        return ak.stock_zh_a_spot_em()
    
    def get_stock_zh_a_hist(self, symbol: str, period: str = "daily", start_date: str = "", end_date: str = "", adjust: str = "") -> pd.DataFrame:

            symbol=symbol,
            period=period,
            start_date=start_date,
            end_date=end_date,
            adjust=adjust
        )

#### 6.2.3 数据源接口映射配置
```python
# config/data_mapping.py
from typing import Dict, List, Callable
from enum import Enum

class DataCategory(Enum):
    """数据类别枚举"""
    BASIC_INFO = "basic_info"           # 基础信息
    REALTIME_QUOTE = "realtime_quote"   # 实时行情
    HISTORICAL_QUOTE = "historical_quote" # 历史行情
    FINANCIAL_DATA = "financial_data"   # 财务数据
    FUND_FLOW = "fund_flow"            # 资金流向
    MARKET_DATA = "market_data"        # 市场数据
    SPECIAL_EVENT = "special_event"    # 特殊事件
    MACRO_DATA = "macro_data"          # 宏观数据
    CROSS_MARKET = "cross_market"      # 跨市场数据
    NEWS_RESEARCH = "news_research"    # 新闻研报

class DataSourceMapping:
    """数据源接口映射配置"""
    
    def __init__(self):
        self.tushare_mapping = {
            DataCategory.BASIC_INFO: [
                'get_stock_basic',           # 股票基础信息
                'get_index_basic',           # 指数基础信息
                'get_concept',               # 概念分类
                'get_concept_detail',        # 概念成份股
            ],
            DataCategory.HISTORICAL_QUOTE: [
                'get_daily_data',            # 日线行情
                'get_index_daily',           # 指数日线
                'get_index_weight',          # 指数权重
            ],
            DataCategory.FINANCIAL_DATA: [
                'get_daily_basic',           # 每日基本面
                'get_income_statement',      # 利润表
                'get_balance_sheet',         # 资产负债表
                'get_cashflow',              # 现金流量表
                'get_fina_indicator',        # 财务指标
                'get_dividend',              # 分红送股
                'get_forecast',              # 业绩预告
                'get_express',               # 业绩快报
            ],
            DataCategory.FUND_FLOW: [
                'get_moneyflow',             # 个股资金流向
            ],
            DataCategory.SPECIAL_EVENT: [
                'get_top_list',              # 龙虎榜
                'get_top_inst',              # 龙虎榜机构
                'get_block_trade',           # 大宗交易
                'get_new_share',             # 新股数据
                'get_margin',                # 融资融券汇总
                'get_margin_detail',         # 融资融券明细
                'get_repurchase',            # 股票回购
                'get_stk_holdernumber',      # 股东人数
                'get_top10_holders',         # 前十大股东
                'get_top10_floatholders',    # 前十大流通股东
            ]
        }
        
        self.akshare_mapping = {
            DataCategory.REALTIME_QUOTE: [
                'get_stock_zh_a_spot_em',        # A股实时行情
                'get_stock_bid_ask_em',          # 五档行情
                'get_stock_zh_a_tick_tx',        # 分时数据
                'get_stock_individual_info_em',   # 个股信息
            ],
            DataCategory.HISTORICAL_QUOTE: [
                'get_stock_zh_a_hist',           # A股历史行情
                'get_index_zh_a_hist',           # 指数历史行情
            ],
            DataCategory.MARKET_DATA: [
                'get_stock_hot_rank_em',         # 热门股票排行
                'get_stock_hot_rank_detail_em',  # 热门股票详情
                'get_stock_hot_rank_latest_em',  # 最新热门股票
                'get_stock_hot_rank_wc',         # 热门股票(微财经)
                'get_stock_market_activity_legu', # 市场活跃度
                'get_stock_comment_em',          # 千股千评
                'get_stock_sector_spot',         # 板块行情
                'get_stock_sector_detail',       # 板块成份股
                'get_stock_board_concept_name_em', # 概念板块名称
                'get_stock_board_concept_cons_em', # 概念板块成份股
                'get_stock_board_industry_name_em', # 行业板块名称
                'get_stock_board_industry_cons_em', # 行业板块成份股
            ],
            DataCategory.FUND_FLOW: [
                'get_stock_individual_fund_flow',     # 个股资金流向
                'get_stock_individual_fund_flow_rank', # 个股资金流向排名
                'get_stock_market_fund_flow',          # 大盘资金流向
                'get_stock_sector_fund_flow_rank',     # 行业资金流向
            ],
            DataCategory.SPECIAL_EVENT: [
                'get_stock_lhb_detail_em',       # 龙虎榜详情
                'get_stock_lhb_ggtj_em',         # 龙虎榜个股统计
                'get_stock_lhb_jgzz_em',         # 龙虎榜机构追踪
                'get_stock_dzjy_mrmx',           # 大宗交易明细
                'get_stock_dzjy_mrtj',           # 大宗交易统计
                'get_stock_ipo_info',            # 新股申购信息
                'get_stock_zh_ipo_sub_new',      # 新股申购查询
                'get_stock_margin_underlying_info_szse', # 融资融券标的
                'get_stock_margin_detail_szse',  # 融资融券明细
                'get_stock_repurchase_em',       # 股票回购
            ],
            DataCategory.FINANCIAL_DATA: [
                'get_stock_financial_abstract_ths',  # 财务摘要
                'get_stock_financial_debt_ths',      # 资产负债表
                'get_stock_financial_benefit_ths',   # 利润表
                'get_stock_financial_cash_ths',      # 现金流量表
            ],
            DataCategory.NEWS_RESEARCH: [
                'get_stock_news_em',             # 个股新闻
                'get_stock_notice_report',       # 个股公告
                'get_stock_research_report_em',  # 研究报告
            ],
            DataCategory.MACRO_DATA: [
                'get_macro_china_gdp',           # 中国GDP
                'get_macro_china_cpi',           # 中国CPI
                'get_macro_china_ppi',           # 中国PPI
                'get_macro_china_pmi',           # 中国PMI
                'get_macro_china_money_supply',  # 货币供应量
            ],
            DataCategory.CROSS_MARKET: [
                'get_stock_us_spot_sina',        # 美股实时行情
                'get_stock_us_hist_sina',        # 美股历史行情
                'get_stock_hk_spot_em',          # 港股实时行情
                'get_stock_hk_hist_em',          # 港股历史行情
                'get_index_investing_global',    # 全球股指
            ]
        }
    
    def get_primary_source(self, data_category: DataCategory) -> str:
        """根据数据类别获取主数据源"""
        if data_category in [DataCategory.REALTIME_QUOTE, DataCategory.MARKET_DATA, 
                           DataCategory.NEWS_RESEARCH, DataCategory.CROSS_MARKET]:
            return "akshare"
        else:
            return "tushare"
    
    def get_fallback_source(self, data_category: DataCategory) -> str:
        """根据数据类别获取备用数据源"""
        primary = self.get_primary_source(data_category)
        return "tushare" if primary == "akshare" else "akshare"
    
    def get_available_methods(self, data_category: DataCategory, source: str) -> List[str]:
        """获取指定数据源的可用方法列表"""
        if source == "tushare":
            return self.tushare_mapping.get(data_category, [])
        elif source == "akshare":
            return self.akshare_mapping.get(data_category, [])
        else:
            return []

#### 6.2.4 数据质量监控配置
```python
# config/data_quality_config.py
from typing import Dict, List, Any
from dataclasses import dataclass
from datetime import datetime, timedelta

@dataclass
class DataQualityRule:
    """数据质量规则"""
    field_name: str
    rule_type: str  # 'not_null', 'range', 'format', 'unique'
    rule_params: Dict[str, Any]
    severity: str  # 'error', 'warning', 'info'
    description: str

class DataQualityConfig:
    """数据质量监控配置"""
    
    def __init__(self):
        self.quality_rules = {
            'stock_basic': [
                DataQualityRule('ts_code', 'not_null', {}, 'error', '股票代码不能为空'),
                DataQualityRule('ts_code', 'format', {'pattern': r'^\d{6}\.(SH|SZ|BJ)$'}, 'error', '股票代码格式错误'),
                DataQualityRule('name', 'not_null', {}, 'error', '股票名称不能为空'),
                DataQualityRule('list_date', 'format', {'pattern': r'^\d{8}$'}, 'warning', '上市日期格式错误'),
            ],
            'daily_data': [
                DataQualityRule('ts_code', 'not_null', {}, 'error', '股票代码不能为空'),
                DataQualityRule('trade_date', 'not_null', {}, 'error', '交易日期不能为空'),
                DataQualityRule('open', 'range', {'min': 0, 'max': 10000}, 'warning', '开盘价异常'),
                DataQualityRule('high', 'range', {'min': 0, 'max': 10000}, 'warning', '最高价异常'),
                DataQualityRule('low', 'range', {'min': 0, 'max': 10000}, 'warning', '最低价异常'),
                DataQualityRule('close', 'range', {'min': 0, 'max': 10000}, 'warning', '收盘价异常'),
                DataQualityRule('vol', 'range', {'min': 0}, 'warning', '成交量不能为负'),
                DataQualityRule('amount', 'range', {'min': 0}, 'warning', '成交额不能为负'),
            ],
            'financial_data': [
                DataQualityRule('ts_code', 'not_null', {}, 'error', '股票代码不能为空'),
                DataQualityRule('end_date', 'not_null', {}, 'error', '报告期不能为空'),
                DataQualityRule('ann_date', 'not_null', {}, 'error', '公告日期不能为空'),
            ],
            'fund_flow': [
                DataQualityRule('ts_code', 'not_null', {}, 'error', '股票代码不能为空'),
                DataQualityRule('trade_date', 'not_null', {}, 'error', '交易日期不能为空'),
            ]
        }
        
        self.data_freshness_rules = {
            'realtime_quote': timedelta(minutes=5),    # 实时行情5分钟内
            'daily_data': timedelta(hours=18),         # 日线数据18小时内
            'financial_data': timedelta(days=90),      # 财务数据90天内
            'fund_flow': timedelta(hours=24),          # 资金流向24小时内
            'market_data': timedelta(hours=6),         # 市场数据6小时内
        }
        
        self.completeness_thresholds = {
            'stock_basic': 0.99,      # 股票基础信息完整度99%
            'daily_data': 0.95,       # 日线数据完整度95%
            'financial_data': 0.90,   # 财务数据完整度90%
            'fund_flow': 0.85,        # 资金流向完整度85%
        }
    
    def get_quality_rules(self, data_type: str) -> List[DataQualityRule]:
        """获取指定数据类型的质量规则"""
        return self.quality_rules.get(data_type, [])
    
    def get_freshness_threshold(self, data_type: str) -> timedelta:
        """获取数据新鲜度阈值"""
        return self.data_freshness_rules.get(data_type, timedelta(days=1))
    
    def get_completeness_threshold(self, data_type: str) -> float:
        """获取数据完整度阈值"""
        return self.completeness_thresholds.get(data_type, 0.80)

#### 6.2.5 数据缓存策略配置
```python
# config/cache_strategy_config.py
from typing import Dict, Any
from dataclasses import dataclass
from datetime import timedelta

@dataclass
class CacheStrategy:
    """缓存策略配置"""
    ttl: timedelta                    # 缓存生存时间
    refresh_interval: timedelta       # 刷新间隔
    max_size: int                    # 最大缓存大小
    compression: bool                # 是否压缩
    persistence: bool                # 是否持久化
    priority: int                    # 缓存优先级 (1-10)

class CacheStrategyConfig:
    """缓存策略配置管理"""
    
    def __init__(self):
        self.cache_strategies = {
            # 实时数据 - 短期缓存，高频刷新
            'realtime_quote': CacheStrategy(
                ttl=timedelta(minutes=1),
                refresh_interval=timedelta(seconds=30),
                max_size=10000,
                compression=False,
                persistence=False,
                priority=10
            ),
            
            # 日线数据 - 中期缓存，日更新
            'daily_data': CacheStrategy(
                ttl=timedelta(hours=18),
                refresh_interval=timedelta(hours=16),
                max_size=50000,
                compression=True,
                persistence=True,
                priority=8
            ),
            
            # 财务数据 - 长期缓存，季度更新
            'financial_data': CacheStrategy(
                ttl=timedelta(days=90),
                refresh_interval=timedelta(days=7),
                max_size=20000,
                compression=True,
                persistence=True,
                priority=6
            ),
            
            # 基础信息 - 长期缓存，低频更新
            'basic_info': CacheStrategy(
                ttl=timedelta(days=30),
                refresh_interval=timedelta(days=1),
                max_size=5000,
                compression=True,
                persistence=True,
                priority=5
            ),
            
            # 资金流向 - 短期缓存，日更新
            'fund_flow': CacheStrategy(
                ttl=timedelta(hours=6),
                refresh_interval=timedelta(hours=4),
                max_size=15000,
                compression=True,
                persistence=True,
                priority=7
            ),
            
            # 市场数据 - 中期缓存，小时更新
            'market_data': CacheStrategy(
                ttl=timedelta(hours=2),
                refresh_interval=timedelta(hours=1),
                max_size=8000,
                compression=False,
                persistence=False,
                priority=9
            ),
            
            # 新闻研报 - 中期缓存，日更新
            'news_research': CacheStrategy(
                ttl=timedelta(hours=12),
                refresh_interval=timedelta(hours=6),
                max_size=3000,
                compression=True,
                persistence=True,
                priority=4
            ),
            
            # 宏观数据 - 长期缓存，月更新
            'macro_data': CacheStrategy(
                ttl=timedelta(days=30),
                refresh_interval=timedelta(days=7),
                max_size=1000,
                compression=True,
                persistence=True,
                priority=3
            ),
            
            # 跨市场数据 - 短期缓存，小时更新
            'cross_market': CacheStrategy(
                ttl=timedelta(hours=4),
                refresh_interval=timedelta(hours=2),
                max_size=5000,
                compression=True,
                persistence=True,
                priority=6
            )
        }
    
    def get_cache_strategy(self, data_type: str) -> CacheStrategy:
        """获取指定数据类型的缓存策略"""
        return self.cache_strategies.get(data_type, CacheStrategy(
            ttl=timedelta(hours=1),
            refresh_interval=timedelta(minutes=30),
            max_size=1000,
            compression=True,
            persistence=False,
            priority=5
        ))
    
    def get_all_strategies(self) -> Dict[str, CacheStrategy]:
        """获取所有缓存策略"""
        ### 6.3 数据处理层设计

#### 6.3.1 数据标准化处理
```python
# services/data_processor.py
import pandas as pd
import numpy as np
from typing import Dict, List, Any, Optional, Union
from datetime import datetime, timedelta
import logging
from dataclasses import dataclass

@dataclass
class DataSchema:
    """数据模式定义"""
    table_name: str
    required_fields: List[str]
    optional_fields: List[str]
    field_types: Dict[str, str]
    field_mappings: Dict[str, str]  # 源字段到目标字段的映射

class DataProcessor:
    """数据处理器 - 负责数据清洗、转换和标准化"""
    
    def __init__(self):
        self.logger = logging.getLogger(__name__)
        self.schemas = self._init_schemas()
    
    def _init_schemas(self) -> Dict[str, DataSchema]:
        """初始化数据模式"""
        return {
            'stock_basic': DataSchema(
                table_name='stocks',
                required_fields=['ts_code', 'symbol', 'name', 'area', 'industry', 'market', 'list_date'],
                optional_fields=['fullname', 'enname', 'cnspell', 'exchange', 'curr_type', 'list_status', 'delist_date', 'is_hs'],
                field_types={
                    'ts_code': 'str', 'symbol': 'str', 'name': 'str', 'area': 'str',
                    'industry': 'str', 'market': 'str', 'list_date': 'date',
                    'fullname': 'str', 'enname': 'str', 'cnspell': 'str',
                    'exchange': 'str', 'curr_type': 'str', 'list_status': 'str',
                    'delist_date': 'date', 'is_hs': 'str'
                },
                field_mappings={
                    'ts_code': 'ts_code', 'symbol': 'symbol', 'name': 'name',
                    'area': 'area', 'industry': 'industry', 'market': 'market',
                    'list_date': 'list_date'
                }
            ),
            'daily_data': DataSchema(
                table_name='stock_daily',
                required_fields=['ts_code', 'trade_date', 'open', 'high', 'low', 'close', 'pre_close', 'change', 'pct_chg', 'vol', 'amount'],
                optional_fields=['turnover_rate', 'volume_ratio', 'pe', 'pb'],
                field_types={
                    'ts_code': 'str', 'trade_date': 'date', 'open': 'float',
                    'high': 'float', 'low': 'float', 'close': 'float',
                    'pre_close': 'float', 'change': 'float', 'pct_chg': 'float',
                    'vol': 'float', 'amount': 'float', 'turnover_rate': 'float',
                    'volume_ratio': 'float', 'pe': 'float', 'pb': 'float'
                },
                field_mappings={
                    'ts_code': 'ts_code', 'trade_date': 'trade_date',
                    'open': 'open', 'high': 'high', 'low': 'low', 'close': 'close',
                    'pre_close': 'pre_close', 'change': 'change', 'pct_chg': 'pct_chg',
                    'vol': 'vol', 'amount': 'amount'
                }
            ),
            'financial_data': DataSchema(
                table_name='financial_statements',
                required_fields=['ts_code', 'ann_date', 'f_ann_date', 'end_date', 'report_type'],
                optional_fields=['comp_type', 'basic_eps', 'diluted_eps'],
                field_types={
                    'ts_code': 'str', 'ann_date': 'date', 'f_ann_date': 'date',
                    'end_date': 'date', 'report_type': 'str', 'comp_type': 'str',
                    'basic_eps': 'float', 'diluted_eps': 'float'
                },
                field_mappings={
                    'ts_code': 'ts_code', 'ann_date': 'ann_date',
                    'f_ann_date': 'f_ann_date', 'end_date': 'end_date',
                    'report_type': 'report_type'
                }
            )
        }
    
    def process_tushare_data(self, data: pd.DataFrame, data_type: str, source: str = 'tushare') -> pd.DataFrame:
        """处理Tushare数据"""
        if data.empty:
            self.logger.warning(f"Empty data received for {data_type}")
            return data
        
        try:
            # 获取数据模式
            schema = self.schemas.get(data_type)
            if not schema:
                self.logger.warning(f"No schema found for {data_type}")
                return data
            
            # 数据清洗
            processed_data = self._clean_data(data, schema)
            
            # 字段映射
            processed_data = self._map_fields(processed_data, schema)
            
            # 类型转换
            processed_data = self._convert_types(processed_data, schema)
            
            # 数据验证
            processed_data = self._validate_data(processed_data, schema)
            
            # 添加元数据
            processed_data = self._add_metadata(processed_data, source)
            
            return processed_data
            
        except Exception as e:
            self.logger.error(f"Error processing {data_type} data: {str(e)}")
            return pd.DataFrame()
    
    def process_akshare_data(self, data: pd.DataFrame, data_type: str, source: str = 'akshare') -> pd.DataFrame:
        """处理AKshare数据"""
        if data.empty:
            self.logger.warning(f"Empty data received for {data_type}")
            return data
        
        try:
            # AKshare数据通常需要更多的清洗和转换
            # 统一字段名称（AKshare字段名通常是中文）
            data = self._normalize_akshare_columns(data, data_type)
            
            # 后续处理与Tushare相同
            return self.process_tushare_data(data, data_type, source)
            
        except Exception as e:
            self.logger.error(f"Error processing AKshare {data_type} data: {str(e)}")
            return pd.DataFrame()
    
    def _clean_data(self, data: pd.DataFrame, schema: DataSchema) -> pd.DataFrame:
        """数据清洗"""
        # 删除重复行
        data = data.drop_duplicates()
        
        # 处理缺失值
        for field in schema.required_fields:
            if field in data.columns:
                # 必填字段不能为空
                data = data.dropna(subset=[field])
        
        # 处理异常值
        for field, field_type in schema.field_types.items():
            if field in data.columns and field_type == 'float':
                # 移除极端异常值
                Q1 = data[field].quantile(0.01)
                Q3 = data[field].quantile(0.99)
                data = data[(data[field] >= Q1) & (data[field] <= Q3)]
        
        return data
    
    def _map_fields(self, data: pd.DataFrame, schema: DataSchema) -> pd.DataFrame:
        """字段映射"""
        mapped_data = pd.DataFrame()
        
        for source_field, target_field in schema.field_mappings.items():
            if source_field in data.columns:
                mapped_data[target_field] = data[source_field]
        
        return mapped_data
    
    def _convert_types(self, data: pd.DataFrame, schema: DataSchema) -> pd.DataFrame:
        """类型转换"""
        for field, field_type in schema.field_types.items():
            if field in data.columns:
                try:
                    if field_type == 'date':
                        data[field] = pd.to_datetime(data[field], format='%Y%m%d', errors='coerce')
                    elif field_type == 'float':
                        data[field] = pd.to_numeric(data[field], errors='coerce')
                    elif field_type == 'str':
                        data[field] = data[field].astype(str)
                except Exception as e:
                    self.logger.warning(f"Type conversion failed for {field}: {str(e)}")
        
        return data
    
    def _validate_data(self, data: pd.DataFrame, schema: DataSchema) -> pd.DataFrame:
        """数据验证"""
        # 检查必填字段
        missing_required = [field for field in schema.required_fields if field not in data.columns]
        if missing_required:
            self.logger.warning(f"Missing required fields: {missing_required}")
        
        # 检查数据完整性
        total_rows = len(data)
        if total_rows == 0:
            self.logger.warning("No valid data after processing")
            return data
        
        # 记录数据质量统计
        null_counts = data.isnull().sum()
        for field, null_count in null_counts.items():
            if null_count > 0:
                null_rate = null_count / total_rows
                if null_rate > 0.1:  # 超过10%的缺失率
                    self.logger.warning(f"High null rate for {field}: {null_rate:.2%}")
        
        return data
    
    def _add_metadata(self, data: pd.DataFrame, source: str) -> pd.DataFrame:
        """添加元数据"""
        data['data_source'] = source
        data['created_at'] = datetime.now()
        data['updated_at'] = datetime.now()
        
        return data
    
    def _normalize_akshare_columns(self, data: pd.DataFrame, data_type: str) -> pd.DataFrame:
        """标准化AKshare列名"""
        column_mappings = {
            'realtime_quote': {
                '代码': 'ts_code', '名称': 'name', '最新价': 'close',
                '涨跌幅': 'pct_chg', '涨跌额': 'change', '成交量': 'vol',
                '成交额': 'amount', '振幅': 'amplitude', '最高': 'high',
                '最低': 'low', '今开': 'open', '昨收': 'pre_close'
            },
            'fund_flow': {
                '代码': 'ts_code', '名称': 'name', '最新价': 'close',
                '涨跌幅': 'pct_chg', '主力净流入-净额': 'main_net_inflow',
                '主力净流入-净占比': 'main_net_inflow_rate',
                '超大单净流入-净额': 'super_large_net_inflow',
                '超大单净流入-净占比': 'super_large_net_inflow_rate',
                '大单净流入-净额': 'large_net_inflow',
                '大单净流入-净占比': 'large_net_inflow_rate'
            }
        }
        
        mapping = column_mappings.get(data_type, {})
        if mapping:
            data = data.rename(columns=mapping)
        
        return data

#### 6.3.2 技术指标计算引擎
```python
# services/technical_indicators.py
import pandas as pd
import numpy as np
import talib
from typing import Dict, List, Any, Optional, Tuple
from dataclasses import dataclass

@dataclass
class IndicatorConfig:
    """技术指标配置"""
    name: str
    params: Dict[str, Any]
    description: str
    category: str  # 'trend', 'momentum', 'volume', 'volatility'

class TechnicalIndicatorEngine:
    """技术指标计算引擎"""
    
    def __init__(self):
        self.indicators_config = self._init_indicators_config()
    
    def _init_indicators_config(self) -> Dict[str, IndicatorConfig]:
        """初始化技术指标配置"""
        return {
            # 趋势指标
            'SMA': IndicatorConfig('SMA', {'timeperiod': 20}, '简单移动平均线', 'trend'),
            'EMA': IndicatorConfig('EMA', {'timeperiod': 20}, '指数移动平均线', 'trend'),
            'MACD': IndicatorConfig('MACD', {'fastperiod': 12, 'slowperiod': 26, 'signalperiod': 9}, 'MACD', 'trend'),
            'BOLL': IndicatorConfig('BOLL', {'timeperiod': 20, 'nbdevup': 2, 'nbdevdn': 2}, '布林带', 'trend'),
            
            # 动量指标
            'RSI': IndicatorConfig('RSI', {'timeperiod': 14}, '相对强弱指数', 'momentum'),
            'KDJ': IndicatorConfig('KDJ', {'fastk_period': 9, 'slowk_period': 3, 'slowd_period': 3}, 'KDJ随机指标', 'momentum'),
            'CCI': IndicatorConfig('CCI', {'timeperiod': 14}, '顺势指标', 'momentum'),
            'WR': IndicatorConfig('WR', {'timeperiod': 14}, '威廉指标', 'momentum'),
            
            # 成交量指标
            'OBV': IndicatorConfig('OBV', {}, '能量潮', 'volume'),
            'AD': IndicatorConfig('AD', {}, '累积/派发线', 'volume'),
            'ADOSC': IndicatorConfig('ADOSC', {'fastperiod': 3, 'slowperiod': 10}, 'A/D振荡器', 'volume'),
            
            # 波动率指标
            'ATR': IndicatorConfig('ATR', {'timeperiod': 14}, '平均真实波幅', 'volatility'),
            'NATR': IndicatorConfig('NATR', {'timeperiod': 14}, '标准化平均真实波幅', 'volatility'),
            
            # 九转指标
            'TD_SEQUENTIAL': IndicatorConfig('TD_SEQUENTIAL', {'setup_count': 9, 'countdown_count': 13}, 'TD序列', 'custom'),
        }
    
    def calculate_all_indicators(self, data: pd.DataFrame) -> pd.DataFrame:
        """计算所有技术指标"""
        if data.empty or len(data) < 30:  # 至少需要30个数据点
            return pd.DataFrame()
        
        result = data.copy()
        
        # 确保数据按日期排序
        result = result.sort_values('trade_date')
        
        # 提取OHLCV数据
        high = result['high'].values
        low = result['low'].values
        close = result['close'].values
        open_price = result['open'].values
        volume = result['vol'].values
        
        try:
            # 计算趋势指标
            result = self._calculate_trend_indicators(result, high, low, close, open_price)
            
            # 计算动量指标
            result = self._calculate_momentum_indicators(result, high, low, close)
            
            # 计算成交量指标
            result = self._calculate_volume_indicators(result, high, low, close, volume)
            
            # 计算波动率指标
            result = self._calculate_volatility_indicators(result, high, low, close)
            
            # 计算自定义指标
            result = self._calculate_custom_indicators(result, high, low, close, open_price)
            
        except Exception as e:
            print(f"Error calculating indicators: {str(e)}")
            return data
        
        return result
    
    def _calculate_trend_indicators(self, data: pd.DataFrame, high: np.array, low: np.array, close: np.array, open_price: np.array) -> pd.DataFrame:
        """计算趋势指标"""
        # 移动平均线
        data['sma_5'] = talib.SMA(close, timeperiod=5)
        data['sma_10'] = talib.SMA(close, timeperiod=10)
        data['sma_20'] = talib.SMA(close, timeperiod=20)
        data['sma_60'] = talib.SMA(close, timeperiod=60)
        
        data['ema_5'] = talib.EMA(close, timeperiod=5)
        data['ema_10'] = talib.EMA(close, timeperiod=10)
        data['ema_20'] = talib.EMA(close, timeperiod=20)
        data['ema_60'] = talib.EMA(close, timeperiod=60)
        
        # MACD
        macd, macdsignal, macdhist = talib.MACD(close, fastperiod=12, slowperiod=26, signalperiod=9)
        data['macd'] = macd
        data['macd_signal'] = macdsignal
        data['macd_hist'] = macdhist
        
        # 布林带
        upper, middle, lower = talib.BBANDS(close, timeperiod=20, nbdevup=2, nbdevdn=2, matype=0)
        data['boll_upper'] = upper
        data['boll_middle'] = middle
        data['boll_lower'] = lower
        data['boll_width'] = (upper - lower) / middle
        data['boll_position'] = (close - lower) / (upper - lower)
        
        return data
    
    def _calculate_momentum_indicators(self, data: pd.DataFrame, high: np.array, low: np.array, close: np.array) -> pd.DataFrame:
        """计算动量指标"""
        # RSI
        data['rsi_6'] = talib.RSI(close, timeperiod=6)
        data['rsi_14'] = talib.RSI(close, timeperiod=14)
        data['rsi_24'] = talib.RSI(close, timeperiod=24)
        
        # KDJ
        slowk, slowd = talib.STOCH(high, low, close, fastk_period=9, slowk_period=3, slowk_matype=0, slowd_period=3, slowd_matype=0)
        data['kdj_k'] = slowk
        data['kdj_d'] = slowd
        data['kdj_j'] = 3 * slowk - 2 * slowd
        
        # CCI
        data['cci'] = talib.CCI(high, low, close, timeperiod=14)
        
        # 威廉指标
        data['wr'] = talib.WILLR(high, low, close, timeperiod=14)
        
        return data
    
    def _calculate_volume_indicators(self, data: pd.DataFrame, high: np.array, low: np.array, close: np.array, volume: np.array) -> pd.DataFrame:
        """计算成交量指标"""
        # OBV
        data['obv'] = talib.OBV(close, volume)
        
        # A/D线
        data['ad'] = talib.AD(high, low, close, volume)
        
        # A/D振荡器
        data['adosc'] = talib.ADOSC(high, low, close, volume, fastperiod=3, slowperiod=10)
        
        # 成交量移动平均
        data['vol_ma_5'] = talib.SMA(volume, timeperiod=5)
        data['vol_ma_10'] = talib.SMA(volume, timeperiod=10)
        data['vol_ma_20'] = talib.SMA(volume, timeperiod=20)
        
        # 量比
        data['volume_ratio'] = volume / data['vol_ma_5']
        
        return data
    
    def _calculate_volatility_indicators(self, data: pd.DataFrame, high: np.array, low: np.array, close: np.array) -> pd.DataFrame:
        """计算波动率指标"""
        # ATR
        data['atr'] = talib.ATR(high, low, close, timeperiod=14)
        data['natr'] = talib.NATR(high, low, close, timeperiod=14)
        
        # 历史波动率
        returns = np.log(close[1:] / close[:-1])
        data['volatility_20'] = pd.Series(returns).rolling(window=20).std() * np.sqrt(252)
        
        return data
    
    def _calculate_custom_indicators(self, data: pd.DataFrame, high: np.array, low: np.array, close: np.array, open_price: np.array) -> pd.DataFrame:
        """计算自定义指标"""
        # TD序列（九转指标）
        data = self._calculate_td_sequential(data, close)
        
        # 支撑阻力位
        data = self._calculate_support_resistance(data, high, low, close)
        
        return data
    
    def _calculate_td_sequential(self, data: pd.DataFrame, close: np.array) -> pd.DataFrame:
        """计算TD序列（九转指标）"""
        n = len(close)
        setup_buy = np.zeros(n)
        setup_sell = np.zeros(n)
        countdown_buy = np.zeros(n)
        countdown_sell = np.zeros(n)
        
        # Setup阶段
        buy_setup_count = 0
        sell_setup_count = 0
        
        for i in range(4, n):
            # 买入Setup：当前收盘价低于4个交易日前的收盘价
            if close[i] < close[i-4]:
                buy_setup_count += 1
                sell_setup_count = 0
            # 卖出Setup：当前收盘价高于4个交易日前的收盘价
            elif close[i] > close[i-4]:
                sell_setup_count += 1
                buy_setup_count = 0
            else:
                buy_setup_count = 0
                sell_setup_count = 0
            
            setup_buy[i] = buy_setup_count if buy_setup_count <= 9 else 0
            setup_sell[i] = sell_setup_count if sell_setup_count <= 9 else 0
            
            # 重置计数器
            if buy_setup_count > 9:
                buy_setup_count = 0
            if sell_setup_count > 9:
                sell_setup_count = 0
        
        data['td_setup_buy'] = setup_buy
        data['td_setup_sell'] = setup_sell
        data['td_countdown_buy'] = countdown_buy
        data['td_countdown_sell'] = countdown_sell
        
        # 标记九转信号
        data['td_buy_signal'] = (data['td_setup_buy'] == 9).astype(int)
        data['td_sell_signal'] = (data['td_setup_sell'] == 9).astype(int)
        
        return data
    
    def _calculate_support_resistance(self, data: pd.DataFrame, high: np.array, low: np.array, close: np.array) -> pd.DataFrame:
        """计算支撑阻力位"""
        n = len(close)
        support = np.zeros(n)
        resistance = np.zeros(n)
        
        window = 20  # 计算窗口
        
        for i in range(window, n):
            recent_high = np.max(high[i-window:i])
            recent_low = np.min(low[i-window:i])
            
            # 简单的支撑阻力计算
            resistance[i] = recent_high
            support[i] = recent_low
        
        data['support'] = support
        data['resistance'] = resistance
        
        return data
    
    def get_indicator_signals(self, data: pd.DataFrame) -> Dict[str, Any]:
        """获取技术指标信号"""
        if data.empty:
            return {}
        
        latest = data.iloc[-1]
        signals = {}
        
        # MACD信号
        if not pd.isna(latest['macd']) and not pd.isna(latest['macd_signal']):
            signals['macd_signal'] = 'buy' if latest['macd'] > latest['macd_signal'] else 'sell'
        
        # RSI信号
        if not pd.isna(latest['rsi_14']):
            if latest['rsi_14'] > 70:
                signals['rsi_signal'] = 'overbought'
            elif latest['rsi_14'] < 30:
                signals['rsi_signal'] = 'oversold'
            else:
                signals['rsi_signal'] = 'neutral'
        
        # KDJ信号
        if not pd.isna(latest['kdj_k']) and not pd.isna(latest['kdj_d']):
            signals['kdj_signal'] = 'buy' if latest['kdj_k'] > latest['kdj_d'] else 'sell'
        
        # 布林带信号
        if not pd.isna(latest['boll_position']):
            if latest['boll_position'] > 0.8:
                signals['boll_signal'] = 'overbought'
            elif latest['boll_position'] < 0.2:
                signals['boll_signal'] = 'oversold'
            else:
                signals['boll_signal'] = 'neutral'
        
        # TD序列信号
        if latest['td_buy_signal'] == 1:
            signals['td_signal'] = 'buy'
        elif latest['td_sell_signal'] == 1:
            signals['td_signal'] = 'sell'
        else:
            signals['td_signal'] = 'neutral'
        
        return signals

#### 6.3.3 九转选股算法
```python
# services/nine_turn_selector.py
import pandas as pd
import numpy as np
from typing import Dict, List, Any, Optional, Tuple
from datetime import datetime, timedelta
from dataclasses import dataclass
import logging

@dataclass
class NineTurnSignal:
    """九转信号数据结构"""
    ts_code: str
    name: str
    signal_type: str  # 'buy' or 'sell'
    signal_date: str
    setup_count: int
    countdown_count: int
    signal_strength: float  # 信号强度 0-1
    price: float
    volume: float
    market_cap: float
    additional_filters: Dict[str, Any]

class NineTurnSelector:
    """九转选股算法"""
    
    def __init__(self):
        self.logger = logging.getLogger(__name__)
        self.min_market_cap = 50  # 最小市值（亿元）
        self.min_volume_ratio = 1.2  # 最小量比
        self.max_price = 100  # 最高价格
        self.min_price = 2  # 最低价格
    
    def scan_nine_turn_signals(self, stock_data: Dict[str, pd.DataFrame], 
                              market_data: pd.DataFrame) -> List[NineTurnSignal]:
        """扫描九转信号"""
        signals = []
        
        for ts_code, data in stock_data.items():
            if data.empty or len(data) < 30:
                continue
            
            try:
                # 计算九转指标
                data_with_td = self._calculate_td_sequential(data)
                
                # 检查最新信号
                latest_signals = self._check_latest_signals(data_with_td, ts_code)
                
                # 应用过滤条件
                filtered_signals = self._apply_filters(latest_signals, data_with_td, market_data)
                
                signals.extend(filtered_signals)
                
            except Exception as e:
                self.logger.error(f"Error processing {ts_code}: {str(e)}")
                continue
        
        # 按信号强度排序
        signals.sort(key=lambda x: x.signal_strength, reverse=True)
        
        return signals
    
    def _calculate_td_sequential(self, data: pd.DataFrame) -> pd.DataFrame:
        """计算TD序列"""
        data = data.copy().sort_values('trade_date')
        close = data['close'].values
        n = len(close)
        
        # 初始化数组
        setup_buy = np.zeros(n)
        setup_sell = np.zeros(n)
        countdown_buy = np.zeros(n)
        countdown_sell = np.zeros(n)
        
        # Setup阶段计算
        buy_setup_count = 0
        sell_setup_count = 0
        buy_setup_start = -1
        sell_setup_start = -1
        
        for i in range(4, n):
            # 买入Setup
            if close[i] < close[i-4]:
                if buy_setup_count == 0:
                    buy_setup_start = i
                buy_setup_count += 1
                sell_setup_count = 0
                sell_setup_start = -1
            # 卖出Setup
            elif close[i] > close[i-4]:
                if sell_setup_count == 0:
                    sell_setup_start = i
                sell_setup_count += 1
                buy_setup_count = 0
                buy_setup_start = -1
            else:
                buy_setup_count = 0
                sell_setup_count = 0
                buy_setup_start = -1
                sell_setup_start = -1
            
            # 记录Setup计数
            if buy_setup_count > 0 and buy_setup_count <= 9:
                setup_buy[i] = buy_setup_count
            if sell_setup_count > 0 and sell_setup_count <= 9:
                setup_sell[i] = sell_setup_count
            
            # Setup完成后开始Countdown
            if buy_setup_count == 9:
                # 买入Setup完成，开始买入Countdown
                countdown_buy = self._calculate_countdown(data, buy_setup_start, i, 'buy')
                buy_setup_count = 0
                buy_setup_start = -1
            
            if sell_setup_count == 9:
                # 卖出Setup完成，开始卖出Countdown
                countdown_sell = self._calculate_countdown(data, sell_setup_start, i, 'sell')
                sell_setup_count = 0
                sell_setup_start = -1
        
        data['td_setup_buy'] = setup_buy
        data['td_setup_sell'] = setup_sell
        data['td_countdown_buy'] = countdown_buy
        data['td_countdown_sell'] = countdown_sell
        
        return data
    
    def _calculate_countdown(self, data: pd.DataFrame, setup_start: int, setup_end: int, signal_type: str) -> np.array:
        """计算Countdown阶段"""
        n = len(data)
        countdown = np.zeros(n)
        
        if setup_start < 0 or setup_end < 0:
            return countdown
        
        close = data['close'].values
        low = data['low'].values
        high = data['high'].values
        
        # 获取Setup阶段的参考价格
        if signal_type == 'buy':
            # 买入Countdown：收盘价低于或等于两个交易日前的最低价
            reference_low = np.min(low[setup_start:setup_end+1])
            countdown_count = 0
            
            for i in range(setup_end + 1, min(setup_end + 22, n)):  # 最多22个交易日
                if close[i] <= low[i-2]:
                    countdown_count += 1
                    countdown[i] = countdown_count
                    if countdown_count >= 13:
                        break
        else:
            # 卖出Countdown：收盘价高于或等于两个交易日前的最高价
            reference_high = np.max(high[setup_start:setup_end+1])
            countdown_count = 0
            
            for i in range(setup_end + 1, min(setup_end + 22, n)):  # 最多22个交易日
                if close[i] >= high[i-2]:
                    countdown_count += 1
                    countdown[i] = countdown_count
                    if countdown_count >= 13:
                        break
        
        return countdown
    
    def _check_latest_signals(self, data: pd.DataFrame, ts_code: str) -> List[NineTurnSignal]:
        """检查最新信号"""
        signals = []
        
        if len(data) < 10:
            return signals
        
        # 检查最近5个交易日的信号
        recent_data = data.tail(5)
        
        for idx, row in recent_data.iterrows():
            # 买入信号
            if row['td_setup_buy'] == 9:
                signal = NineTurnSignal(
                    ts_code=ts_code,
                    name=row.get('name', ''),
                    signal_type='buy',
                    signal_date=row['trade_date'].strftime('%Y-%m-%d'),
                    setup_count=9,
                    countdown_count=int(row['td_countdown_buy']),
                    signal_strength=0.0,  # 待计算
                    price=row['close'],
                    volume=row['vol'],
                    market_cap=0.0,  # 待填充
                    additional_filters={}
                )
                signals.append(signal)
            
            # 卖出信号
            if row['td_setup_sell'] == 9:
                signal = NineTurnSignal(
                    ts_code=ts_code,
                    name=row.get('name', ''),
                    signal_type='sell',
                    signal_date=row['trade_date'].strftime('%Y-%m-%d'),
                    setup_count=9,
                    countdown_count=int(row['td_countdown_sell']),
                    signal_strength=0.0,  # 待计算
                    price=row['close'],
                    volume=row['vol'],
                    market_cap=0.0,  # 待填充
                    additional_filters={}
                )
                signals.append(signal)
            
            # Countdown完成信号
            if row['td_countdown_buy'] == 13:
                signal = NineTurnSignal(
                    ts_code=ts_code,
                    name=row.get('name', ''),
                    signal_type='buy',
                    signal_date=row['trade_date'].strftime('%Y-%m-%d'),
                    setup_count=9,
                    countdown_count=13,
                    signal_strength=0.0,  # 待计算
                    price=row['close'],
                    volume=row['vol'],
                    market_cap=0.0,  # 待填充
                    additional_filters={'countdown_complete': True}
                )
                signals.append(signal)
            
            if row['td_countdown_sell'] == 13:
                signal = NineTurnSignal(
