                    ts_code=ts_code,
                    name=row.get('name', ''),
                    signal_type='sell',
                    signal_date=row['trade_date'].strftime('%Y-%m-%d'),
                    setup_count=9,
                    countdown_count=13,
                    signal_strength=0.0,  # 待计算
                    price=row['close'],
                    volume=row['vol'],
                    market_cap=0.0,  # 待填充
                    additional_filters={'countdown_complete': True}
                )
                signals.append(signal)
        
        return signals
    
    def _apply_filters(self, signals: List[NineTurnSignal], 
                      stock_data: pd.DataFrame, 
                      market_data: pd.DataFrame) -> List[NineTurnSignal]:
        """应用过滤条件"""
        filtered_signals = []
        
        for signal in signals:
            try:
                # 基本过滤条件
                if not self._basic_filters(signal, stock_data):
                    continue
                
                # 计算信号强度
                signal.signal_strength = self._calculate_signal_strength(signal, stock_data, market_data)
                
                # 信号强度过滤
                if signal.signal_strength < 0.3:  # 最低信号强度阈值
                    continue
                
                # 添加额外的技术指标过滤
                if self._technical_filters(signal, stock_data):
                    filtered_signals.append(signal)
                
            except Exception as e:
                self.logger.error(f"Error filtering signal for {signal.ts_code}: {str(e)}")
                continue
        
        return filtered_signals
    
    def _basic_filters(self, signal: NineTurnSignal, stock_data: pd.DataFrame) -> bool:
        """基本过滤条件"""
        latest = stock_data.iloc[-1]
        
        # 价格过滤
        if signal.price < self.min_price or signal.price > self.max_price:
            return False
        
        # 成交量过滤
        if len(stock_data) >= 5:
            avg_volume = stock_data.tail(5)['vol'].mean()
            volume_ratio = signal.volume / avg_volume if avg_volume > 0 else 0
            if volume_ratio < self.min_volume_ratio:
                return False
        
        # 涨跌停过滤
        if abs(latest.get('pct_chg', 0)) > 9.5:  # 接近涨跌停
            return False
        
        return True
    
    def _technical_filters(self, signal: NineTurnSignal, stock_data: pd.DataFrame) -> bool:
        """技术指标过滤"""
        if len(stock_data) < 20:
            return False
        
        latest = stock_data.iloc[-1]
        
        # RSI过滤
        if 'rsi_14' in latest:
            rsi = latest['rsi_14']
            if signal.signal_type == 'buy' and rsi > 70:  # 买入信号但RSI超买
                return False
            if signal.signal_type == 'sell' and rsi < 30:  # 卖出信号但RSI超卖
                return False
        
        # 成交量确认
        if 'vol_ma_5' in latest:
            vol_ratio = latest['vol'] / latest['vol_ma_5'] if latest['vol_ma_5'] > 0 else 0
            if vol_ratio < 1.5:  # 成交量不够放大
                return False
        
        return True
    
    def _calculate_signal_strength(self, signal: NineTurnSignal, 
                                 stock_data: pd.DataFrame, 
                                 market_data: pd.DataFrame) -> float:
        """计算信号强度"""
        strength = 0.5  # 基础强度
        
        try:
            latest = stock_data.iloc[-1]
            
            # Countdown完成加分
            if signal.additional_filters.get('countdown_complete', False):
                strength += 0.3
            
            # 成交量放大加分
            if len(stock_data) >= 5:
                avg_volume = stock_data.tail(5)['vol'].mean()
                volume_ratio = signal.volume / avg_volume if avg_volume > 0 else 1
                if volume_ratio > 2:
                    strength += 0.2
                elif volume_ratio > 1.5:
                    strength += 0.1
            
            # RSI配合加分
            if 'rsi_14' in latest:
                rsi = latest['rsi_14']
                if signal.signal_type == 'buy' and rsi < 40:
                    strength += 0.15
                elif signal.signal_type == 'sell' and rsi > 60:
                    strength += 0.15
            
            # 布林带位置加分
            if 'boll_position' in latest:
                boll_pos = latest['boll_position']
                if signal.signal_type == 'buy' and boll_pos < 0.3:
                    strength += 0.1
                elif signal.signal_type == 'sell' and boll_pos > 0.7:
                    strength += 0.1
            
            # 市场环境调整
            if not market_data.empty:
                market_trend = self._get_market_trend(market_data)
                if signal.signal_type == 'buy' and market_trend > 0:
                    strength += 0.1
                elif signal.signal_type == 'sell' and market_trend < 0:
                    strength += 0.1
            
        except Exception as e:
            self.logger.error(f"Error calculating signal strength: {str(e)}")
        
        return min(strength, 1.0)  # 最大强度为1.0
    
    def _get_market_trend(self, market_data: pd.DataFrame) -> float:
        """获取市场趋势"""
        if len(market_data) < 5:
            return 0
        
        recent_data = market_data.tail(5)
        trend = recent_data['pct_chg'].mean()
        
        ### 6.4 业务逻辑层设计

#### 6.4.1 股票数据服务
```python
# services/stock_service.py
import pandas as pd
import numpy as np
from typing import Dict, List, Any, Optional, Union
from datetime import datetime, timedelta
import logging
from dataclasses import dataclass, asdict
import asyncio
import aioredis
from sqlalchemy.orm import Session

from .data_source_manager import DataSourceManager
from .data_processor import DataProcessor
from .technical_indicators import TechnicalIndicatorEngine
from .nine_turn_selector import NineTurnSelector, NineTurnSignal
from ..models.database import SessionLocal
from ..models.stock_models import Stock, StockDaily, TechnicalIndicator, NineTurnSignals
from ..core.cache import CacheManager

@dataclass
class StockInfo:
    """股票信息数据结构"""
    ts_code: str
    symbol: str
    name: str
    area: str
    industry: str
    market: str
    list_date: str
    fullname: Optional[str] = None
    enname: Optional[str] = None
    exchange: Optional[str] = None
    curr_type: Optional[str] = None
    list_status: Optional[str] = None
    delist_date: Optional[str] = None
    is_hs: Optional[str] = None

@dataclass
class StockQuote:
    """股票行情数据结构"""
    ts_code: str
    name: str
    trade_date: str
    open: float
    high: float
    low: float
    close: float
    pre_close: float
    change: float
    pct_chg: float
    vol: float
    amount: float
    turnover_rate: Optional[float] = None
    volume_ratio: Optional[float] = None
    pe: Optional[float] = None
    pb: Optional[float] = None

class StockService:
    """股票数据服务"""
    
    def __init__(self):
        self.logger = logging.getLogger(__name__)
        self.data_source_manager = DataSourceManager()
        self.data_processor = DataProcessor()
        self.indicator_engine = TechnicalIndicatorEngine()
        self.nine_turn_selector = NineTurnSelector()
        self.cache_manager = CacheManager()
    
    async def get_stock_list(self, market: Optional[str] = None, 
                           list_status: str = 'L') -> List[StockInfo]:
        """获取股票列表"""
        try:
            # 尝试从缓存获取
            cache_key = f"stock_list:{market}:{list_status}"
            cached_data = await self.cache_manager.get(cache_key)
            
            if cached_data:
                return [StockInfo(**item) for item in cached_data]
            
            # 从数据源获取
            raw_data = await self.data_source_manager.get_stock_basic(
                market=market, list_status=list_status
            )
            
            if raw_data.empty:
                return []
            
            # 数据处理
            processed_data = self.data_processor.process_tushare_data(
                raw_data, 'stock_basic'
            )
            
            # 转换为数据结构
            stock_list = []
            for _, row in processed_data.iterrows():
                stock_info = StockInfo(
                    ts_code=row['ts_code'],
                    symbol=row['symbol'],
                    name=row['name'],
                    area=row['area'],
                    industry=row['industry'],
                    market=row['market'],
                    list_date=row['list_date'].strftime('%Y-%m-%d') if pd.notna(row['list_date']) else '',
                    fullname=row.get('fullname'),
                    enname=row.get('enname'),
                    exchange=row.get('exchange'),
                    curr_type=row.get('curr_type'),
                    list_status=row.get('list_status'),
                    delist_date=row['delist_date'].strftime('%Y-%m-%d') if pd.notna(row.get('delist_date')) else None,
                    is_hs=row.get('is_hs')
                )
                stock_list.append(stock_info)
            
            # 缓存结果
            await self.cache_manager.set(
                cache_key, 
                [asdict(stock) for stock in stock_list],
                ttl=3600  # 1小时
            )
            
            return stock_list
            
        except Exception as e:
            self.logger.error(f"Error getting stock list: {str(e)}")
            return []
    
    async def get_stock_quote(self, ts_code: str, 
                            start_date: Optional[str] = None,
                            end_date: Optional[str] = None,
                            limit: int = 100) -> List[StockQuote]:
        """获取股票行情数据"""
        try:
            # 设置默认日期
            if not end_date:
                end_date = datetime.now().strftime('%Y%m%d')
            if not start_date:
                start_date = (datetime.now() - timedelta(days=limit)).strftime('%Y%m%d')
            
            # 尝试从缓存获取
            cache_key = f"stock_quote:{ts_code}:{start_date}:{end_date}"
            cached_data = await self.cache_manager.get(cache_key)
            
            if cached_data:
                return [StockQuote(**item) for item in cached_data]
            
            # 从数据源获取
            raw_data = await self.data_source_manager.get_daily_data(
                ts_code=ts_code, start_date=start_date, end_date=end_date
            )
            
            if raw_data.empty:
                return []
            
            # 数据处理
            processed_data = self.data_processor.process_tushare_data(
                raw_data, 'daily_data'
            )
            
            # 转换为数据结构
            quote_list = []
            for _, row in processed_data.iterrows():
                quote = StockQuote(
                    ts_code=row['ts_code'],
                    name=row.get('name', ''),
                    trade_date=row['trade_date'].strftime('%Y-%m-%d'),
                    open=float(row['open']),
                    high=float(row['high']),
                    low=float(row['low']),
                    close=float(row['close']),
                    pre_close=float(row['pre_close']),
                    change=float(row['change']),
                    pct_chg=float(row['pct_chg']),
                    vol=float(row['vol']),
                    amount=float(row['amount']),
                    turnover_rate=float(row['turnover_rate']) if pd.notna(row.get('turnover_rate')) else None,
                    volume_ratio=float(row['volume_ratio']) if pd.notna(row.get('volume_ratio')) else None,
                    pe=float(row['pe']) if pd.notna(row.get('pe')) else None,
                    pb=float(row['pb']) if pd.notna(row.get('pb')) else None
                )
                quote_list.append(quote)
            
            # 按日期排序
            quote_list.sort(key=lambda x: x.trade_date)
            
            # 缓存结果
            await self.cache_manager.set(
                cache_key,
                [asdict(quote) for quote in quote_list],
                ttl=300  # 5分钟
            )
            
            return quote_list
            
        except Exception as e:
            self.logger.error(f"Error getting stock quote for {ts_code}: {str(e)}")
            return []
    
    async def get_realtime_quote(self, ts_codes: List[str]) -> Dict[str, Dict[str, Any]]:
        """获取实时行情数据"""
        try:
            # 批量获取实时数据
            realtime_data = {}
            
            for ts_code in ts_codes:
                # 尝试从缓存获取
                cache_key = f"realtime_quote:{ts_code}"
                cached_data = await self.cache_manager.get(cache_key)
                
                if cached_data:
                    realtime_data[ts_code] = cached_data
                    continue
                
                # 从AKshare获取实时数据
                raw_data = await self.data_source_manager.get_realtime_quote(ts_code)
                
                if not raw_data.empty:
                    # 数据处理
                    processed_data = self.data_processor.process_akshare_data(
                        raw_data, 'realtime_quote'
                    )
                    
                    if not processed_data.empty:
                        latest = processed_data.iloc[-1]
                        quote_data = {
                            'ts_code': ts_code,
                            'name': latest.get('name', ''),
                            'price': float(latest['close']),
                            'change': float(latest['change']),
                            'pct_chg': float(latest['pct_chg']),
                            'volume': float(latest['vol']),
                            'amount': float(latest['amount']),
                            'high': float(latest['high']),
                            'low': float(latest['low']),
                            'open': float(latest['open']),
                            'pre_close': float(latest['pre_close']),
                            'update_time': datetime.now().isoformat()
                        }
                        
                        realtime_data[ts_code] = quote_data
                        
                        # 缓存结果（短期缓存）
                        await self.cache_manager.set(
                            cache_key, quote_data, ttl=10  # 10秒
                        )
            
            return realtime_data
            
        except Exception as e:
            self.logger.error(f"Error getting realtime quotes: {str(e)}")
            return {}
    
    async def get_technical_indicators(self, ts_code: str, 
                                     period: int = 100) -> Dict[str, Any]:
        """获取技术指标"""
        try:
            # 获取历史数据
            end_date = datetime.now().strftime('%Y%m%d')
            start_date = (datetime.now() - timedelta(days=period * 2)).strftime('%Y%m%d')
            
            raw_data = await self.data_source_manager.get_daily_data(
                ts_code=ts_code, start_date=start_date, end_date=end_date
            )
            
            if raw_data.empty or len(raw_data) < 30:
                return {}
            
            # 计算技术指标
            data_with_indicators = self.indicator_engine.calculate_all_indicators(raw_data)
            
            if data_with_indicators.empty:
                return {}
            
            # 获取最新指标值
            latest = data_with_indicators.iloc[-1]
            
            indicators = {
                'ts_code': ts_code,
                'trade_date': latest['trade_date'].strftime('%Y-%m-%d'),
                'price': float(latest['close']),
                
                # 趋势指标
                'sma_5': float(latest['sma_5']) if pd.notna(latest['sma_5']) else None,
                'sma_10': float(latest['sma_10']) if pd.notna(latest['sma_10']) else None,
                'sma_20': float(latest['sma_20']) if pd.notna(latest['sma_20']) else None,
                'sma_60': float(latest['sma_60']) if pd.notna(latest['sma_60']) else None,
                
                'ema_5': float(latest['ema_5']) if pd.notna(latest['ema_5']) else None,
                'ema_10': float(latest['ema_10']) if pd.notna(latest['ema_10']) else None,
                'ema_20': float(latest['ema_20']) if pd.notna(latest['ema_20']) else None,
                'ema_60': float(latest['ema_60']) if pd.notna(latest['ema_60']) else None,
                
                'macd': float(latest['macd']) if pd.notna(latest['macd']) else None,
                'macd_signal': float(latest['macd_signal']) if pd.notna(latest['macd_signal']) else None,
                'macd_hist': float(latest['macd_hist']) if pd.notna(latest['macd_hist']) else None,
                
                'boll_upper': float(latest['boll_upper']) if pd.notna(latest['boll_upper']) else None,
                'boll_middle': float(latest['boll_middle']) if pd.notna(latest['boll_middle']) else None,
                'boll_lower': float(latest['boll_lower']) if pd.notna(latest['boll_lower']) else None,
                'boll_width': float(latest['boll_width']) if pd.notna(latest['boll_width']) else None,
                'boll_position': float(latest['boll_position']) if pd.notna(latest['boll_position']) else None,
                
                # 动量指标
                'rsi_6': float(latest['rsi_6']) if pd.notna(latest['rsi_6']) else None,
                'rsi_14': float(latest['rsi_14']) if pd.notna(latest['rsi_14']) else None,
                'rsi_24': float(latest['rsi_24']) if pd.notna(latest['rsi_24']) else None,
                
                'kdj_k': float(latest['kdj_k']) if pd.notna(latest['kdj_k']) else None,
                'kdj_d': float(latest['kdj_d']) if pd.notna(latest['kdj_d']) else None,
                'kdj_j': float(latest['kdj_j']) if pd.notna(latest['kdj_j']) else None,
                
                'cci': float(latest['cci']) if pd.notna(latest['cci']) else None,
                'wr': float(latest['wr']) if pd.notna(latest['wr']) else None,
                
                # 成交量指标
                'obv': float(latest['obv']) if pd.notna(latest['obv']) else None,
                'ad': float(latest['ad']) if pd.notna(latest['ad']) else None,
                'adosc': float(latest['adosc']) if pd.notna(latest['adosc']) else None,
                'volume_ratio': float(latest['volume_ratio']) if pd.notna(latest['volume_ratio']) else None,
                
                # 波动率指标
                'atr': float(latest['atr']) if pd.notna(latest['atr']) else None,
                'natr': float(latest['natr']) if pd.notna(latest['natr']) else None,
                'volatility_20': float(latest['volatility_20']) if pd.notna(latest['volatility_20']) else None,
                
                # 九转指标
                'td_setup_buy': int(latest['td_setup_buy']) if pd.notna(latest['td_setup_buy']) else 0,
                'td_setup_sell': int(latest['td_setup_sell']) if pd.notna(latest['td_setup_sell']) else 0,
                'td_countdown_buy': int(latest['td_countdown_buy']) if pd.notna(latest['td_countdown_buy']) else 0,
                'td_countdown_sell': int(latest['td_countdown_sell']) if pd.notna(latest['td_countdown_sell']) else 0,
                'td_buy_signal': int(latest['td_buy_signal']) if pd.notna(latest['td_buy_signal']) else 0,
                'td_sell_signal': int(latest['td_sell_signal']) if pd.notna(latest['td_sell_signal']) else 0,
                
                # 支撑阻力
                'support': float(latest['support']) if pd.notna(latest['support']) else None,
                'resistance': float(latest['resistance']) if pd.notna(latest['resistance']) else None,
            }
            
            # 获取技术指标信号
            signals = self.indicator_engine.get_indicator_signals(data_with_indicators)
            indicators['signals'] = signals
            
            return indicators
            
        except Exception as e:
            self.logger.error(f"Error getting technical indicators for {ts_code}: {str(e)}")
            return {}
    
    async def scan_nine_turn_signals(self, market: Optional[str] = None,
                                   min_signal_strength: float = 0.5) -> List[Dict[str, Any]]:
        """扫描九转信号"""
        try:
            # 获取股票列表
            stock_list = await self.get_stock_list(market=market)
            
            if not stock_list:
                return []
            
            # 批量获取股票数据
            stock_data = {}
            tasks = []
            
            for stock in stock_list[:100]:  # 限制处理数量
                task = self._get_stock_data_for_nine_turn(stock.ts_code)
                tasks.append(task)
            
            results = await asyncio.gather(*tasks, return_exceptions=True)
            
            for i, result in enumerate(results):
                if isinstance(result, Exception):
                    continue
                if not result.empty:
                    stock_data[stock_list[i].ts_code] = result
            
            # 获取市场数据
            market_data = await self._get_market_data()
            
            # 扫描九转信号
            signals = self.nine_turn_selector.scan_nine_turn_signals(
                stock_data, market_data
            )
            
            # 过滤信号强度
            filtered_signals = [
                signal for signal in signals 
                if signal.signal_strength >= min_signal_strength
            ]
            
            # 转换为字典格式
            result = []
            for signal in filtered_signals:
                signal_dict = {
                    'ts_code': signal.ts_code,
                    'name': signal.name,
                    'signal_type': signal.signal_type,
                    'signal_date': signal.signal_date,
                    'setup_count': signal.setup_count,
                    'countdown_count': signal.countdown_count,
                    'signal_strength': signal.signal_strength,
                    'price': signal.price,
                    'volume': signal.volume,
                    'market_cap': signal.market_cap,
                    'additional_filters': signal.additional_filters
                }
                result.append(signal_dict)
            
            return result
            
        except Exception as e:
            self.logger.error(f"Error scanning nine turn signals: {str(e)}")
            return []
    
    async def _get_stock_data_for_nine_turn(self, ts_code: str) -> pd.DataFrame:
        """获取九转分析所需的股票数据"""
        try:
            # 获取最近60个交易日的数据
            end_date = datetime.now().strftime('%Y%m%d')
            start_date = (datetime.now() - timedelta(days=120)).strftime('%Y%m%d')
            
            data = await self.data_source_manager.get_daily_data(
                ts_code=ts_code, start_date=start_date, end_date=end_date
            )
            
            return data
            
        except Exception as e:
            self.logger.error(f"Error getting stock data for nine turn {ts_code}: {str(e)}")
            return pd.DataFrame()
    
    async def _get_market_data(self) -> pd.DataFrame:
        """获取市场数据"""
        try:
            # 获取上证指数数据作为市场参考
            end_date = datetime.now().strftime('%Y%m%d')
            start_date = (datetime.now() - timedelta(days=30)).strftime('%Y%m%d')
            
            data = await self.data_source_manager.get_index_daily(
                ts_code='000001.SH', start_date=start_date, end_date=end_date
            )
            
            return data
            
        except Exception as e:
            self.logger.error(f"Error getting market data: {str(e)}")
            return pd.DataFrame()

#### 6.4.2 用户服务
```python
# services/user_service.py
import hashlib
import jwt
import secrets
from typing import Dict, List, Any, Optional
from datetime import datetime, timedelta
from dataclasses import dataclass
import logging
from sqlalchemy.orm import Session
from sqlalchemy import and_, or_

from ..models.database import SessionLocal
from ..models.user_models import User, UserWatchlist, UserSettings
from ..core.config import settings
from ..core.cache import CacheManager

@dataclass
class UserInfo:
    """用户信息数据结构"""
    id: int
    username: str
    email: str
    nickname: Optional[str]
    avatar: Optional[str]
    created_at: datetime
    last_login: Optional[datetime]
    is_active: bool

@dataclass
class WatchlistItem:
    """自选股数据结构"""
    id: int
    ts_code: str
    symbol: str
    name: str
    added_date: datetime
    notes: Optional[str]
    alert_price_high: Optional[float]
    alert_price_low: Optional[float]
    sort_order: int

class UserService:
    """用户服务"""
    
    def __init__(self):
        self.logger = logging.getLogger(__name__)
        self.cache_manager = CacheManager()
        self.secret_key = settings.SECRET_KEY
        self.algorithm = "HS256"
        self.access_token_expire_minutes = 30
    
    def create_user(self, username: str, email: str, password: str,
                   nickname: Optional[str] = None) -> Optional[UserInfo]:
        """创建用户"""
        db = SessionLocal()
        try:
            # 检查用户名和邮箱是否已存在
            existing_user = db.query(User).filter(
                or_(User.username == username, User.email == email)
            ).first()
            
            if existing_user:
                self.logger.warning(f"User already exists: {username} or {email}")
                return None
            
            # 密码加密
            password_hash = self._hash_password(password)
            
            # 创建用户
            user = User(
                username=username,
                email=email,
                password_hash=password_hash,
                nickname=nickname,
                created_at=datetime.now(),
                is_active=True
            )
            
            db.add(user)
            db.commit()
            db.refresh(user)
            
            # 创建默认设置
            self._create_default_settings(db, user.id)
            
            return UserInfo(
                id=user.id,
                username=user.username,
                email=user.email,
                nickname=user.nickname,
                avatar=user.avatar,
                created_at=user.created_at,
                last_login=user.last_login,
                is_active=user.is_active
            )
            
        except Exception as e:
            db.rollback()
            self.logger.error(f"Error creating user: {str(e)}")
            return None
        finally:
            db.close()
    
    def authenticate_user(self, username: str, password: str) -> Optional[UserInfo]:
        """用户认证"""
        db = SessionLocal()
        try:
            user = db.query(User).filter(
                or_(User.username == username, User.email == username)
            ).first()
            
            if not user or not user.is_active:
                return None
            
            if not self._verify_password(password, user.password_hash):
                return None
            
            # 更新最后登录时间
            user.last_login = datetime.now()
            db.commit()
            
            return UserInfo(
                id=user.id,
                username=user.username,
                email=user.email,
                nickname=user.nickname,
                avatar=user.avatar,
                created_at=user.created_at,
                last_login=user.last_login,
                is_active=user.is_active
            )
            
        except Exception as e:
            self.logger.error(f"Error authenticating user: {str(e)}")
            return None
        finally:
            db.close()
    
    def create_access_token(self, user_id: int, username: str) -> str:
        """创建访问令牌"""
        expire = datetime.utcnow() + timedelta(minutes=self.access_token_expire_minutes)
        to_encode = {
            "sub": str(user_id),
            "username": username,
            "exp": expire
        }
        encoded_jwt = jwt.encode(to_encode, self.secret_key, algorithm=self.algorithm)
        return encoded_jwt
    
    def verify_token(self, token: str) -> Optional[Dict[str, Any]]:
        """验证令牌"""
        try:
            payload = jwt.decode(token, self.secret_key, algorithms=[self.algorithm])
            user_id: str = payload.get("sub")
            username: str = payload.get("username")
            
            if user_id is None or username is None:
                return None
            
            return {"user_id": int(user_id), "username": username}
            
        except jwt.PyJWTError:
            return None
    
    def get_user_watchlist(self, user_id: int) -> List[WatchlistItem]:
        """获取用户自选股"""
        db = SessionLocal()
        try:
            watchlist = db.query(UserWatchlist).filter(
                UserWatchlist.user_id == user_id
            ).order_by(UserWatchlist.sort_order).all()
            
            result = []
            for item in watchlist:
                watchlist_item = WatchlistItem(
                    id=item.id,
                    ts_code=item.ts_code,
                    symbol=item.symbol,
                    name=item.name,
                    added_date=item.added_date,
                    notes=item.notes,
                    alert_price_high=item.alert_price_high,
                    alert_price_low=item.alert_price_low,
                    sort_order=item.sort_order
                )
                result.append(watchlist_item)
            
            return result
            
        except Exception as e:
            self.logger.error(f"Error getting user watchlist: {str(e)}")
            return []
        finally:
            db.close()
    
    def add_to_watchlist(self, user_id: int, ts_code: str, symbol: str, 
                        name: str, notes: Optional[str] = None) -> bool:
        """添加到自选股"""
        db = SessionLocal()
        try:
            # 检查是否已存在
            existing = db.query(UserWatchlist).filter(
                and_(UserWatchlist.user_id == user_id, UserWatchlist.ts_code == ts_code)
            ).first()
            
            if existing:
                self.logger.warning(f"Stock {ts_code} already in watchlist for user {user_id}")
                return False
            
            # 获取下一个排序号
            max_order = db.query(UserWatchlist).filter(
                UserWatchlist.user_id == user_id
            ).count()
            
            # 添加到自选股
            watchlist_item = UserWatchlist(
                user_id=user_id,
                ts_code=ts_code,
                symbol=symbol,
                name=name,
                notes=notes,
                added_date=datetime.now(),
                sort_order=max_order + 1
            )
            
            db.add(watchlist_item)
            db.commit()
            
            # 清除缓存
            cache_key = f"user_watchlist:{user_id}"
            asyncio.create_task(self.cache_manager.delete(cache_key))
            
            return True
            
        except Exception as e:
            db.rollback()
            self.logger.error(f"Error adding to watchlist: {str(e)}")
            return False
        finally:
            db.close()
    
    def remove_from_watchlist(self, user_id: int, ts_code: str) -> bool:
        """从自选股移除"""
        db = SessionLocal()
        try:
            watchlist_item = db.query(UserWatchlist).filter(
                and_(UserWatchlist.user_id == user_id, UserWatchlist.ts_code == ts_code)
            ).first()
            
            if not watchlist_item:
                return False
            
            db.delete(watchlist_item)
            db.commit()
            
            # 清除缓存
            cache_key = f"user_watchlist:{user_id}"
            asyncio.create_task(self.cache_manager.delete(cache_key))
            
            return True
            
        except Exception as e:
            db.rollback()
            self.logger.error(f"Error removing from watchlist: {str(e)}")
            return False
        finally:
            db.close()
    
    def update_watchlist_notes(self, user_id: int, ts_code: str, notes: str) -> bool:
        """更新自选股备注"""
        db = SessionLocal()
        try:
            watchlist_item = db.query(UserWatchlist).filter(
                and_(UserWatchlist.user_id == user_id, UserWatchlist.ts_code == ts_code)
            ).first()
            
            if not watchlist_item:
                return False
            
            watchlist_item.notes = notes
            db.commit()
            
            return True
            
        except Exception as e:
            db.rollback()
            self.logger.error(f"Error updating watchlist notes: {str(e)}")
            return False
        finally:
            db.close()
    
    def set_price_alert(self, user_id: int, ts_code: str, 
                       high_price: Optional[float] = None,
                       low_price: Optional[float] = None) -> bool:
        """设置价格提醒"""
        db = SessionLocal()
        try:
            watchlist_item = db.query(UserWatchlist).filter(
                and_(UserWatchlist.user_id == user_id, UserWatchlist.ts_code == ts_code)
            ).first()
            
            if not watchlist_item:
                return False
            
            watchlist_item.alert_price_high = high_price
            watchlist_item.alert_price_low = low_price
            db.commit()
            
            return True
            
        except Exception as e:
            db.rollback()
            self.logger.error(f"Error setting price alert: {str(e)}")
            return False
        finally:
            db.close()
    
    def _hash_password(self, password: str) -> str:
        """密码加密"""
        salt = secrets.token_hex(16)
        password_hash = hashlib.pbkdf2_hmac('sha256', password.encode('utf-8'), salt.encode('utf-8'), 100000)
        return salt + password_hash.hex()
    
    def _verify_password(self, password: str, password_hash: str) -> bool:
        """验证密码"""
        salt = password_hash[:32]
        stored_hash = password_hash[32:]
        password_hash_check = hashlib.pbkdf2_hmac('sha256', password.encode('utf-8'), salt.encode('utf-8'), 100000)
        return password_hash_check.hex() == stored_hash
    
    def _create_default_settings(self, db: Session, user_id: int):
        """创建默认用户设置"""
        default_settings = UserSettings(
            user_id=user_id,
            theme='light',
            language='zh-CN',
            timezone='Asia/Shanghai',
            email_notifications=True,
            price_alerts=True,
            news_notifications=False,
            auto_refresh_interval=30,
            default_chart_period='1d',
            show_technical_indicators=True,
            created_at=datetime.now()
        )
        
        db.add(default_settings)
        db.commit()

#### 6.4.3 市场数据服务
```python
# services/market_service.py
import pandas as pd
import numpy as np
from typing import Dict, List, Any, Optional, Union
from datetime import datetime, timedelta
import logging
from dataclasses import dataclass, asdict
import asyncio

from .data_source_manager import DataSourceManager
from .data_processor import DataProcessor
from ..core.cache import CacheManager

@dataclass
class MarketOverview:
    """市场概览数据结构"""
    date: str
    sh_index: Dict[str, Any]  # 上证指数
    sz_index: Dict[str, Any]  # 深证成指
    cy_index: Dict[str, Any]  # 创业板指
    hs300_index: Dict[str, Any]  # 沪深300
    up_count: int  # 上涨家数
    down_count: int  # 下跌家数
    flat_count: int  # 平盘家数
    limit_up_count: int  # 涨停家数
    limit_down_count: int  # 跌停家数
    total_amount: float  # 总成交额
    total_volume: float  # 总成交量

@dataclass
class SectorData:
    """板块数据结构"""
    sector_code: str
    sector_name: str
    change_pct: float
    amount: float
    volume: float
    up_count: int
    down_count: int
    leading_stock: Dict[str, Any]

@dataclass
class HotStock:
    """热门股票数据结构"""
    ts_code: str
    name: str
    price: float
    change_pct: float
    amount: float
    volume: float
    turnover_rate: float
    reason: str  # 上榜原因

class MarketService:
    """市场数据服务"""
    
    def __init__(self):
        self.logger = logging.getLogger(__name__)
        self.data_source_manager = DataSourceManager()
        self.data_processor = DataProcessor()
        self.cache_manager = CacheManager()
    
    async def get_market_overview(self) -> Optional[MarketOverview]:
        """获取市场概览"""
        try:
            # 尝试从缓存获取
            cache_key = "market_overview"
            cached_data = await self.cache_manager.get(cache_key)
            
            if cached_data:
                return MarketOverview(**cached_data)
            
            # 获取主要指数数据
            today = datetime.now().strftime('%Y%m%d')
            
            # 并行获取指数数据
            tasks = [
                self.data_source_manager.get_index_daily('000001.SH', today, today),  # 上证指数
                self.data_source_manager.get_index_daily('399001.SZ', today, today),  # 深证成指
                self.data_source_manager.get_index_daily('399006.SZ', today, today),  # 创业板指
                self.data_source_manager.get_index_daily('000300.SH', today, today),  # 沪深300
            ]
            
            results = await asyncio.gather(*tasks, return_exceptions=True)
            
            # 处理指数数据
            indices_data = {}
            index_codes = ['000001.SH', '399001.SZ', '399006.SZ', '000300.SH']
            index_names = ['sh_index', 'sz_index', 'cy_index', 'hs300_index']
            
            for i, result in enumerate(results):
                if isinstance(result, Exception) or result.empty:
                    indices_data[index_names[i]] = {}
                    continue
                
                latest = result.iloc[-1]
                indices_data[index_names[i]] = {
                    'code': index_codes[i],
                    'name': latest.get('name', ''),
                    'close': float(latest['close']),
                    'change': float(latest['change']),
                    'pct_chg': float(latest['pct_chg']),
                    'volume': float(latest['vol']),
                    'amount': float(latest['amount']),
                    'high': float(latest['high']),
                    'low': float(latest['low']),
                    'open': float(latest['open'])
                }
            
            # 获取市场统计数据
            market_stats = await self._get_market_statistics()
            
            overview = MarketOverview(
                date=today,
                sh_index=indices_data.get('sh_index', {}),
                sz_index=indices_data.get('sz_index', {}),
                cy_index=indices_data.get('cy_index', {}),
                hs300_index=indices_data.get('hs300_index', {}),
                up_count=market_stats.get('up_count', 0),
                down_count=market_stats.get('down_count', 0),
                flat_count=market_stats.get('flat_count', 0),
                limit_up_count=market_stats.get('limit_up_count', 0),
                limit_down_count=market_stats.get('limit_down_count', 0),
                total_amount=market_stats.get('total_amount', 0.0),
                total_volume=market_stats.get('total_volume', 0.0)
            )
            
            # 缓存结果
            await self.cache_manager.set(
                cache_key, asdict(overview), ttl=60  # 1分钟
            )
            
            return overview
            
        except Exception as e:
            self.logger.error(f"Error getting market overview: {str(e)}")
            return None
    
    async def get_sector_ranking(self, limit: int = 20) -> List[SectorData]:
        """获取板块排行"""
        try:
            # 尝试从缓存获取
            cache_key = f"sector_ranking:{limit}"
            cached_data = await self.cache_manager.get(cache_key)
            
            if cached_data:
                return [SectorData(**item) for item in cached_data]
            
            # 从数据源获取板块数据
            sector_data = await self.data_source_manager.get_sector_performance()
            
            if sector_data.empty:
                return []
            
            # 数据处理
            processed_data = self.data_processor.process_akshare_data(
                sector_data, 'sector_performance'
            )
            
            # 转换为数据结构
            sectors = []
            for _, row in processed_data.head(limit).iterrows():
                # 获取板块龙头股
                leading_stock = await self._get_sector_leading_stock(row['sector_code'])
                
                sector = SectorData(
                    sector_code=row['sector_code'],
                    sector_name=row['sector_name'],
                    change_pct=float(row['change_pct']),
                    amount=float(row['amount']),
                    volume=float(row['volume']),
                    up_count=int(row.get('up_count', 0)),
                    down_count=int(row.get('down_count', 0)),
                    leading_stock=leading_stock
                )
                sectors.append(sector)
            
            # 缓存结果
            await self.cache_manager.set(
                cache_key,
                [asdict(sector) for sector in sectors],
                ttl=300  # 5分钟
            )
            
            return sectors
            
        except Exception as e:
            self.logger.error(f"Error getting sector ranking: {str(e)}")
            return []
    
    async def get_hot_stocks(self, category: str = 'volume', 
                           limit: int = 20) -> List[HotStock]:
        """获取热门股票"""
        try:
            # 尝试从缓存获取
            cache_key = f"hot_stocks:{category}:{limit}"
            cached_data = await self.cache_manager.get(cache_key)
            
            if cached_data:
                return [HotStock(**item) for item in cached_data]
            
            # 根据类别获取不同的热门股票
            if category == 'volume':
                raw_data = await self.data_source_manager.get_volume_ranking()
                reason = '成交量排行'
            elif category == 'amount':
                raw_data = await self.data_source_manager.get_amount_ranking()
                reason = '成交额排行'
            elif category == 'pct_chg':
                raw_data = await self.data_source_manager.get_pct_change_ranking()
                reason = '涨幅排行'
            elif category == 'turnover':
                raw_data = await self.data_source_manager.get_turnover_ranking()
                reason = '换手率排行'
            else:
                raw_data = await self.data_source_manager.get_volume_ranking()
                reason = '成交量排行'
            
            if raw_data.empty:
                return []
            
            # 数据处理
            processed_data = self.data_processor.process_akshare_data(
                raw_data, 'hot_stocks'
            )
            
            # 转换为数据结构
            hot_stocks = []
            for _, row in processed_data.head(limit).iterrows():
                hot_stock = HotStock(
                    ts_code=row['ts_code'],
                    name=row['name'],
                    price=float(row['price']),
                    change_pct=float(row['pct_chg']),
                    amount=float(row['amount']),
                    volume=float(row['volume']),
                    turnover_rate=float(row.get('turnover_rate', 0)),
                    reason=reason
                )
                hot_stocks.append(hot_stock)
            
            # 缓存结果
            await self.cache_manager.set(
                cache_key,
                [asdict(stock) for stock in hot_stocks],
                ttl=300  # 5分钟
            )
            
            return hot_stocks
            
        except Exception as e:
            self.logger.error(f"Error getting hot stocks: {str(e)}")
            return []
    
    async def get_money_flow(self, ts_code: Optional[str] = None) -> Dict[str, Any]:
        """获取资金流向"""
        try:
            if ts_code:
                # 个股资金流向
                cache_key = f"money_flow:{ts_code}"
                cached_data = await self.cache_manager.get(cache_key)
                
                if cached_data:
                    return cached_data
                
                raw_data = await self.data_source_manager.get_individual_money_flow(ts_code)
            else:
                # 市场整体资金流向
                cache_key = "market_money_flow"
                cached_data = await self.cache_manager.get(cache_key)
                
                if cached_data:
                    return cached_data
                
                raw_data = await self.data_source_manager.get_market_money_flow()
            
            if raw_data.empty:
                return {}
            
            # 数据处理
            processed_data = self.data_processor.process_akshare_data(
                raw_data, 'money_flow'
            )
            
            if processed_data.empty:
                return {}
            
            latest = processed_data.iloc[-1]
            
            money_flow_data = {
                'ts_code': ts_code or 'market',
                'date': latest.get('trade_date', datetime.now().strftime('%Y-%m-%d')),
                'main_net_inflow': float(latest.get('main_net_inflow', 0)),
                'main_net_inflow_rate': float(latest.get('main_net_inflow_rate', 0)),
                'super_large_net_inflow': float(latest.get('super_large_net_inflow', 0)),
                'super_large_net_inflow_rate': float(latest.get('super_large_net_inflow_rate', 0)),
                'large_net_inflow': float(latest.get('large_net_inflow', 0)),
                'large_net_inflow_rate': float(latest.get('large_net_inflow_rate', 0)),
                'medium_net_inflow': float(latest.get('medium_net_inflow', 0)),
                'medium_net_inflow_rate': float(latest.get('medium_net_inflow_rate', 0)),
                'small_net_inflow': float(latest.get('small_net_inflow', 0)),
                'small_net_inflow_rate': float(latest.get('small_net_inflow_rate', 0))
            }
            
            # 缓存结果
            await self.cache_manager.set(
                cache_key, money_flow_data, ttl=300  # 5分钟
            )
            
            return money_flow_data
            
        except Exception as e:
            self.logger.error(f"Error getting money flow: {str(e)}")
            return {}
    
    async def _get_market_statistics(self) -> Dict[str, Any]:
        """获取市场统计数据"""
        try:
            # 获取今日所有股票数据进行统计
            today = datetime.now().strftime('%Y%m%d')
            
            # 这里应该获取所有股票的今日数据，为了性能考虑，可以使用预计算的统计数据
            # 或者从专门的市场统计接口获取
            market_stats = await self.data_source_manager.get_market_statistics()
            
            if market_stats.empty:
                return {
                    'up_count': 0, 'down_count': 0, 'flat_count': 0,
                    'limit_up_count': 0, 'limit_down_count': 0,
                    'total_amount': 0.0, 'total_volume': 0.0
                }
            
            latest = market_stats.iloc[-1]
            
            return {
                'up_count': int(latest.get('up_count', 0)),
                'down_count': int(latest.get('down_count', 0)),
                'flat_count': int(latest.get('flat_count', 0)),
                'limit_up_count': int(latest.get('limit_up_count', 0)),
                'limit_down_count': int(latest.get('limit_down_count', 0)),
                'total_amount': float(latest.get('total_amount', 0)),
                'total_volume': float(latest.get('total_volume', 0))
            }
            
        except Exception as e:
            self.logger.error(f"Error getting market statistics: {str(e)}")
            return {
                'up_count': 0, 'down_count': 0, 'flat_count': 0,
                'limit_up_count': 0, 'limit_down_count': 0,
                'total_amount': 0.0, 'total_volume': 0.0
            }
    
    async def _get_sector_leading_stock(self, sector_code: str) -> Dict[str, Any]:
        """获取板块龙头股"""
        try:
            # 获取板块成分股
            stocks = await self.data_source_manager.get_sector_stocks(sector_code)
            
            if stocks.empty:
                return {}
            
            # 按成交额排序，取第一名作为龙头股
            leading = stocks.iloc[0]
            
            return {
                'ts_code': leading['ts_code'],
                'name': leading['name'],
                'price': float(leading['close']),
                'change_pct': float(leading['pct_chg']),
                'amount': float(leading['amount'])
            }
            
        except Exception as e:
            self.logger.error(f"Error getting sector leading stock: {str(e)}")
            #### 6.4.4 WebSocket 实时数据服务
```python
# services/websocket_service.py
import asyncio
import json
import logging
from typing import Dict, List, Set, Any, Optional
from datetime import datetime
import websockets
from websockets.server import WebSocketServerProtocol
from dataclasses import asdict

from .stock_service import StockService
from .market_service import MarketService
from ..core.cache import CacheManager

class WebSocketManager:
    """WebSocket 连接管理器"""
    
    def __init__(self):
        self.logger = logging.getLogger(__name__)
        self.connections: Dict[str, WebSocketServerProtocol] = {}
        self.subscriptions: Dict[str, Set[str]] = {}  # user_id -> set of subscription keys
        self.stock_service = StockService()
        self.market_service = MarketService()
        self.cache_manager = CacheManager()
        self.is_running = False
        
    async def register_connection(self, websocket: WebSocketServerProtocol, user_id: str):
        """注册 WebSocket 连接"""
        self.connections[user_id] = websocket
        self.subscriptions[user_id] = set()
        self.logger.info(f"User {user_id} connected")
        
        try:
            await websocket.wait_closed()
        finally:
            await self.unregister_connection(user_id)
    
    async def unregister_connection(self, user_id: str):
        """注销 WebSocket 连接"""
        if user_id in self.connections:
            del self.connections[user_id]
        if user_id in self.subscriptions:
            del self.subscriptions[user_id]
        self.logger.info(f"User {user_id} disconnected")
    
    async def handle_message(self, websocket: WebSocketServerProtocol, user_id: str, message: str):
        """处理客户端消息"""
        try:
            data = json.loads(message)
            action = data.get('action')
            
            if action == 'subscribe':
                await self._handle_subscribe(user_id, data)
            elif action == 'unsubscribe':
                await self._handle_unsubscribe(user_id, data)
            elif action == 'get_realtime_quote':
                await self._handle_get_realtime_quote(websocket, user_id, data)
            elif action == 'get_market_overview':
                await self._handle_get_market_overview(websocket, user_id)
            else:
                await self._send_error(websocket, f"Unknown action: {action}")
                
        except json.JSONDecodeError:
            await self._send_error(websocket, "Invalid JSON format")
        except Exception as e:
            self.logger.error(f"Error handling message: {str(e)}")
            await self._send_error(websocket, "Internal server error")
    
    async def _handle_subscribe(self, user_id: str, data: Dict[str, Any]):
        """处理订阅请求"""
        subscription_type = data.get('type')
        params = data.get('params', {})
        
        if subscription_type == 'stock_quote':
            ts_codes = params.get('ts_codes', [])
            for ts_code in ts_codes:
                subscription_key = f"stock_quote:{ts_code}"
                self.subscriptions[user_id].add(subscription_key)
                
        elif subscription_type == 'market_overview':
            subscription_key = "market_overview"
            self.subscriptions[user_id].add(subscription_key)
            
        elif subscription_type == 'sector_ranking':
            subscription_key = "sector_ranking"
            self.subscriptions[user_id].add(subscription_key)
            
        elif subscription_type == 'hot_stocks':
            category = params.get('category', 'volume')
            subscription_key = f"hot_stocks:{category}"
            self.subscriptions[user_id].add(subscription_key)
        
        self.logger.info(f"User {user_id} subscribed to {subscription_type}")
    
    async def _handle_unsubscribe(self, user_id: str, data: Dict[str, Any]):
        """处理取消订阅请求"""
        subscription_type = data.get('type')
        params = data.get('params', {})
        
        if subscription_type == 'stock_quote':
            ts_codes = params.get('ts_codes', [])
            for ts_code in ts_codes:
                subscription_key = f"stock_quote:{ts_code}"
                self.subscriptions[user_id].discard(subscription_key)
                
        elif subscription_type == 'market_overview':
            subscription_key = "market_overview"
            self.subscriptions[user_id].discard(subscription_key)
            
        elif subscription_type == 'sector_ranking':
            subscription_key = "sector_ranking"
            self.subscriptions[user_id].discard(subscription_key)
            
        elif subscription_type == 'hot_stocks':
            category = params.get('category', 'volume')
            subscription_key = f"hot_stocks:{category}"
            self.subscriptions[user_id].discard(subscription_key)
        
        self.logger.info(f"User {user_id} unsubscribed from {subscription_type}")
    
    async def _handle_get_realtime_quote(self, websocket: WebSocketServerProtocol, 
                                       user_id: str, data: Dict[str, Any]):
        """处理获取实时行情请求"""
        ts_codes = data.get('params', {}).get('ts_codes', [])
        
        if not ts_codes:
            await self._send_error(websocket, "ts_codes parameter is required")
            return
        
        try:
            quotes = await self.stock_service.get_realtime_quote(ts_codes)
            
            response = {
                'type': 'realtime_quote',
                'data': quotes,
                'timestamp': datetime.now().isoformat()
            }
            
            await self._send_message(websocket, response)
            
        except Exception as e:
            self.logger.error(f"Error getting realtime quote: {str(e)}")
            await self._send_error(websocket, "Failed to get realtime quote")
    
    async def _handle_get_market_overview(self, websocket: WebSocketServerProtocol, user_id: str):
        """处理获取市场概览请求"""
        try:
            overview = await self.market_service.get_market_overview()
            
            if overview:
                response = {
                    'type': 'market_overview',
                    'data': asdict(overview),
                    'timestamp': datetime.now().isoformat()
                }
            else:
                response = {
                    'type': 'market_overview',
                    'data': None,
                    'timestamp': datetime.now().isoformat()
                }
            
            await self._send_message(websocket, response)
            
        except Exception as e:
            self.logger.error(f"Error getting market overview: {str(e)}")
            await self._send_error(websocket, "Failed to get market overview")
    
    async def start_data_broadcast(self):
        """启动数据广播"""
        self.is_running = True
        
        # 启动不同的广播任务
        tasks = [
            asyncio.create_task(self._broadcast_stock_quotes()),
            asyncio.create_task(self._broadcast_market_overview()),
            asyncio.create_task(self._broadcast_sector_ranking()),
            asyncio.create_task(self._broadcast_hot_stocks()),
        ]
        
        try:
            await asyncio.gather(*tasks)
        except Exception as e:
            self.logger.error(f"Error in data broadcast: {str(e)}")
        finally:
            self.is_running = False
    
    async def stop_data_broadcast(self):
        """停止数据广播"""
        self.is_running = False
    
    async def _broadcast_stock_quotes(self):
        """广播股票实时行情"""
        while self.is_running:
            try:
                # 收集所有订阅的股票代码
                subscribed_stocks = set()
                for user_id, subscriptions in self.subscriptions.items():
                    for subscription in subscriptions:
                        if subscription.startswith('stock_quote:'):
                            ts_code = subscription.split(':', 1)[1]
                            subscribed_stocks.add(ts_code)
                
                if subscribed_stocks:
                    # 批量获取实时行情
                    quotes = await self.stock_service.get_realtime_quote(list(subscribed_stocks))
                    
                    # 向订阅用户推送数据
                    for user_id, subscriptions in self.subscriptions.items():
                        user_quotes = {}
                        for subscription in subscriptions:
                            if subscription.startswith('stock_quote:'):
                                ts_code = subscription.split(':', 1)[1]
                                if ts_code in quotes:
                                    user_quotes[ts_code] = quotes[ts_code]
                        
                        if user_quotes and user_id in self.connections:
                            response = {
                                'type': 'stock_quote_update',
                                'data': user_quotes,
                                'timestamp': datetime.now().isoformat()
                            }
                            
                            try:
                                await self._send_message(self.connections[user_id], response)
                            except Exception as e:
                                self.logger.error(f"Error sending to user {user_id}: {str(e)}")
                
                await asyncio.sleep(5)  # 5秒更新一次
                
            except Exception as e:
                self.logger.error(f"Error in stock quotes broadcast: {str(e)}")
                await asyncio.sleep(10)
    
    async def _broadcast_market_overview(self):
        """广播市场概览"""
        while self.is_running:
            try:
                # 检查是否有用户订阅市场概览
                subscribed_users = []
                for user_id, subscriptions in self.subscriptions.items():
                    if 'market_overview' in subscriptions:
                        subscribed_users.append(user_id)
                
                if subscribed_users:
                    overview = await self.market_service.get_market_overview()
                    
                    if overview:
                        response = {
                            'type': 'market_overview_update',
                            'data': asdict(overview),
                            'timestamp': datetime.now().isoformat()
                        }
                        
                        for user_id in subscribed_users:
                            if user_id in self.connections:
                                try:
                                    await self._send_message(self.connections[user_id], response)
                                except Exception as e:
                                    self.logger.error(f"Error sending to user {user_id}: {str(e)}")
                
                await asyncio.sleep(30)  # 30秒更新一次
                
            except Exception as e:
                self.logger.error(f"Error in market overview broadcast: {str(e)}")
                await asyncio.sleep(60)
    
    async def _broadcast_sector_ranking(self):
        """广播板块排行"""
        while self.is_running:
            try:
                # 检查是否有用户订阅板块排行
                subscribed_users = []
                for user_id, subscriptions in self.subscriptions.items():
                    if 'sector_ranking' in subscriptions:
                        subscribed_users.append(user_id)
                
                if subscribed_users:
                    sectors = await self.market_service.get_sector_ranking()
                    
                    response = {
                        'type': 'sector_ranking_update',
                        'data': [asdict(sector) for sector in sectors],
                        'timestamp': datetime.now().isoformat()
                    }
                    
                    for user_id in subscribed_users:
                        if user_id in self.connections:
                            try:
                                await self._send_message(self.connections[user_id], response)
                            except Exception as e:
                                self.logger.error(f"Error sending to user {user_id}: {str(e)}")
                
                await asyncio.sleep(60)  # 1分钟更新一次
                
            except Exception as e:
                self.logger.error(f"Error in sector ranking broadcast: {str(e)}")
                await asyncio.sleep(120)
    
    async def _broadcast_hot_stocks(self):
        """广播热门股票"""
        while self.is_running:
            try:
                # 收集所有订阅的热门股票类别
                subscribed_categories = set()
                for user_id, subscriptions in self.subscriptions.items():
                    for subscription in subscriptions:
                        if subscription.startswith('hot_stocks:'):
                            category = subscription.split(':', 1)[1]
                            subscribed_categories.add(category)
                
                for category in subscribed_categories:
                    hot_stocks = await self.market_service.get_hot_stocks(category)
                    
                    response = {
                        'type': 'hot_stocks_update',
                        'category': category,
                        'data': [asdict(stock) for stock in hot_stocks],
                        'timestamp': datetime.now().isoformat()
                    }
                    
                    # 向订阅该类别的用户推送
                    subscription_key = f"hot_stocks:{category}"
                    for user_id, subscriptions in self.subscriptions.items():
                        if subscription_key in subscriptions and user_id in self.connections:
                            try:
                                await self._send_message(self.connections[user_id], response)
                            except Exception as e:
                                self.logger.error(f"Error sending to user {user_id}: {str(e)}")
                
                await asyncio.sleep(120)  # 2分钟更新一次
                
            except Exception as e:
                self.logger.error(f"Error in hot stocks broadcast: {str(e)}")
                await asyncio.sleep(180)
    
    async def _send_message(self, websocket: WebSocketServerProtocol, message: Dict[str, Any]):
        """发送消息到客户端"""
        try:
            await websocket.send(json.dumps(message, ensure_ascii=False))
        except websockets.exceptions.ConnectionClosed:
            pass
        except Exception as e:
            self.logger.error(f"Error sending message: {str(e)}")
    
    async def _send_error(self, websocket: WebSocketServerProtocol, error_message: str):
        """发送错误消息"""
        error_response = {
            'type': 'error',
            'message': error_message,
            'timestamp': datetime.now().isoformat()
        }
        await self._send_message(websocket, error_response)

# WebSocket 服务器启动函数
async def websocket_handler(websocket: WebSocketServerProtocol, path: str):
    """WebSocket 处理函数"""
    manager = WebSocketManager()
    
    # 这里应该从 WebSocket 连接中获取用户认证信息
    # 简化处理，使用 IP 作为用户标识
    user_id = websocket.remote_address[0]
    
    await manager.register_connection(websocket, user_id)
    
    try:
        async for message in websocket:
            await manager.handle_message(websocket, user_id, message)
    except websockets.exceptions.ConnectionClosed:
        pass
    except Exception as e:
        logging.error(f"WebSocket error: {str(e)}")

### 6.5 API 路由层设计

#### 6.5.1 FastAPI 应用配置
```python
# main.py
from fastapi import FastAPI, HTTPException, Depends, status
from fastapi.middleware.cors import CORSMiddleware
from fastapi.security import HTTPBearer, HTTPAuthorizationCredentials
from fastapi.responses import JSONResponse
import uvicorn
import logging
from contextlib import asynccontextmanager

from .routers import auth, stocks, market, users, websocket
from .services.websocket_service import WebSocketManager
from .core.config import settings
from .core.database import engine, Base
from .services.user_service import UserService

# 配置日志
logging.basicConfig(
    level=logging.INFO,
    format='%(asctime)s - %(name)s - %(levelname)s - %(message)s'
)

# 创建数据库表
Base.metadata.create_all(bind=engine)

# WebSocket 管理器
websocket_manager = WebSocketManager()

@asynccontextmanager
async def lifespan(app: FastAPI):
    """应用生命周期管理"""
    # 启动时执行
    logging.info("Starting stock trading system...")
    
    # 启动 WebSocket 数据广播
    import asyncio
    broadcast_task = asyncio.create_task(websocket_manager.start_data_broadcast())
    
    yield
    
    # 关闭时执行
    logging.info("Shutting down stock trading system...")
    await websocket_manager.stop_data_broadcast()
    broadcast_task.cancel()

# 创建 FastAPI 应用
app = FastAPI(
    title="股票交易系统 API",
    description="基于 FastAPI 的股票数据分析和九转选股系统",
    version="1.0.0",
    lifespan=lifespan
)

# 配置 CORS
app.add_middleware(
    CORSMiddleware,
    allow_origins=settings.ALLOWED_HOSTS,
    allow_credentials=True,
    allow_methods=["*"],
    allow_headers=["*"],
)

# 安全配置
security = HTTPBearer()
user_service = UserService()

async def get_current_user(credentials: HTTPAuthorizationCredentials = Depends(security)):
    """获取当前用户"""
    token = credentials.credentials
    user_info = user_service.verify_token(token)
    
    if not user_info:
        raise HTTPException(
            status_code=status.HTTP_401_UNAUTHORIZED,
            detail="Invalid authentication credentials",
            headers={"WWW-Authenticate": "Bearer"},
        )
    
    return user_info

# 注册路由
app.include_router(auth.router, prefix="/api/v1/auth", tags=["认证"])
app.include_router(stocks.router, prefix="/api/v1/stocks", tags=["股票数据"])
app.include_router(market.router, prefix="/api/v1/market", tags=["市场数据"])
app.include_router(users.router, prefix="/api/v1/users", tags=["用户管理"])
app.include_router(websocket.router, prefix="/api/v1/ws", tags=["WebSocket"])

# 全局异常处理
@app.exception_handler(Exception)
async def global_exception_handler(request, exc):
    """全局异常处理"""
    logging.error(f"Global exception: {str(exc)}")
    return JSONResponse(
        status_code=500,
        content={"message": "Internal server error", "detail": str(exc)}
    )

# 健康检查
@app.get("/health")
async def health_check():
    """健康检查"""
    return {"status": "healthy", "timestamp": "2024-01-01T00:00:00Z"}

# 根路径
@app.get("/")
async def root():
    """根路径"""
    return {
        "message": "股票交易系统 API",
        "version": "1.0.0",
        "docs": "/docs",
        "redoc": "/redoc"
    }

if __name__ == "__main__":
    uvicorn.run(
        "main:app",
        host=settings.HOST,
        port=settings.PORT,
        reload=settings.DEBUG,
        log_level="info"
    )

#### 6.5.2 认证路由
```python
# routers/auth.py
from fastapi import APIRouter, HTTPException, status, Depends
from fastapi.security import OAuth2PasswordRequestForm
from pydantic import BaseModel, EmailStr
from typing import Optional

from ..services.user_service import UserService, UserInfo

router = APIRouter()
user_service = UserService()

class UserRegister(BaseModel):
    """用户注册请求"""
    username: str
    email: EmailStr
    password: str
    nickname: Optional[str] = None

class UserLogin(BaseModel):
    """用户登录请求"""
    username: str
    password: str

class TokenResponse(BaseModel):
    """令牌响应"""
    access_token: str
    token_type: str
    user_info: dict

@router.post("/register", response_model=TokenResponse)
async def register(user_data: UserRegister):
    """用户注册"""
    # 创建用户
    user_info = user_service.create_user(
        username=user_data.username,
        email=user_data.email,
        password=user_data.password,
        nickname=user_data.nickname
    )
    
    if not user_info:
        raise HTTPException(
            status_code=status.HTTP_400_BAD_REQUEST,
            detail="Username or email already exists"
        )
    
    # 生成访问令牌
    access_token = user_service.create_access_token(
        user_id=user_info.id,
        username=user_info.username
    )
    
    return TokenResponse(
        access_token=access_token,
        token_type="bearer",
        user_info={
            "id": user_info.id,
            "username": user_info.username,
            "email": user_info.email,
            "nickname": user_info.nickname,
            "avatar": user_info.avatar
        }
    )

@router.post("/login", response_model=TokenResponse)
async def login(user_data: UserLogin):
    """用户登录"""
    # 用户认证
    user_info = user_service.authenticate_user(
        username=user_data.username,
        password=user_data.password
    )
    
    if not user_info:
        raise HTTPException(
            status_code=status.HTTP_401_UNAUTHORIZED,
            detail="Incorrect username or password"
        )
    
    # 生成访问令牌
    access_token = user_service.create_access_token(
        user_id=user_info.id,
        username=user_info.username
    )
    
    return TokenResponse(
        access_token=access_token,
        token_type="bearer",
        user_info={
            "id": user_info.id,
            "username": user_info.username,
            "email": user_info.email,
            "nickname": user_info.nickname,
            "avatar": user_info.avatar
        }
    )

@router.post("/token", response_model=TokenResponse)
async def login_for_access_token(form_data: OAuth2PasswordRequestForm = Depends()):
    """OAuth2 兼容的登录接口"""
    user_info = user_service.authenticate_user(
        username=form_data.username,
        password=form_data.password
    )
    
    if not user_info:
        raise HTTPException(
            status_code=status.HTTP_401_UNAUTHORIZED,
            detail="Incorrect username or password",
            headers={"WWW-Authenticate": "Bearer"},
        )
    
    access_token = user_service.create_access_token(
        user_id=user_info.id,
        username=user_info.username
    )
    
    return TokenResponse(
        access_token=access_token,
        token_type="bearer",
        user_info={
            "id": user_info.id,
            "username": user_info.username,
            "email": user_info.email,
            "nickname": user_info.nickname,
            "avatar": user_info.avatar
        }
    )

#### 6.5.3 股票数据路由
```python
# routers/stocks.py
from fastapi import APIRouter, HTTPException, Depends, Query
from typing import List, Optional, Dict, Any
from pydantic import BaseModel
from datetime import datetime

from ..services.stock_service import StockService, StockInfo, StockQuote
from ..main import get_current_user

router = APIRouter()
stock_service = StockService()

class StockListResponse(BaseModel):
    """股票列表响应"""
    stocks: List[dict]
    total: int

class StockQuoteResponse(BaseModel):
    """股票行情响应"""
    ts_code: str
    quotes: List[dict]

class TechnicalIndicatorsResponse(BaseModel):
    """技术指标响应"""
    ts_code: str
    indicators: dict

class NineTurnSignalsResponse(BaseModel):
    """九转信号响应"""
    signals: List[dict]
    total: int

@router.get("/list", response_model=StockListResponse)
async def get_stock_list(
    market: Optional[str] = Query(None, description="市场类型"),
    list_status: str = Query("L", description="上市状态"),
    current_user: dict = Depends(get_current_user)
):
    """获取股票列表"""
    try:
        stocks = await stock_service.get_stock_list(market=market, list_status=list_status)
        
        return StockListResponse(
            stocks=[{
                "ts_code": stock.ts_code,
                "symbol": stock.symbol,
                "name": stock.name,
                "area": stock.area,
                "industry": stock.industry,
                "market": stock.market,
                "list_date": stock.list_date
            } for stock in stocks],
            total=len(stocks)
        )
        
    except Exception as e:
        raise HTTPException(status_code=500, detail=str(e))

@router.get("/{ts_code}/quote", response_model=StockQuoteResponse)
async def get_stock_quote(
    ts_code: str,
    start_date: Optional[str] = Query(None, description="开始日期 YYYYMMDD"),
    end_date: Optional[str] = Query(None, description="结束日期 YYYYMMDD"),
    limit: int = Query(100, description="数据条数"),
    current_user: dict = Depends(get_current_user)
):
    """获取股票行情"""
    try:
        quotes = await stock_service.get_stock_quote(
            ts_code=ts_code,
            start_date=start_date,
            end_date=end_date,
            limit=limit
        )
        
        return StockQuoteResponse(
            ts_code=ts_code,
            quotes=[{
                "trade_date": quote.trade_date,
                "open": quote.open,
                "high": quote.high,
                "low": quote.low,
                "close": quote.close,
                "pre_close": quote.pre_close,
                "change": quote.change,
                "pct_chg": quote.pct_chg,
                "vol": quote.vol,
                "amount": quote.amount,
                "turnover_rate": quote.turnover_rate,
                "volume_ratio": quote.volume_ratio,
                "pe": quote.pe,
                "pb": quote.pb
            } for quote in quotes]
        )
        
    except Exception as e:
        raise HTTPException(status_code=500, detail=str(e))

@router.post("/realtime")
async def get_realtime_quotes(
    ts_codes: List[str],
    current_user: dict = Depends(get_current_user)
):
    """获取实时行情"""
    try:
        quotes = await stock_service.get_realtime_quote(ts_codes)
        return {"quotes": quotes}
        
    except Exception as e:
        raise HTTPException(status_code=500, detail=str(e))

@router.get("/{ts_code}/indicators", response_model=TechnicalIndicatorsResponse)
async def get_technical_indicators(
    ts_code: str,
    period: int = Query(100, description="计算周期"),
    current_user: dict = Depends(get_current_user)
):
    """获取技术指标"""
    try:
        indicators = await stock_service.get_technical_indicators(ts_code, period)
        
        return TechnicalIndicatorsResponse(
            ts_code=ts_code,
            indicators=indicators
        )
        
    except Exception as e:
        raise HTTPException(status_code=500, detail=str(e))

@router.get("/nine-turn-signals", response_model=NineTurnSignalsResponse)
async def get_nine_turn_signals(
    market: Optional[str] = Query(None, description="市场类型"),
    min_signal_strength: float = Query(0.5, description="最小信号强度"),
    current_user: dict = Depends(get_current_user)
):
    """获取九转信号"""
    try:
        signals = await stock_service.scan_nine_turn_signals(
            market=market,
            min_signal_strength=min_signal_strength
        )
        
        return NineTurnSignalsResponse(
            signals=signals,
            total=len(signals)
        )
        
    except Exception as e:
        raise HTTPException(status_code=500, detail=str(e))

#### 6.5.4 市场数据路由
```python
# routers/market.py
from fastapi import APIRouter, HTTPException, Depends, Query
from typing import List, Optional
from pydantic import BaseModel

from ..services.market_service import MarketService
from ..main import get_current_user

router = APIRouter()
market_service = MarketService()

class MarketOverviewResponse(BaseModel):
    """市场概览响应"""
    overview: dict

class SectorRankingResponse(BaseModel):
    """板块排行响应"""
    sectors: List[dict]
    total: int

class HotStocksResponse(BaseModel):
    """热门股票响应"""
    stocks: List[dict]
    category: str
    total: int

class MoneyFlowResponse(BaseModel):
    """资金流向响应"""
    money_flow: dict

@router.get("/overview", response_model=MarketOverviewResponse)
async def get_market_overview(current_user: dict = Depends(get_current_user)):
    """获取市场概览"""
    try:
        overview = await market_service.get_market_overview()
        
        if not overview:
            raise HTTPException(status_code=404, detail="Market overview not found")
        
        return MarketOverviewResponse(overview=overview.__dict__)
        
    except Exception as e:
        raise HTTPException(status_code=500, detail=str(e))

@router.get("/sectors", response_model=SectorRankingResponse)
async def get_sector_ranking(
    limit: int = Query(20, description="返回数量"),
    current_user: dict = Depends(get_current_user)
):
    """获取板块排行"""
    try:
        sectors = await market_service.get_sector_ranking(limit=limit)
        
        return SectorRankingResponse(
            sectors=[{
                "sector_code": sector.sector_code,
                "sector_name": sector.sector_name,
                "change_pct": sector.change_pct,
                "amount": sector.amount,
                "volume": sector.volume,
                "up_count": sector.up_count,
                "down_count": sector.down_count,
                "leading_stock": sector.leading_stock
            } for sector in sectors],
            total=len(sectors)
        )
        
    except Exception as e:
        raise HTTPException(status_code=500, detail=str(e))

@router.get("/hot-stocks", response_model=HotStocksResponse)
async def get_hot_stocks(
    category: str = Query("volume", description="排行类别"),
    limit: int = Query(20, description="返回数量"),
    current_user: dict = Depends(get_current_user)
):
    """获取热门股票"""
    try:
        stocks = await market_service.get_hot_stocks(category=category, limit=limit)
        
        return HotStocksResponse(
            stocks=[{
                "ts_code": stock.ts_code,
                "name": stock.name,
                "price": stock.price,
                "change_pct": stock.change_pct,
                "amount": stock.amount,
                "volume": stock.volume,
                "turnover_rate": stock.turnover_rate,
                "reason": stock.reason
            } for stock in stocks],
            category=category,
            total=len(stocks)
        )
        
    except Exception as e:
        raise HTTPException(status_code=500, detail=str(e))

@router.get("/money-flow", response_model=MoneyFlowResponse)
async def get_money_flow(
    ts_code: Optional[str] = Query(None, description="股票代码，为空则获取市场整体资金流向"),
    current_user: dict = Depends(get_current_user)
):
    """获取资金流向"""
    try:
        money_flow = await market_service.get_money_flow(ts_code=ts_code)
        
        return MoneyFlowResponse(money_flow=money_flow)
        
    except Exception as e:
        raise HTTPException(status_code=500, detail=str(e))

        """获取指数历史数据 - 完整字段"""

            fields='ts_code,trade_date,close,open,high,low,pre_close,change,pct_chg,vol,amount'
