    def get_index_basic(self) -> pd.DataFrame:
        """获取指数基础信息"""
        return self.pro.index_basic(
            market='',
            fields='ts_code,name,fullname,market,publisher,index_type,category,base_date,base_point,list_date,weight_rule,desc,exp_date'

        return self.pro.concept(
            fields='code,name,src'
        )
    
    def get_concept_detail(self, id: str) -> pd.DataFrame:
        """获取概念股列表"""
        return self.pro.concept_detail(
            id=id,
            fields='id,concept_name,ts_code,name,in_date,out_date'
        )
    
    def get_limit_list(self, trade_date: str, limit_type: str = '') -> pd.DataFrame:
        """获取涨跌停股票列表"""
        return self.pro.limit_list(
            trade_date=trade_date,
            limit_type=limit_type,
            fields='trade_date,ts_code,name,close,pct_chg,amp,fc_ratio,fl_ratio,fd_amount,first_time,last_time,open_times,strth,limit'
        )
    
    def get_stk_holdernumber(self, ts_code: str) -> pd.DataFrame:
        """获取股东人数数据"""
        return self.pro.stk_holdernumber(
            ts_code=ts_code,
            fields='ts_code,ann_date,end_date,holder_num'
        )
    
    def get_top10_holders(self, ts_code: str, period: str) -> pd.DataFrame:
        """获取前十大股东"""
        return self.pro.top10_holders(
            ts_code=ts_code,
            period=period,
            fields='ts_code,ann_date,end_date,holder_name,hold_amount,hold_ratio'
        )
    
    def get_top10_floatholders(self, ts_code: str, period: str) -> pd.DataFrame:
        """获取前十大流通股东"""
        return self.pro.top10_floatholders(
            ts_code=ts_code,
            period=period,
            fields='ts_code,ann_date,end_date,holder_name,hold_amount,hold_ratio'
        )
    
    def get_block_trade(self, ts_code: str, start_date: str, end_date: str) -> pd.DataFrame:
        """获取大宗交易数据"""
        return self.pro.block_trade(
            ts_code=ts_code,
            start_date=start_date,
            end_date=end_date,
            fields='ts_code,trade_date,price,vol,amount,buyer,seller'
        )
    
    def get_stk_rewards(self, ts_code: str) -> pd.DataFrame:
        """获取管理层薪酬和持股"""
        return self.pro.stk_rewards(
            ts_code=ts_code,
            fields='ts_code,ann_date,end_date,name,title,reward,hold_vol'
        )
    
    def get_repurchase(self, ts_code: str) -> pd.DataFrame:
        """获取股票回购数据"""
        return self.pro.repurchase(
            ts_code=ts_code,
            fields='ts_code,ann_date,end_date,proc,exp_date,vol,amount,high_limit,low_limit'
        )
```

#### 6.2.2 AKshare 配置 (实时数据优先)
```python
# config/akshare_config.py
import akshare as ak
import pandas as pd
from typing import Optional, Dict, Any, List
from datetime import datetime, timedelta

class AkshareConfig:
    
    def get_realtime_data(self) -> pd.DataFrame:
        """获取A股实时行情数据 - 完整字段"""
        return ak.stock_zh_a_spot_em()
    
    def get_realtime_single(self, symbol: str) -> Dict[str, Any]:
        """获取单只股票实时数据 - 增强版"""
        try:
            # 获取实时价格 - 使用最新接口
            current_data = ak.stock_zh_a_hist(symbol=symbol, period="daily", start_date="20231201", end_date="20231215", adjust="")
            if not current_data.empty:
                latest = current_data.iloc[-1]
                return {
                    'symbol': symbol,
                    'name': self._get_stock_name(symbol),
                    'price': latest['收盘'],
                    'open': latest['开盘'],
                    'high': latest['最高'],
                    'low': latest['最低'],
                    'change': latest['涨跌额'],
                    'change_pct': latest['涨跌幅'],
                    'volume': latest['成交量'],
                    'amount': latest['成交额'],
                    'turnover': latest.get('换手率', 0),
                    'timestamp': latest['日期']
                }
        except Exception as e:
            print(f"获取 {symbol} 实时数据失败: {e}")
        return None
    
    def _get_stock_name(self, symbol: str) -> str:
        """获取股票名称"""
        try:
            stock_info = ak.stock_individual_info_em(symbol=symbol)
            return stock_info.get('股票简称', symbol)
        except:
            return symbol
    
    def get_stock_zh_a_hist_min_em(self, symbol: str, period: str = "1") -> pd.DataFrame:
        """获取A股分钟级别数据"""
        return ak.stock_zh_a_hist_min_em(symbol=symbol, period=period, adjust="")
    
    def get_stock_zh_a_hist_pre_min_em(self, symbol: str) -> pd.DataFrame:
        """获取A股盘前分钟数据"""
        return ak.stock_zh_a_hist_pre_min_em(symbol=symbol)
    
    def get_index_realtime(self) -> pd.DataFrame:
        """获取实时指数数据 - 完整版"""
        return ak.stock_zh_index_spot_em()
    
    def get_index_hist(self, symbol: str, period: str = "daily") -> pd.DataFrame:
        """获取指数历史数据"""
        return ak.stock_zh_index_daily_em(symbol=symbol, period=period)
    
    def get_fund_flow_realtime(self, symbol: str) -> Optional[pd.DataFrame]:
        """获取个股实时资金流向 - AKshare独有"""
        try:
            return ak.stock_individual_fund_flow_rank(symbol=symbol)
        except Exception as e:
            print(f"获取 {symbol} 资金流向失败: {e}")
            return None
    
    def get_fund_flow_concept(self) -> pd.DataFrame:
        """获取概念板块资金流向"""
        return ak.stock_fund_flow_concept()
    
    def get_fund_flow_industry(self) -> pd.DataFrame:
        """获取行业板块资金流向"""
        return ak.stock_fund_flow_industry()
    
    def get_fund_flow_big(self) -> pd.DataFrame:
        """获取大盘资金流向"""
        return ak.stock_fund_flow_big_deal()
    
    def get_hot_rank(self) -> pd.DataFrame:
        """获取热门股票排行 - 东方财富"""
        return ak.stock_hot_rank_em()
    
    def get_hot_rank_detail(self) -> pd.DataFrame:
        """获取热门股票详细排行"""
        return ak.stock_hot_rank_detail_em()
    
    def get_hot_rank_latest(self) -> pd.DataFrame:
        """获取最新热门股票"""
        return ak.stock_hot_rank_latest_em()
    
    def get_market_sentiment(self) -> Dict[str, Any]:
        """获取市场情绪指标 - 增强版"""
        try:
            today = datetime.now().strftime("%Y%m%d")
            
            # 涨跌停统计
            limit_up = ak.stock_zt_pool_em(date=today)
            limit_down = ak.stock_dt_pool_em(date=today)
            
            # 强势股池
            strong_pool = ak.stock_zt_pool_strong_em(date=today)
            
            # 次新股池
            sub_new_pool = ak.stock_zt_pool_sub_new_em(date=today)
            
            # 破板股池
            broken_pool = ak.stock_zt_pool_zbgc_em(date=today)
            
            return {
                'date': today,
                'limit_up_count': len(limit_up),
                'limit_down_count': len(limit_down),
                'strong_count': len(strong_pool),
                'sub_new_count': len(sub_new_pool),
                'broken_count': len(broken_pool),
                'market_sentiment': 'positive' if len(limit_up) > len(limit_down) else 'negative',
                'sentiment_score': (len(limit_up) - len(limit_down)) / max(1, len(limit_up) + len(limit_down))
            }
        except Exception as e:
            print(f"获取市场情绪数据失败: {e}")
            return {}
    
    def get_stock_comment_em(self) -> pd.DataFrame:
        """获取千股千评数据"""
        return ak.stock_comment_em()
    
    def get_stock_comment_detail_scrd_em(self, symbol: str) -> pd.DataFrame:
        """获取个股千股千评详情"""
        return ak.stock_comment_detail_scrd_em(symbol=symbol)
    
    def get_stock_board_concept_name_em(self) -> pd.DataFrame:
        """获取概念板块名称"""
        return ak.stock_board_concept_name_em()
    
    def get_stock_board_concept_cons_em(self, symbol: str) -> pd.DataFrame:
        """获取概念板块成分股"""
        return ak.stock_board_concept_cons_em(symbol=symbol)
    
    def get_stock_board_industry_name_em(self) -> pd.DataFrame:
        """获取行业板块名称"""
        return ak.stock_board_industry_name_em()
    
    def get_stock_board_industry_cons_em(self, symbol: str) -> pd.DataFrame:
        """获取行业板块成分股"""
        return ak.stock_board_industry_cons_em(symbol=symbol)
    
    def get_stock_lhb_detail_em(self, start_date: str, end_date: str) -> pd.DataFrame:
        """获取龙虎榜详情"""
        return ak.stock_lhb_detail_em(start_date=start_date, end_date=end_date)
    
    def get_stock_lhb_ggtj_em(self, symbol: str) -> pd.DataFrame:
        """获取个股龙虎榜统计"""
        return ak.stock_lhb_ggtj_em(symbol=symbol)
    
    def get_stock_lhb_jgzz_em(self, start_date: str, end_date: str) -> pd.DataFrame:
        """获取机构席位追踪"""
        return ak.stock_lhb_jgzz_em(start_date=start_date, end_date=end_date)
    
    def get_stock_dzjy_mrmx(self, start_date: str, end_date: str) -> pd.DataFrame:
        """获取大宗交易每日明细"""
        return ak.stock_dzjy_mrmx(start_date=start_date, end_date=end_date)
    
    def get_stock_dzjy_mrtj(self, start_date: str, end_date: str) -> pd.DataFrame:
        """获取大宗交易每日统计"""
        return ak.stock_dzjy_mrtj(start_date=start_date, end_date=end_date)
    
    def get_stock_margin_detail_em(self) -> pd.DataFrame:
        """获取融资融券详情"""
        return ak.stock_margin_detail_em()
    
    def get_stock_margin_underlying_info_em(self) -> pd.DataFrame:
        """获取融资融券标的信息"""
        return ak.stock_margin_underlying_info_em()
    
    def get_stock_repurchase_em(self) -> pd.DataFrame:
        """获取股票回购信息"""
        return ak.stock_repurchase_em()
    
    def get_stock_restricted_release_queue_em(self) -> pd.DataFrame:
        """获取限售解禁队列"""
        return ak.stock_restricted_release_queue_em()
    
    def get_stock_ipo_info(self) -> pd.DataFrame:
        """获取新股申购信息"""
        return ak.stock_ipo_info()
    
    def get_stock_new_a_em(self) -> pd.DataFrame:
        """获取新股数据"""
        return ak.stock_new_a_em()
    
    def get_stock_zh_a_gdhs(self, symbol: str) -> pd.DataFrame:
        """获取股东户数数据"""
        return ak.stock_zh_a_gdhs(symbol=symbol)
    
    def get_stock_financial_abstract_em(self, symbol: str) -> pd.DataFrame:
        """获取财务摘要数据"""
        return ak.stock_financial_abstract_em(symbol=symbol)
    
    def get_stock_financial_analysis_indicator(self, symbol: str) -> pd.DataFrame:
        """获取财务分析指标"""
        return ak.stock_financial_analysis_indicator(symbol=symbol)
    
    def get_stock_profit_forecast(self, symbol: str) -> pd.DataFrame:
        """获取盈利预测数据"""
        return ak.stock_profit_forecast(symbol=symbol)
    
    def get_stock_analyst_rank_em(self) -> pd.DataFrame:
        """获取分析师排名"""
        return ak.stock_analyst_rank_em()
    
    def get_stock_research_report_em(self, symbol: str) -> pd.DataFrame:
        """获取研究报告"""
        return ak.stock_research_report_em(symbol=symbol)
    
    def get_stock_news_em(self, symbol: str) -> pd.DataFrame:
        """获取个股新闻"""
        return ak.stock_news_em(symbol=symbol)
    
    def get_stock_notice_report(self, symbol: str) -> pd.DataFrame:
        """获取个股公告"""
        return ak.stock_notice_report(symbol=symbol)
    
    def get_macro_china_gdp(self) -> pd.DataFrame:
        """获取中国GDP数据"""
        return ak.macro_china_gdp()
    
    def get_macro_china_cpi(self) -> pd.DataFrame:
        """获取中国CPI数据"""
        return ak.macro_china_cpi()
    
    def get_macro_china_ppi(self) -> pd.DataFrame:
        """获取中国PPI数据"""
        return ak.macro_china_ppi()
    
    def get_macro_china_pmi(self) -> pd.DataFrame:
        """获取中国PMI数据"""
        return ak.macro_china_pmi()
    
    def get_currency_boc_safe(self) -> pd.DataFrame:
        """获取外汇牌价数据"""
        return ak.currency_boc_safe()
    
    def get_bond_zh_us_rate(self) -> pd.DataFrame:
        """获取中美国债收益率"""
        return ak.bond_zh_us_rate()
    
    def get_energy_oil_hist(self) -> pd.DataFrame:
        """获取原油历史数据"""
        return ak.energy_oil_hist()
    
    def get_futures_main_sina(self) -> pd.DataFrame:
        """获取期货主力合约数据"""
        return ak.futures_main_sina()
    
    def get_fund_etf_category_sina(self, symbol: str) -> pd.DataFrame:
        """获取ETF基金数据"""
        return ak.fund_etf_category_sina(symbol=symbol)
    
    def get_stock_us_spot_em(self) -> pd.DataFrame:
        """获取美股实时数据"""
        return ak.stock_us_spot_em()
    
    def get_stock_hk_spot_em(self) -> pd.DataFrame:
        """获取港股实时数据"""
        return ak.stock_hk_spot_em()
    
    def get_crypto_spot_em(self) -> pd.DataFrame:
        """获取数字货币实时数据"""
        return ak.crypto_spot_em()
    
    def get_stock_sector_summary(self) -> Dict[str, pd.DataFrame]:
        """获取板块汇总数据"""
        try:
            return {
                'concept': ak.stock_board_concept_name_em(),
                'industry': ak.stock_board_industry_name_em(),
                'area': ak.stock_board_area_name_em() if hasattr(ak, 'stock_board_area_name_em') else pd.DataFrame()
            }
        except Exception as e:
            print(f"获取板块数据失败: {e}")
            return {}
    
    def get_market_overview(self) -> Dict[str, Any]:
        """获取市场概览数据"""
        try:
            # 获取主要指数
            indices = ak.stock_zh_index_spot_em()
            
            # 获取涨跌分布
            up_down = ak.stock_zh_a_spot_em()
            up_count = len(up_down[up_down['涨跌幅'] > 0])
            down_count = len(up_down[up_down['涨跌幅'] < 0])
            flat_count = len(up_down[up_down['涨跌幅'] == 0])
            
            return {
                'indices': indices.head(10).to_dict('records'),
                'up_count': up_count,
                'down_count': down_count,
                'flat_count': flat_count,
                'total_count': len(up_down),
                'up_ratio': up_count / len(up_down) if len(up_down) > 0 else 0
            }
        except Exception as e:
            print(f"获取市场概览失败: {e}")
            return {}
```

#### 6.2.3 数据源统一接口
```python
# services/unified_data_service.py
from config.tushare_config import TushareConfig
from config.akshare_config import AkshareConfig
from services.data_source_manager import DataSourceManager, DataType
import pandas as pd
from typing import Optional, Dict, Any, List
import asyncio
from datetime import datetime, timedelta

class UnifiedDataService:
    def __init__(self, tushare_token: str):
        self.tushare = TushareConfig(tushare_token)
        self.akshare = AkshareConfig()
        self.data_manager = DataSourceManager()
    
    # ==================== 基础数据获取 ====================
    
    async def get_historical_data(self, symbol: str, start_date: str, end_date: str) -> Optional[pd.DataFrame]:
        """
        获取历史数据 - 优先使用TUshare
        """
        return await self.data_manager.get_data_with_fallback(
            DataType.HISTORICAL,
            symbol=symbol,
            start_date=start_date,
            end_date=end_date
        )
    
    async def get_realtime_data(self, symbol: Optional[str] = None) -> Optional[Dict[str, Any]]:
        """
        获取实时数据 - 优先使用AKshare
        """
        return await self.data_manager.get_data_with_fallback(
            DataType.REALTIME,
            symbol=symbol
        )
    
    async def get_daily_basic_data(self, symbol: str, start_date: str, end_date: str) -> Optional[pd.DataFrame]:
        """
        获取每日基本面数据 - TUshare Pro专业数据
        """
        try:
            return self.tushare.get_daily_basic(symbol, start_date, end_date)
        except Exception as e:
            print(f"获取每日基本面数据失败: {e}")
            return None
    
    async def get_moneyflow_data(self, symbol: str, start_date: str, end_date: str) -> Optional[pd.DataFrame]:
        """
        获取资金流向数据 - 优先TUshare，备用AKshare
        """
        try:
            # 优先使用TUshare专业资金流向数据
            return self.tushare.get_moneyflow(symbol, start_date, end_date)
        except Exception as e:
            print(f"TUshare资金流向获取失败，切换到AKshare: {e}")
            try:
                return self.akshare.get_fund_flow_realtime(symbol)
            except Exception as e2:
                print(f"AKshare资金流向获取失败: {e2}")
                return None
    
    # ==================== 财务数据获取 ====================
    
    async def get_financial_data(self, symbol: str, period: str) -> Optional[Dict[str, pd.DataFrame]]:
        """
        获取完整财务数据 - 强制使用TUshare (专业优势)
        """
        try:
            return {
                'income': self.tushare.get_income_statement(symbol, period),
                'balance': self.tushare.get_balance_sheet(symbol, period),
                'cashflow': self.tushare.get_cashflow(symbol, period),
                'indicators': self.tushare.get_fina_indicator(symbol, period)
            }
        except Exception as e:
            print(f"获取财务数据失败: {e}")
            return None
    
    async def get_dividend_data(self, symbol: str) -> Optional[pd.DataFrame]:
        """
        获取分红送股数据 - TUshare专业数据
        """
        try:
            return self.tushare.get_dividend(symbol)
        except Exception as e:
            print(f"获取分红数据失败: {e}")
            return None
    
    async def get_forecast_data(self, symbol: str, period: str) -> Optional[Dict[str, pd.DataFrame]]:
        """
        获取业绩预告和快报数据 - TUshare专业数据
        """
        try:
            return {
                'forecast': self.tushare.get_forecast(symbol, period),
                'express': self.tushare.get_express(symbol, period)
            }
        except Exception as e:
            print(f"获取业绩预告数据失败: {e}")
            return None
    
    # ==================== 实时数据获取 ====================
    
    async def get_fund_flow(self, symbol: str) -> Optional[Dict[str, pd.DataFrame]]:
        """
        获取资金流向 - 强制使用AKshare (独有功能)
        """
        try:
            return {
                'individual': self.akshare.get_fund_flow_realtime(symbol),
                'concept': self.akshare.get_fund_flow_concept(),
                'industry': self.akshare.get_fund_flow_industry(),
                'big_deal': self.akshare.get_fund_flow_big()
            }
        except Exception as e:
            print(f"获取资金流向失败: {e}")
            return None
    
    async def get_market_sentiment(self) -> Optional[Dict[str, Any]]:
        """
        获取市场情绪数据 - AKshare实时优势
        """
        try:
            return self.akshare.get_market_sentiment()
        except Exception as e:
            print(f"获取市场情绪失败: {e}")
            return None
    
    async def get_hot_stocks(self) -> Optional[Dict[str, pd.DataFrame]]:
        """
        获取热门股票数据 - AKshare实时数据
        """
        try:
            return {
                'hot_rank': self.akshare.get_hot_rank(),
                'hot_detail': self.akshare.get_hot_rank_detail(),
                'hot_latest': self.akshare.get_hot_rank_latest()
            }
        except Exception as e:
            print(f"获取热门股票失败: {e}")
            return None
    
    # ==================== 板块数据获取 ====================
    
    async def get_sector_data(self) -> Optional[Dict[str, pd.DataFrame]]:
        """
        获取板块数据 - AKshare丰富数据
        """
        try:
            return {
                'concept_names': self.akshare.get_stock_board_concept_name_em(),
                'industry_names': self.akshare.get_stock_board_industry_name_em(),
                'sector_summary': self.akshare.get_stock_sector_summary()
            }
        except Exception as e:
            print(f"获取板块数据失败: {e}")
            return None
    
    async def get_concept_stocks(self, concept_code: str) -> Optional[pd.DataFrame]:
        """
        获取概念股成分 - 使用 AKshare (Tushare concept 接口需要5000积分)
        """
        try:
            # 使用 AKshare 获取概念股成分
            return self.akshare.get_stock_board_concept_cons_em(concept_code)
        except Exception as e:
            print(f"AKshare概念股获取失败: {e}")
            return None
    
    # ==================== 龙虎榜和大宗交易 ====================
    
    async def get_lhb_data(self, start_date: str, end_date: str, symbol: str = None) -> Optional[Dict[str, pd.DataFrame]]:
        """
        获取龙虎榜数据 - AKshare独有
        """
        try:
            result = {
                'detail': self.akshare.get_stock_lhb_detail_em(start_date, end_date),
                'institution': self.akshare.get_stock_lhb_jgzz_em(start_date, end_date)
            }
            if symbol:
                result['individual'] = self.akshare.get_stock_lhb_ggtj_em(symbol)
            return result
        except Exception as e:
            print(f"获取龙虎榜数据失败: {e}")
            return None
    
    async def get_block_trade_data(self, start_date: str, end_date: str, symbol: str = None) -> Optional[Dict[str, pd.DataFrame]]:
        """
        获取大宗交易数据 - 双数据源
        """
        try:
            result = {}
            
            # TUshare大宗交易数据
            if symbol:
                result['tushare'] = self.tushare.get_block_trade(symbol, start_date, end_date)
            
            # AKshare大宗交易数据
            result['akshare_detail'] = self.akshare.get_stock_dzjy_mrmx(start_date, end_date)
            result['akshare_summary'] = self.akshare.get_stock_dzjy_mrtj(start_date, end_date)
            
            return result
        except Exception as e:
            print(f"获取大宗交易数据失败: {e}")
            return None
    
    # ==================== 股东和治理数据 ====================
    
    async def get_shareholder_data(self, symbol: str, period: str = None) -> Optional[Dict[str, pd.DataFrame]]:
        """
        获取股东数据 - 双数据源互补
        """
        try:
            result = {}
            
            # TUshare股东数据
            if period:
                result['top10_holders'] = self.tushare.get_top10_holders(symbol, period)
                result['top10_float_holders'] = self.tushare.get_top10_floatholders(symbol, period)
            
            result['holder_number'] = self.tushare.get_stk_holdernumber(symbol)
            result['rewards'] = self.tushare.get_stk_rewards(symbol)
            
            # AKshare股东户数
            result['akshare_gdhs'] = self.akshare.get_stock_zh_a_gdhs(symbol)
            
            return result
        except Exception as e:
            print(f"获取股东数据失败: {e}")
            return None
    
    # ==================== 新股和特殊事件 ====================
    
    async def get_ipo_data(self) -> Optional[Dict[str, pd.DataFrame]]:
        """
        获取新股数据 - AKshare实时优势
        """
        try:
            return {
                'ipo_info': self.akshare.get_stock_ipo_info(),
                'new_stocks': self.akshare.get_stock_new_a_em()
            }
        except Exception as e:
            print(f"获取新股数据失败: {e}")
            return None
    
    async def get_margin_data(self) -> Optional[Dict[str, pd.DataFrame]]:
        """
        获取融资融券数据 - AKshare独有
        """
        try:
            return {
                'detail': self.akshare.get_stock_margin_detail_em(),
                'underlying': self.akshare.get_stock_margin_underlying_info_em()
            }
        except Exception as e:
            print(f"获取融资融券数据失败: {e}")
            return None
    
    async def get_repurchase_data(self, symbol: str = None) -> Optional[Dict[str, pd.DataFrame]]:
        """
        获取股票回购数据 - 双数据源
        """
        try:
            result = {}
            
            # TUshare回购数据
            if symbol:
                result['tushare'] = self.tushare.get_repurchase(symbol)
            
            # AKshare回购数据
            result['akshare'] = self.akshare.get_stock_repurchase_em()
            
            return result
        except Exception as e:
            print(f"获取回购数据失败: {e}")
            return None
    
    # ==================== 研究和分析数据 ====================
    
    async def get_research_data(self, symbol: str) -> Optional[Dict[str, pd.DataFrame]]:
        """
        获取研究分析数据 - AKshare丰富内容
        """
        try:
            return {
                'comment': self.akshare.get_stock_comment_detail_scrd_em(symbol),
                'profit_forecast': self.akshare.get_stock_profit_forecast(symbol),
                'research_report': self.akshare.get_stock_research_report_em(symbol),
                'analyst_rank': self.akshare.get_stock_analyst_rank_em()
            }
        except Exception as e:
            print(f"获取研究数据失败: {e}")
            return None
    
    async def get_news_data(self, symbol: str) -> Optional[Dict[str, pd.DataFrame]]:
        """
        获取新闻公告数据 - AKshare实时内容
        """
        try:
            return {
                'news': self.akshare.get_stock_news_em(symbol),
                'notice': self.akshare.get_stock_notice_report(symbol)
            }
        except Exception as e:
            print(f"获取新闻数据失败: {e}")
            return None
    
    # ==================== 宏观经济数据 ====================
    
    async def get_macro_data(self) -> Optional[Dict[str, pd.DataFrame]]:
        """
        获取宏观经济数据 - AKshare丰富数据
        """
        try:
            return {
                'gdp': self.akshare.get_macro_china_gdp(),
                'cpi': self.akshare.get_macro_china_cpi(),
                'ppi': self.akshare.get_macro_china_ppi(),
                'pmi': self.akshare.get_macro_china_pmi()
            }
        except Exception as e:
            print(f"获取宏观数据失败: {e}")
            return None
    
    # ==================== 限售股解禁数据 ====================
    
    async def get_restricted_release_data(self) -> Optional[Dict[str, pd.DataFrame]]:
        """
        获取限售股解禁数据 - 使用 AKshare (Tushare share_float 接口需要3000积分)
        """
        try:
            return {
                'release_queue': self.akshare.get_stock_restricted_release_queue_sina(),
                'release_summary': self.akshare.get_stock_restricted_release_summary_em()
            }
        except Exception as e:
            print(f"获取限售股解禁数据失败: {e}")
            return None

    # ==================== 跨市场数据 ====================
    
    async def get_cross_market_data(self) -> Optional[Dict[str, pd.DataFrame]]:
        """
        获取跨市场数据 - AKshare全球数据
        """
        try:
            return {
                'us_stocks': self.akshare.get_stock_us_spot_em(),
                'hk_stocks': self.akshare.get_stock_hk_spot_em(),
                'crypto': self.akshare.get_crypto_spot_em(),
                'currency': self.akshare.get_currency_boc_safe(),
                'bond': self.akshare.get_bond_zh_us_rate(),
                'oil': self.akshare.get_energy_oil_hist(),
                'futures': self.akshare.get_futures_main_sina()
            }
        except Exception as e:
            print(f"获取跨市场数据失败: {e}")
            return None
    
    # ==================== 综合数据获取 ====================
    
    async def get_comprehensive_stock_data(self, symbol: str, period: str = "20231201", end_period: str = "20231215") -> Optional[Dict[str, Any]]:
        """
        获取股票综合数据 - 一次性获取所有相关数据
        """
        try:
            tasks = [
                self.get_historical_data(symbol, period, end_period),
                self.get_realtime_data(symbol),
                self.get_daily_basic_data(symbol, period, end_period),
                self.get_moneyflow_data(symbol, period, end_period),
                self.get_financial_data(symbol, period[:4]),  # 年度财务数据
                self.get_dividend_data(symbol),
                self.get_shareholder_data(symbol, period[:4]),
                self.get_research_data(symbol),
                self.get_news_data(symbol)
            ]
            
            results = await asyncio.gather(*tasks, return_exceptions=True)
            
            return {
                'historical': results[0] if not isinstance(results[0], Exception) else None,
                'realtime': results[1] if not isinstance(results[1], Exception) else None,
                'daily_basic': results[2] if not isinstance(results[2], Exception) else None,
                'moneyflow': results[3] if not isinstance(results[3], Exception) else None,
                'financial': results[4] if not isinstance(results[4], Exception) else None,
                'dividend': results[5] if not isinstance(results[5], Exception) else None,
                'shareholder': results[6] if not isinstance(results[6], Exception) else None,
                'research': results[7] if not isinstance(results[7], Exception) else None,
                'news': results[8] if not isinstance(results[8], Exception) else None
            }
        except Exception as e:
            print(f"获取综合数据失败: {e}")
            return None
    
    async def get_market_overview_comprehensive(self) -> Optional[Dict[str, Any]]:
        """
        获取市场综合概览 - 全方位市场数据
        """
        try:
            tasks = [
                self.get_market_sentiment(),
                self.get_hot_stocks(),
                self.get_sector_data(),
                self.get_ipo_data(),
                self.get_margin_data(),
                self.get_macro_data(),
                self.akshare.get_market_overview()
            ]
            
            results = await asyncio.gather(*tasks, return_exceptions=True)
            
            return {
                'sentiment': results[0] if not isinstance(results[0], Exception) else None,
                'hot_stocks': results[1] if not isinstance(results[1], Exception) else None,
                'sectors': results[2] if not isinstance(results[2], Exception) else None,
                'ipo': results[3] if not isinstance(results[3], Exception) else None,
                'margin': results[4] if not isinstance(results[4], Exception) else None,
                'macro': results[5] if not isinstance(results[5], Exception) else None,
                'overview': results[6] if not isinstance(results[6], Exception) else None
            }
        except Exception as e:
            print(f"获取市场概览失败: {e}")
            return None
```

### 6.2 数据处理服务

#### 6.2.1 技术指标计算
```python
# services/technical_analysis.py
import pandas as pd
import talib

class TechnicalAnalysis:
    
    def calculate_macd(self, close_prices):
        """计算MACD指标"""
        dif, dea, histogram = talib.MACD(close_prices)
        return {
            'dif': dif,
            'dea': dea,
            'histogram': histogram
        }
    
    def calculate_kdj(self, high_prices, low_prices, close_prices):
        """计算KDJ指标"""
        k, d = talib.STOCH(high_prices, low_prices, close_prices)
        j = 3 * k - 2 * d
        return {
            'k': k,
            'd': d,
            'j': j
        }
    
    def calculate_rsi(self, close_prices, periods=[6, 12, 24]):
        """计算RSI指标"""
        rsi_values = {}
        for period in periods:
            rsi_values[f'rsi_{period}'] = talib.RSI(close_prices, timeperiod=period)
        return rsi_values
```

#### 6.2.2 九转指标计算
```python
# services/nine_turn.py
import pandas as pd

class NineTurnAnalysis:
    
    def calculate_setup(self, df):
        """计算九转设置"""
        df['setup_buy'] = 0
        df['setup_sell'] = 0
        
        # 买入设置：收盘价低于4个交易日前的收盘价
        for i in range(4, len(df)):
            if df.iloc[i]['close'] < df.iloc[i-4]['close']:
                if i > 0 and df.iloc[i-1]['setup_buy'] > 0:
                    df.iloc[i, df.columns.get_loc('setup_buy')] = df.iloc[i-1]['setup_buy'] + 1
                else:
                    df.iloc[i, df.columns.get_loc('setup_buy')] = 1
        
        # 卖出设置：收盘价高于4个交易日前的收盘价
        for i in range(4, len(df)):
            if df.iloc[i]['close'] > df.iloc[i-4]['close']:
                if i > 0 and df.iloc[i-1]['setup_sell'] > 0:
                    df.iloc[i, df.columns.get_loc('setup_sell')] = df.iloc[i-1]['setup_sell'] + 1
                else:
                    df.iloc[i, df.columns.get_loc('setup_sell')] = 1
        
        return df
    
    def find_signals(self, df):
        """查找九转信号"""
        signals = []
        
        # 查找买入信号（设置达到9）
        buy_signals = df[df['setup_buy'] == 9]
        for _, row in buy_signals.iterrows():
            signals.append({
                'date': row['trade_date'],
                'type': 'buy_setup',
                'value': 9,
                'price': row['close']
            })
        
        # 查找卖出信号（设置达到9）
        sell_signals = df[df['setup_sell'] == 9]
        for _, row in sell_signals.iterrows():
            signals.append({
                'date': row['trade_date'],
                'type': 'sell_setup',
                'value': 9,
                'price': row['close']
            })
        
        return signals
```

## 7. 定时任务设计

### 7.0 24小时运行架构设计

#### 7.0.1 系统运行环境
- **部署环境**: Ubuntu Server 22.04 LTS 云服务器
- **运行模式**: 24小时不间断运行
- **容器化**: Docker + Docker Compose 部署
- **进程管理**: Supervisor + Systemd 双重保障
- **监控告警**: Prometheus + Grafana + AlertManager

#### 7.0.2 A股交易日自动化流程

**09:30 - 实时数据同步启动**
```python
# tasks/realtime_data_sync.py
@app.task(bind=True, queue='realtime', priority=10)
def start_realtime_data_sync(self):
    """
    A股开盘时启动实时数据同步
    - 启动AKShare实时行情获取
    - 数据缓存到Redis
    - WebSocket推送到前端
    """
    logger.info("A股开盘，启动实时数据同步...")
    
    # 启动实时行情数据获取
    realtime_quotes_task.apply_async(queue='realtime')
    
    # 启动资金流向数据获取
    fund_flow_task.apply_async(queue='realtime')
    
    # 启动技术指标实时计算
    realtime_indicators_task.apply_async(queue='analysis')
    
    logger.info("实时数据同步已启动")
```

**15:00 - 交易结束数据处理**
```python
# tasks/end_of_day_processing.py
@app.task(bind=True, queue='data_migration', priority=9)
def end_of_day_data_processing(self):
    """
    交易结束后的数据处理流程
    - 停止实时数据获取
    - Redis数据迁移到PostgreSQL
    - 数据完整性检查
    - 触发九转选股算法
    """
    logger.info("交易结束，开始数据处理...")
    
    # 1. 停止实时数据获取任务
    stop_realtime_tasks()
    
    # 2. Redis → PostgreSQL 数据迁移
    migrate_redis_to_postgresql.apply_async(queue='data_migration')
    
    # 3. 数据完整性检查
    data_integrity_check.apply_async(queue='maintenance')
    
    # 4. 等待数据迁移完成后触发九转选股
    chain(
        migrate_redis_to_postgresql.s(),
        nine_turn_stock_selection.s()
    ).apply_async()
    
    logger.info("数据处理流程已启动")

@app.task(bind=True, queue='data_migration', priority=8)
def migrate_redis_to_postgresql(self):
    """
    Redis数据迁移到PostgreSQL
    采用批量插入优化性能
    """
    logger.info("开始Redis数据迁移...")
    
    # 获取当日Redis中的所有数据
    redis_client = get_redis_client()
    today = datetime.now().strftime('%Y%m%d')
    
    # 批量迁移股票行情数据
    stock_data = redis_client.hgetall(f"stock_quotes:{today}")
    if stock_data:
        batch_insert_stock_daily(stock_data)
    
    # 批量迁移资金流向数据
    flow_data = redis_client.hgetall(f"money_flow:{today}")
    if flow_data:
        batch_insert_money_flow(flow_data)
    
    # 批量迁移技术指标数据
    indicator_data = redis_client.hgetall(f"indicators:{today}")
    if indicator_data:
        batch_insert_technical_indicators(indicator_data)
    
    # 数据迁移完成后清理Redis
    cleanup_redis_data(today)
    
    logger.info("Redis数据迁移完成")
    return {"status": "success", "date": today}
```

**16:00 - 九转系列选股自动执行**
```python
# tasks/nine_turn_selection.py
@app.task(bind=True, queue='analysis', priority=9)
def nine_turn_stock_selection(self, migration_result=None):
    """
    九转系列选股算法自动执行
    - 获取当日完整数据
    - 计算九转买入/卖出信号
    - 更新选股结果表
    - 生成选股报告
    """
    logger.info("开始执行九转系列选股算法...")
    
    today = datetime.now().strftime('%Y-%m-%d')
    
    # 1. 获取所有股票代码
    stock_codes = get_all_stock_codes()
    
    # 2. 并行计算九转信号
    selection_results = []
    
    # 分批处理，避免内存溢出
    batch_size = 100
    for i in range(0, len(stock_codes), batch_size):
        batch_codes = stock_codes[i:i+batch_size]
        
        # 并行计算当前批次的九转信号
        batch_results = group(
            calculate_nine_turn_signals.s(code) for code in batch_codes
        ).apply_async()
        
        selection_results.extend(batch_results.get())
    
    # 3. 筛选出有效信号
    buy_signals = [r for r in selection_results if r.get('buy_signal')]
    sell_signals = [r for r in selection_results if r.get('sell_signal')]
    
    # 4. 保存选股结果到数据库
    save_nine_turn_results(buy_signals, sell_signals, today)
    
    # 5. 生成选股报告
    generate_selection_report(buy_signals, sell_signals, today)
    
    # 6. 发送通知
    send_selection_notification(len(buy_signals), len(sell_signals))
    
    logger.info(f"九转选股完成: 买入信号{len(buy_signals)}个, 卖出信号{len(sell_signals)}个")
    
    return {
        "date": today,
        "buy_signals_count": len(buy_signals),
        "sell_signals_count": len(sell_signals)
    }

@app.task(bind=True, queue='analysis', priority=8)
def calculate_nine_turn_signals(self, stock_code):
    """
    计算单个股票的九转信号
    """
    try:
        # 获取股票历史数据（最近30个交易日）
        df = get_stock_history_data(stock_code, days=30)
        
        if df.empty or len(df) < 20:
            return {"stock_code": stock_code, "error": "数据不足"}
        
        # 计算九转买入信号
        buy_setup = calculate_buy_setup(df)
        buy_countdown = calculate_buy_countdown(df)
        
        # 计算九转卖出信号
        sell_setup = calculate_sell_setup(df)
        sell_countdown = calculate_sell_countdown(df)
        
        result = {
            "stock_code": stock_code,
            "buy_signal": buy_setup or buy_countdown,
            "sell_signal": sell_setup or sell_countdown,
            "buy_setup_value": buy_setup.get('value') if buy_setup else None,
            "buy_countdown_value": buy_countdown.get('value') if buy_countdown else None,
            "sell_setup_value": sell_setup.get('value') if sell_setup else None,
            "sell_countdown_value": sell_countdown.get('value') if sell_countdown else None,
            "current_price": df.iloc[-1]['close'],
            "signal_date": datetime.now().strftime('%Y-%m-%d')
        }
        
        return result
        
    except Exception as e:
        logger.error(f"计算{stock_code}九转信号失败: {e}")
        return {"stock_code": stock_code, "error": str(e)}
```

**17:00 - 数据清理与系统维护**
```python
# tasks/system_maintenance.py
@app.task(bind=True, queue='maintenance', priority=7)
def daily_system_maintenance(self):
    """
    每日系统维护任务
    - 清理Redis临时数据
    - 数据库索引优化
    - 日志文件归档
    - 系统健康检查
    """
    logger.info("开始每日系统维护...")
    
    # 1. 清理Redis临时数据（保留最近3天）
    cleanup_old_redis_data(days=3)
    
    # 2. 数据库维护
    optimize_database_indexes()
    vacuum_database_tables()
    
    # 3. 日志文件归档
    archive_log_files()
    
    # 4. 系统健康检查
    health_check_result = perform_system_health_check()
    
    # 5. 生成维护报告
    generate_maintenance_report(health_check_result)
    
    logger.info("每日系统维护完成")
    
    return health_check_result
```

```python
# monitoring/system_monitor.py
@app.task(bind=True, queue='monitoring', priority=6)
def system_health_monitor(self):
    """
    系统健康监控
    每5分钟执行一次
    """
    metrics = {
        "cpu_usage": get_cpu_usage(),
        "memory_usage": get_memory_usage(),
        "disk_usage": get_disk_usage(),
        "database_connections": get_db_connections(),
        "redis_memory": get_redis_memory_usage(),
        "api_response_time": get_api_response_time(),
        "data_sync_status": get_data_sync_status()
    }
    
    # 检查告警阈值
    alerts = check_alert_thresholds(metrics)
    
    if alerts:
        send_alert_notifications(alerts)
    
    # 记录监控数据
    record_monitoring_metrics(metrics)
    
    return metrics
```

### 7.1 全面数据更新任务配置

#### 7.1.1 定时任务调度配置
```python
# tasks/scheduled_tasks.py
from celery import Celery
from celery.schedules import crontab

app = Celery('stock_system')

# 配置定时任务
app.conf.beat_schedule = {
    # ==================== 24小时运行核心任务 ====================
    
    # A股开盘实时数据同步启动 (交易日上午9:30)
    'start-realtime-data-sync': {
        'task': 'tasks.start_realtime_data_sync',
        'schedule': crontab(hour=9, minute=30, day_of_week='1-5'),
        'options': {'queue': 'realtime', 'priority': 10}
    },
    
    # 交易结束数据处理 (交易日下午3:00)
    'end-of-day-processing': {
        'task': 'tasks.end_of_day_data_processing',
        'schedule': crontab(hour=15, minute=0, day_of_week='1-5'),
        'options': {'queue': 'data_migration', 'priority': 9}
    },
    
    # 九转系列选股自动执行 (交易日下午4:00)
    'nine-turn-stock-selection': {
        'task': 'tasks.nine_turn_stock_selection',
        'schedule': crontab(hour=16, minute=0, day_of_week='1-5'),
        'options': {'queue': 'analysis', 'priority': 9}
    },
    
    # 每日系统维护 (交易日下午5:00)
    'daily-system-maintenance': {
        'task': 'tasks.daily_system_maintenance',
        'schedule': crontab(hour=17, minute=0, day_of_week='1-5'),
        'options': {'queue': 'maintenance', 'priority': 7}
    },
    
    # 系统健康监控 (每5分钟)
    'system-health-monitor': {
        'task': 'tasks.system_health_monitor',
        'schedule': crontab(minute='*/5'),
        'options': {'queue': 'monitoring', 'priority': 6}
    },

#### 7.1.2 历史数据更新任务 - 优先TUshare
```python
# tasks/daily_update.py
from celery import current_app
from services.unified_data_service import UnifiedDataService
from services.data_source_manager import DataType
from utils.retry_decorator import retry_with_fallback
import asyncio
import logging
from datetime import datetime, timedelta

logger = logging.getLogger(__name__)

@current_app.task(bind=True, name='tasks.update_daily_historical_data')
@retry_with_fallback(max_retries=3, countdown=120)
async def update_daily_historical_data(self):
    """更新每日历史行情数据 - 优先使用TUshare"""
    try:
        logger.info("开始更新每日历史行情数据")
        
        data_service = UnifiedDataService(tushare_token="your_token")
        
        # 获取所有股票代码
        stock_codes = await data_service.get_all_stock_codes()
        
        today = datetime.now().strftime('%Y%m%d')
        yesterday = (datetime.now() - timedelta(days=1)).strftime('%Y%m%d')
        
        success_count = 0
        fail_count = 0
        
        for code in stock_codes:
            try:
                # 使用统一接口获取历史数据 (自动优先TUshare)
                daily_data = await data_service.get_historical_data(
                    symbol=code,
                    start_date=yesterday,
                    end_date=today
                )
                
                if daily_data is not None and not daily_data.empty:
                    # 保存到数据库
                    await data_service.save_daily_data(daily_data)
                    success_count += 1
                else:
                    fail_count += 1
                    logger.warning(f"股票 {code} 历史数据获取失败")
                    
            except Exception as e:
                fail_count += 1
                logger.error(f"更新股票 {code} 数据失败: {e}")
        
        logger.info(f"历史数据更新完成: 成功 {success_count}, 失败 {fail_count}")
        return {"status": "success", "success_count": success_count, "fail_count": fail_count}
        
    except Exception as e:
        logger.error(f"更新历史数据失败: {e}")
        raise self.retry(exc=e)

@current_app.task(bind=True, name='tasks.update_financial_statements')
@retry_with_fallback(max_retries=3, countdown=300)
async def update_financial_statements(self):
    """更新财务报表数据 - 强制使用TUshare"""
    try:
        logger.info("开始更新财务报表数据")
        
        data_service = UnifiedDataService(tushare_token="your_token")
        stock_codes = await data_service.get_all_stock_codes()
        
        current_year = datetime.now().year
        success_count = 0
        
        for code in stock_codes:
            try:
                # 强制使用TUshare获取财务数据
                financial_data = await data_service.get_financial_data(code, str(current_year))
                if financial_data is not None:
                    await data_service.save_financial_data(financial_data)
                    success_count += 1
            except Exception as e:
                logger.error(f"更新股票 {code} 财务数据失败: {e}")
        
        logger.info(f"财务报表数据更新完成，成功处理 {success_count} 只股票")
        return {"status": "success", "count": success_count}
        
    except Exception as e:
        logger.error(f"更新财务报表数据失败: {e}")
        raise self.retry(exc=e)

@current_app.task(bind=True, name='tasks.update_nine_turn_signals')
@retry_with_fallback(max_retries=2, countdown=60)
async def update_nine_turn_signals(self):
    """更新九转信号 - 基于历史数据(TUshare优先)"""
    try:
        logger.info("开始更新九转信号")
        
        data_service = UnifiedDataService(tushare_token="your_token")
        nine_turn = NineTurnAnalysis()
        
        stock_codes = await data_service.get_all_stock_codes()
        success_count = 0
        
        for code in stock_codes:
            try:
                # 获取历史数据用于九转计算
                df = await data_service.get_historical_data(
                    symbol=code,
                    start_date="20240101",
                    end_date="20241231"
                )
                
                if df is not None and not df.empty:
                    # 计算九转指标
                    df = nine_turn.calculate_setup(df)
                    signals = nine_turn.find_signals(df)
                    
                    # 保存信号
                    await data_service.save_nine_turn_signals(code, signals)
                    success_count += 1
                
            except Exception as e:
                logger.error(f"更新股票 {code} 九转信号失败: {e}")
        
        logger.info(f"九转信号更新完成，成功处理 {success_count} 只股票")
        return {"status": "success", "count": success_count}
        
    except Exception as e:
        logger.error(f"更新九转信号失败: {e}")
        raise self.retry(exc=e)
```

#### 7.1.3 实时数据更新任务 - 优先AKshare
```python
# tasks/realtime_update.py
@current_app.task(bind=True, name='tasks.update_realtime_quotes')
@retry_with_fallback(max_retries=2, countdown=30)
async def update_realtime_quotes(self):
    """更新实时数据 - 优先使用AKshare"""
    if not is_trading_time():
        return {"status": "not_trading_time"}
    
    try:
        logger.info("开始更新实时行情数据")
        
        data_service = UnifiedDataService(tushare_token="your_token")
        
        # 使用统一接口获取实时行情 (自动优先AKshare)
        realtime_data = await data_service.get_realtime_data()
        
        if realtime_data is not None:
            # 缓存到Redis
            await data_service.cache_realtime_data(realtime_data)
            
            # 推送到前端
            await websocket_service.broadcast_realtime_data(realtime_data)
            
            logger.info("实时数据更新成功")
            return {"status": "success", "data_count": len(realtime_data)}
        else:
            logger.warning("实时数据获取失败，所有数据源都不可用")
            return {"status": "no_data"}
        
    except Exception as e:
        logger.error(f"更新实时数据失败: {e}")
        raise self.retry(exc=e)

@current_app.task(bind=True, name='tasks.update_fund_flow_data')
@retry_with_fallback(max_retries=2, countdown=60)
async def update_fund_flow_data(self):
    """更新资金流向数据 - 强制使用AKshare"""
    if not is_trading_time():
        return {"status": "not_trading_time"}
    
    try:
        logger.info("开始更新资金流向数据")
        
        data_service = UnifiedDataService(tushare_token="your_token")
        
        # 获取热门股票列表
        hot_stocks = await data_service.get_hot_stocks()
        success_count = 0
        
        if hot_stocks and 'hot_rank' in hot_stocks:
            stock_codes = hot_stocks['hot_rank']['symbol'].tolist()[:50]  # 取前50只热门股票
            
            for stock_code in stock_codes:
                try:
                    # 强制使用AKshare获取资金流向
                    fund_flow = await data_service.get_fund_flow(stock_code)
                    if fund_flow is not None:
                        await data_service.cache_fund_flow(stock_code, fund_flow)
                        success_count += 1
                except Exception as e:
                    logger.warning(f"更新股票 {stock_code} 资金流向失败: {e}")
        
        logger.info(f"资金流向数据更新完成，成功处理 {success_count} 只股票")
        return {"status": "success", "count": success_count}
        
    except Exception as e:
        logger.error(f"更新资金流向数据失败: {e}")
        raise self.retry(exc=e)

@current_app.task(bind=True, name='tasks.update_market_sentiment')
@retry_with_fallback(max_retries=2, countdown=30)
async def update_market_sentiment(self):
    """更新市场情绪数据 - 使用AKshare实时数据"""
    try:
        logger.info("开始更新市场情绪数据")
        
        data_service = UnifiedDataService(tushare_token="your_token")
        
        # 获取市场情绪指标
        sentiment_data = await data_service.get_market_sentiment()
        if sentiment_data:
            await data_service.cache_market_sentiment(sentiment_data)
            logger.info("市场情绪数据更新成功")
            return {"status": "success", "data": sentiment_data}
        else:
            logger.warning("市场情绪数据获取失败")
            return {"status": "no_data"}
            
    except Exception as e:
        logger.error(f"更新市场情绪数据失败: {e}")
        raise self.retry(exc=e)

def is_trading_time():
    """判断是否为交易时间"""
    import datetime
    now = datetime.datetime.now()
    
    # 周末不交易
    if now.weekday() >= 5:
        return False
    
    # 交易时间：9:30-11:30, 13:00-15:00
    morning_start = now.replace(hour=9, minute=30, second=0)
    morning_end = now.replace(hour=11, minute=30, second=0)
    afternoon_start = now.replace(hour=13, minute=0, second=0)
    afternoon_end = now.replace(hour=15, minute=0, second=0)
    
    return (morning_start <= now <= morning_end) or (afternoon_start <= now <= afternoon_end)
```

#### 7.1.4 财务和基本面数据更新任务
```python
# tasks/financial_update.py
@current_app.task(bind=True, name='tasks.update_daily_basic_data')
@retry_with_fallback(max_retries=3, countdown=180)
async def update_daily_basic_data(self):
    """更新每日基本面数据 - 使用TUshare"""
    try:
        logger.info("开始更新每日基本面数据")
        
        data_service = UnifiedDataService(tushare_token="your_token")
        today = datetime.now().strftime('%Y%m%d')
        
        # 获取每日基本面数据
        daily_basic = await data_service.get_daily_basic(trade_date=today)
        if daily_basic is not None:
            await data_service.save_daily_basic(daily_basic)
            
        # 获取资金流向数据
        moneyflow = await data_service.get_moneyflow(trade_date=today)
        if moneyflow is not None:
            await data_service.save_moneyflow(moneyflow)
            
        logger.info("每日基本面数据更新完成")
        return {"status": "success"}
        
    except Exception as e:
        logger.error(f"更新每日基本面数据失败: {e}")
        raise self.retry(exc=e)

@current_app.task(bind=True, name='tasks.update_financial_indicators')
@retry_with_fallback(max_retries=3, countdown=300)
async def update_financial_indicators(self):
    """更新财务指标数据"""
    try:
        logger.info("开始更新财务指标数据")
        
        data_service = UnifiedDataService(tushare_token="your_token")
        stock_codes = await data_service.get_all_stock_codes()
        
        current_year = datetime.now().year
        periods = [f"{current_year}1231", f"{current_year-1}1231"]
        
        success_count = 0
        for code in stock_codes:
            try:
                for period in periods:
                    indicators = await data_service.get_fina_indicator(ts_code=code, period=period)
                    if indicators is not None:
                        await data_service.save_financial_indicators(indicators)
                success_count += 1
            except Exception as e:
                logger.warning(f"更新股票 {code} 财务指标失败: {e}")
        
        logger.info(f"财务指标数据更新完成，成功处理 {success_count} 只股票")
        return {"status": "success", "count": success_count}
        
    except Exception as e:
        logger.error(f"更新财务指标数据失败: {e}")
        raise self.retry(exc=e)

@current_app.task(bind=True, name='tasks.update_dividend_data')
@retry_with_fallback(max_retries=2, countdown=120)
async def update_dividend_data(self):
    """更新分红送股数据"""
    try:
        logger.info("开始更新分红送股数据")
        
        data_service = UnifiedDataService(tushare_token="your_token")
        
        # 获取分红数据
        dividend_data = await data_service.get_dividend()
        if dividend_data is not None:
            await data_service.save_dividend_data(dividend_data)
            
        logger.info("分红送股数据更新完成")
        return {"status": "success"}
        
    except Exception as e:
        logger.error(f"更新分红送股数据失败: {e}")
        raise self.retry(exc=e)

@current_app.task(bind=True, name='tasks.update_forecast_data')
@retry_with_fallback(max_retries=2, countdown=120)
async def update_forecast_data(self):
    """更新业绩预告数据"""
    try:
        logger.info("开始更新业绩预告数据")
        
        data_service = UnifiedDataService(tushare_token="your_token")
        
        # 获取业绩预告和快报
        forecast_data = await data_service.get_forecast()
        if forecast_data is not None:
            await data_service.save_forecast_data(forecast_data)
            
        express_data = await data_service.get_express()
        if express_data is not None:
            await data_service.save_express_data(express_data)
            
        logger.info("业绩预告数据更新完成")
        return {"status": "success"}
        
    except Exception as e:
        logger.error(f"更新业绩预告数据失败: {e}")
        raise self.retry(exc=e)
```

#### 7.1.5 板块和概念数据更新任务
```python
# tasks/sector_update.py
@current_app.task(bind=True, name='tasks.update_sector_data')
@retry_with_fallback(max_retries=2, countdown=90)
async def update_sector_data(self):
    """更新板块数据"""
    try:
        logger.info("开始更新板块数据")
        
        data_service = UnifiedDataService(tushare_token="your_token")
        
        # 获取板块资金流向 (AKshare)
        sector_flow = await data_service.get_sector_fund_flow()
        if sector_flow is not None:
            await data_service.save_sector_flow(sector_flow)
            
        # 获取行业分类 (TUshare)
        industry_data = await data_service.get_industry_classify()
        if industry_data is not None:
            await data_service.save_industry_data(industry_data)
            
        logger.info("板块数据更新完成")
        return {"status": "success"}
        
    except Exception as e:
        logger.error(f"更新板块数据失败: {e}")
        raise self.retry(exc=e)

@current_app.task(bind=True, name='tasks.update_concept_stocks')
@retry_with_fallback(max_retries=2, countdown=120)
async def update_concept_stocks(self):
    """更新概念股成分 - 使用 AKshare (Tushare concept 接口需要5000积分)"""
    try:
        logger.info("开始更新概念股成分")
        
        data_service = UnifiedDataService(tushare_token="your_token")
        
        # 使用 AKshare 获取概念分类
        concepts = await data_service.akshare_service.get_stock_board_concept_name_em()
        if concepts is not None:
            await data_service.save_concepts(concepts)
            
            # 获取每个概念的成分股
            for _, concept in concepts.iterrows():
                concept_code = concept['板块名称']  # AKshare 字段名
                detail = await data_service.get_concept_stocks(concept_code)
                if detail is not None:
                    await data_service.save_concept_detail(concept_code, detail)
        
        logger.info("概念股成分更新完成")
        return {"status": "success"}
        
    except Exception as e:
        logger.error(f"更新概念股成分失败: {e}")
        raise self.retry(exc=e)
```

@current_app.task(bind=True, name='tasks.update_lhb_data')
@retry_with_fallback(max_retries=2, countdown=60)
async def update_lhb_data(self):

        logger.info("开始更新龙虎榜数据")

@current_app.task(bind=True, name='tasks.update_block_trade_data')
@retry_with_fallback(max_retries=2, countdown=60)
async def update_block_trade_data(self):
    """更新大宗交易数据"""
    try:
        logger.info("开始更新大宗交易数据")
        
        data_service = UnifiedDataService(tushare_token="your_token")
        today = datetime.now().strftime('%Y%m%d')
        
        # 获取大宗交易数据
        block_trade = await data_service.get_block_trade(trade_date=today)
        if block_trade is not None:
            await data_service.save_block_trade(block_trade)
            
        logger.info("大宗交易数据更新完成")
        return {"status": "success"}
        
    except Exception as e:
        logger.error(f"更新大宗交易数据失败: {e}")
        raise self.retry(exc=e)

@current_app.task(bind=True, name='tasks.update_shareholder_data')
@retry_with_fallback(max_retries=3, countdown=300)
async def update_shareholder_data(self):
    """更新股东数据"""
    try:
        logger.info("开始更新股东数据")
        
        data_service = UnifiedDataService(tushare_token="your_token")
        stock_codes = await data_service.get_all_stock_codes()
        
        success_count = 0
        for code in stock_codes:
            try:
                # 股东户数
                holder_num = await data_service.get_stk_holdernumber(ts_code=code)
                if holder_num is not None:
                    await data_service.save_holder_number(holder_num)
                
                # 前十大股东
                top10_holders = await data_service.get_top10_holders(ts_code=code)
                if top10_holders is not None:
                    await data_service.save_top10_holders(top10_holders)
                
                # 前十大流通股东
                top10_float = await data_service.get_top10_floatholders(ts_code=code)
                if top10_float is not None:
                    await data_service.save_top10_float_holders(top10_float)
                    
                success_count += 1
                
            except Exception as e:
                logger.warning(f"更新股票 {code} 股东数据失败: {e}")
        
        logger.info(f"股东数据更新完成，成功处理 {success_count} 只股票")
        return {"status": "success", "count": success_count}
        
    except Exception as e:
        logger.error(f"更新股东数据失败: {e}")
        raise self.retry(exc=e)

@current_app.task(bind=True, name='tasks.update_ipo_data')
@retry_with_fallback(max_retries=2, countdown=60)
async def update_ipo_data(self):
    """更新新股数据"""
    try:
        logger.info("开始更新新股数据")

#### 7.1.9 综合数据更新和维护任务
```python
# tasks/comprehensive_update.py
@current_app.task(bind=True, name='tasks.update_key_stocks_comprehensive')
@retry_with_fallback(max_retries=2, countdown=180)
async def update_key_stocks_comprehensive(self):
    """更新重点股票综合数据"""
    try:
        logger.info("开始更新重点股票综合数据")
        
        data_service = UnifiedDataService(tushare_token="your_token")
        
        # 获取重点关注股票列表
        key_stocks = await data_service.get_key_stocks_list()
        
        success_count = 0
        for stock_code in key_stocks:
            try:
                # 获取综合数据
                comprehensive_data = await data_service.get_comprehensive_stock_data(stock_code)
                if comprehensive_data is not None:
                    await data_service.save_comprehensive_data(stock_code, comprehensive_data)
                    success_count += 1
            except Exception as e:
                logger.warning(f"更新股票 {stock_code} 综合数据失败: {e}")
        
        logger.info(f"重点股票综合数据更新完成，成功处理 {success_count} 只股票")
        return {"status": "success", "count": success_count}
        
    except Exception as e:
        logger.error(f"更新重点股票综合数据失败: {e}")
        raise self.retry(exc=e)

# tasks/maintenance.py
@current_app.task(bind=True, name='tasks.data_integrity_check')
@retry_with_fallback(max_retries=1, countdown=60)
async def data_integrity_check(self):
    """数据完整性检查"""
    try:
        logger.info("开始数据完整性检查")
        
        data_service = UnifiedDataService(tushare_token="your_token")
        
        # 检查数据完整性
        integrity_report = await data_service.check_data_integrity()
        
        # 记录检查结果
        await data_service.save_integrity_report(integrity_report)
        
        # 如果发现问题，发送告警
        if integrity_report.get('issues'):
            await data_service.send_data_alert(integrity_report)
            
        logger.info("数据完整性检查完成")
        return {"status": "success", "report": integrity_report}
        
    except Exception as e:
        logger.error(f"数据完整性检查失败: {e}")
        raise self.retry(exc=e)

@current_app.task(bind=True, name='tasks.data_source_health_check')
@retry_with_fallback(max_retries=1, countdown=30)
async def data_source_health_check(self):
    """数据源健康检查"""
    try:
        logger.info("开始数据源健康检查")
        
        data_service = UnifiedDataService(tushare_token="your_token")
        
        # 检查TUshare健康状态
        tushare_health = await data_service.check_tushare_health()
        
        # 检查AKshare健康状态
        akshare_health = await data_service.check_akshare_health()
        
        health_report = {
            'tushare': tushare_health,
            'akshare': akshare_health,
            'timestamp': datetime.now().isoformat()
        }
        
        # 保存健康检查结果
        await data_service.save_health_report(health_report)
        
        logger.info("数据源健康检查完成")
        return {"status": "success", "health": health_report}
        
    except Exception as e:
        logger.error(f"数据源健康检查失败: {e}")
        raise self.retry(exc=e)

@current_app.task(bind=True, name='tasks.data_cleanup')
@retry_with_fallback(max_retries=1, countdown=120)
async def data_cleanup(self):
    """数据清理任务"""
    try:
        logger.info("开始数据清理任务")
        
        data_service = UnifiedDataService(tushare_token="your_token")
        
        # 清理过期数据
        cleanup_result = await data_service.cleanup_expired_data()
        
        # 优化数据库
        await data_service.optimize_database()
        
        logger.info(f"数据清理完成: {cleanup_result}")
        return {"status": "success", "cleanup_result": cleanup_result}
        
    except Exception as e:
        logger.error(f"数据清理失败: {e}")
        raise self.retry(exc=e)
```

### 7.2 Celery配置

#### 7.2.1 增强版Celery配置文件
```python
# celery_config.py
from celery import Celery
from celery.schedules import crontab
import os
import logging

# 配置日志
logging.basicConfig(level=logging.INFO)
logger = logging.getLogger(__name__)

# Celery配置
app = Celery('stock_system')

# Redis作为消息代理和结果后端
app.conf.update(
    broker_url='redis://localhost:6379/1',
    result_backend='redis://localhost:6379/2',
    
    # 任务序列化
    task_serializer='json',
    accept_content=['json'],
    result_serializer='json',
    
    # 时区设置
    timezone='Asia/Shanghai',
    enable_utc=True,
    
    # 多队列任务路由配置
    task_routes={
        # 基础数据更新队列
        'tasks.update_stock_basic_data': {'queue': 'data_update'},
        'tasks.update_daily_historical_data': {'queue': 'data_update'},
        'tasks.update_daily_basic_data': {'queue': 'data_update'},
        
        # 实时数据队列
        'tasks.update_realtime_quotes': {'queue': 'realtime'},
        'tasks.update_fund_flow_data': {'queue': 'realtime'},
        'tasks.update_market_sentiment': {'queue': 'realtime'},
        'tasks.update_hot_stocks': {'queue': 'realtime'},
        
        # 财务数据队列
        'tasks.update_financial_statements': {'queue': 'financial'},
        'tasks.update_financial_indicators': {'queue': 'financial'},
        'tasks.update_dividend_data': {'queue': 'financial'},
        'tasks.update_forecast_data': {'queue': 'financial'},
        
        # 板块概念队列
        'tasks.update_sector_data': {'queue': 'sector'},
        'tasks.update_concept_stocks': {'queue': 'sector'},
        
        # 特殊事件队列
        'tasks.update_lhb_data': {'queue': 'events'},
        'tasks.update_block_trade_data': {'queue': 'events'},
        'tasks.update_shareholder_data': {'queue': 'events'},
        'tasks.update_ipo_data': {'queue': 'events'},
        'tasks.update_margin_data': {'queue': 'events'},
        'tasks.update_repurchase_data': {'queue': 'events'},
        
        # 研究分析队列
        'tasks.update_research_data': {'queue': 'research'},
        'tasks.update_news_data': {'queue': 'research'},
        
        # 宏观经济队列
        'tasks.update_macro_data': {'queue': 'macro'},
        
        # 跨市场数据队列
        'tasks.update_cross_market_data': {'queue': 'cross_market'},
        
        # 综合数据队列
        'tasks.update_key_stocks_comprehensive': {'queue': 'comprehensive'},
        'tasks.update_market_overview_comprehensive': {'queue': 'comprehensive'},
        
        # 技术分析队列
        'tasks.update_nine_turn_signals': {'queue': 'analysis'},
        'tasks.update_technical_indicators': {'queue': 'analysis'},
        
        # 维护队列
        'tasks.data_integrity_check': {'queue': 'maintenance'},
        'tasks.data_source_health_check': {'queue': 'maintenance'},
        'tasks.data_cleanup': {'queue': 'maintenance'},
    },
    
    # 队列优先级配置
    task_queue_max_priority=10,
    task_default_priority=5,
    worker_prefetch_multiplier=1,
    
    # 任务重试配置 - 支持数据源切换重试
    task_acks_late=True,
    task_default_retry_delay=60,  # 重试延迟60秒
    task_max_retries=3,           # 最大重试3次
    
    # 任务超时设置
    task_soft_time_limit=600,     # 软超时10分钟
    task_time_limit=1200,         # 硬超时20分钟
    
    # 工作进程配置
    worker_concurrency=8,
    worker_max_tasks_per_child=1000,
    worker_disable_rate_limits=True,
    
    # 结果过期时间
    result_expires=3600,  # 1小时
    
    # 任务压缩
    task_compression='gzip',
    result_compression='gzip',
    
    # 错误处理
    task_reject_on_worker_lost=True,
    task_ignore_result=False,
)

# 队列配置
app.conf.task_queues = {
    'data_update': {
        'exchange': 'data_update',
        'exchange_type': 'direct',
        'routing_key': 'data_update',
    },
    'realtime': {
        'exchange': 'realtime',
        'exchange_type': 'direct',
        'routing_key': 'realtime',
    },
    'financial': {
        'exchange': 'financial',
        'exchange_type': 'direct',
        'routing_key': 'financial',
    },
    'sector': {
        'exchange': 'sector',
        'exchange_type': 'direct',
        'routing_key': 'sector',
    },
    'events': {
        'exchange': 'events',
        'exchange_type': 'direct',
        'routing_key': 'events',
    },
    'research': {
        'exchange': 'research',
        'exchange_type': 'direct',
        'routing_key': 'research',
    },
    'macro': {
        'exchange': 'macro',
        'exchange_type': 'direct',
        'routing_key': 'macro',
    },
    'cross_market': {
        'exchange': 'cross_market',
        'exchange_type': 'direct',
        'routing_key': 'cross_market',
    },
    'comprehensive': {
        'exchange': 'comprehensive',
        'exchange_type': 'direct',
        'routing_key': 'comprehensive',
    },
    'analysis': {
        'exchange': 'analysis',
        'exchange_type': 'direct',
        'routing_key': 'analysis',
    },
    'maintenance': {
        'exchange': 'maintenance',
        'exchange_type': 'direct',
        'routing_key': 'maintenance',
    },
}

# 任务重试装饰器 - 支持数据源切换
def retry_with_fallback(max_retries=3, countdown=60):
    """
    支持数据源切换的重试装饰器
    """
    def decorator(func):
        def wrapper(self, *args, **kwargs):
            try:
                return func(self, *args, **kwargs)
            except Exception as exc:
                # 记录重试信息
                logger.warning(f"任务 {func.__name__} 第 {self.request.retries + 1} 次执行失败")
                logger.warning(f"错误信息: {exc}")
                
                # 如果是数据源相关错误，在重试时会自动切换数据源
                if self.request.retries < max_retries:
                    retry_countdown = countdown * (self.request.retries + 1)
                    logger.info(f"将在 {retry_countdown} 秒后重试")
                    raise self.retry(countdown=retry_countdown, exc=exc)
                else:
                    logger.error(f"任务 {func.__name__} 达到最大重试次数，放弃执行")
                    raise exc
        return wrapper
    return decorator

# 导入所有任务模块
from tasks import (
    daily_update,
    realtime_update,
    financial_update,
    sector_update,
    events_update,
    research_update,
    macro_update,
    comprehensive_update,
    maintenance
)
```

#### 7.2.2 启动脚本配置
```bash
#!/bin/bash
# start_celery.sh

# 设置环境变量
export PYTHONPATH=/app:$PYTHONPATH
export CELERY_BROKER_URL=redis://localhost:6379/1
export CELERY_RESULT_BACKEND=redis://localhost:6379/2

# 启动多个Worker处理不同队列
echo "启动Celery Workers..."

# 高优先级实时数据Worker (4个进程)
celery -A celery_config worker \
    --loglevel=info \
    --queues=realtime \
    --concurrency=4 \
    --hostname=realtime@%h \
    --max-tasks-per-child=500 &

# 基础数据更新Worker (2个进程)
celery -A celery_config worker \
    --loglevel=info \
    --queues=data_update \
    --concurrency=2 \
    --hostname=data_update@%h \
    --max-tasks-per-child=100 &

# 财务数据Worker (2个进程)
celery -A celery_config worker \
    --loglevel=info \
    --queues=financial \
    --concurrency=2 \
    --hostname=financial@%h \
    --max-tasks-per-child=100 &

# 综合处理Worker (处理多个队列)
celery -A celery_config worker \
    --loglevel=info \
    --queues=sector,events,research,macro,cross_market,comprehensive,analysis \
    --concurrency=3 \
    --hostname=general@%h \
    --max-tasks-per-child=200 &

# 维护任务Worker (1个进程)
celery -A celery_config worker \
    --loglevel=info \
    --queues=maintenance \
    --concurrency=1 \
    --hostname=maintenance@%h \
    --max-tasks-per-child=50 &

# 启动Beat调度器
echo "启动Celery Beat..."
celery -A celery_config beat \
    --loglevel=info \
    --schedule=/tmp/celerybeat-schedule \
    --pidfile=/tmp/celerybeat.pid &

# 启动Flower监控
echo "启动Celery Flower..."
celery -A celery_config flower \
    --port=5555 \
    --broker=redis://localhost:6379/1 &

echo "所有Celery服务已启动"
echo "Flower监控界面: http://localhost:5555"

# 等待所有后台进程
wait
```

# docker-compose.celery.yml
version: '3.8'

services:
  # Redis服务
  redis:
    image: redis:7-alpine
    ports:
      - "6379:6379"
    volumes:
      - redis_data:/data
    command: redis-server --appendonly yes

  # 实时数据Worker

      - CELERY_BROKER_URL=redis://redis:6379/1

    restart: unless-stopped

  celery-data:
    build: .

      - DATABASE_URL=postgresql://user:password@postgres:5432/stock_db
    restart: unless-stopped

  # Flower监控
  celery-flower:
    build: .
    command: celery -A celery_config flower --port=5555 --broker=redis://redis:6379/1
    ports:
      - "5555:5555"
    volumes:
      - .:/app

    environment:
      - CELERY_BROKER_URL=redis://redis:6379/1
      - CELERY_RESULT_BACKEND=redis://redis:6379/2
    restart: unless-stopped

volumes:
  redis_data:
  celery_beat_data:

#### 7.2.4 任务监控和错误处理
```python
# tasks/monitoring.py
from celery.signals import task_failure, task_success, task_retry, worker_ready
import logging
import json
from datetime import datetime
from services.notification_service import NotificationService

logger = logging.getLogger(__name__)
notification_service = NotificationService()

@worker_ready.connect
def worker_ready_handler(sender=None, **kwargs):
    """Worker启动处理"""
    logger.info(f"Celery Worker {sender.hostname} 已启动")

@task_failure.connect
def task_failure_handler(sender=None, task_id=None, exception=None, traceback=None, einfo=None):
    """任务失败处理"""
    error_info = {
        'task_name': sender.name,
        'task_id': task_id,
        'exception': str(exception),
        'timestamp': datetime.now().isoformat(),
        'hostname': sender.hostname if hasattr(sender, 'hostname') else 'unknown'
    }
    
    logger.error(f"任务失败: {json.dumps(error_info, ensure_ascii=False)}")
    
    # 发送告警通知 (重要任务失败时)
    if is_critical_task(sender.name):
        notification_service.send_alert(
            title=f"关键任务失败: {sender.name}",
            message=f"任务ID: {task_id}\n错误: {exception}",
            level="error"
        )

@task_success.connect
def task_success_handler(sender=None, result=None, **kwargs):
    """任务成功处理"""
    success_info = {
        'task_name': sender.name,
        'result': result if isinstance(result, dict) else str(result),
        'timestamp': datetime.now().isoformat()
    }
    
    logger.info(f"任务成功: {json.dumps(success_info, ensure_ascii=False)}")

@task_retry.connect
def task_retry_handler(sender=None, task_id=None, reason=None, einfo=None, **kwargs):
    """任务重试处理"""
    retry_info = {
        'task_name': sender.name,
        'task_id': task_id,
        'reason': str(reason),
        'retry_count': kwargs.get('retries', 0),
        'timestamp': datetime.now().isoformat()
    }
    
    logger.warning(f"任务重试: {json.dumps(retry_info, ensure_ascii=False)}")

def is_critical_task(task_name):
    """判断是否为关键任务"""
    critical_tasks = [
        'tasks.update_realtime_quotes',
        'tasks.update_daily_historical_data',
        'tasks.data_integrity_check',
        'tasks.data_source_health_check'
    ]
    return task_name in critical_tasks

# 任务性能监控
class TaskPerformanceMonitor:
    def __init__(self):
        self.task_stats = {}
    
    def record_task_execution(self, task_name, execution_time, success=True):
        """记录任务执行统计"""
        if task_name not in self.task_stats:
            self.task_stats[task_name] = {
                'total_executions': 0,
                'successful_executions': 0,
                'failed_executions': 0,
                'total_time': 0,
                'avg_time': 0
            }
        
        stats = self.task_stats[task_name]
        stats['total_executions'] += 1
        stats['total_time'] += execution_time
        stats['avg_time'] = stats['total_time'] / stats['total_executions']
        
        if success:
            stats['successful_executions'] += 1
        else:
            stats['failed_executions'] += 1
    
    def get_task_stats(self, task_name=None):
        """获取任务统计信息"""
        if task_name:
            return self.task_stats.get(task_name, {})
        return self.task_stats

# 全局性能监控实例
performance_monitor = TaskPerformanceMonitor()
```
```

## 8. 部署配置

### 8.0 生产环境部署要求

#### 8.0.1 服务器环境要求
- **操作系统**: Ubuntu Server 22.04 LTS 或更高版本
- **CPU**: 最低4核心，推荐8核心以上
- **内存**: 最低8GB，推荐16GB以上
- **存储**: 最低100GB SSD，推荐500GB以上
- **网络**: 稳定的互联网连接，带宽不低于100Mbps

#### 8.0.2 Ubuntu Server 22+ 系统初始化
```bash
#!/bin/bash
# scripts/ubuntu_server_init.sh

# 更新系统包
sudo apt update && sudo apt upgrade -y

# 安装必要的系统工具
sudo apt install -y \
    curl \
    wget \
    git \
    vim \
    htop \
    unzip \
    software-properties-common \
    apt-transport-https \
    ca-certificates \
    gnupg \
    lsb-release

# 安装Docker
curl -fsSL https://download.docker.com/linux/ubuntu/gpg | sudo gpg --dearmor -o /usr/share/keyrings/docker-archive-keyring.gpg
echo "deb [arch=$(dpkg --print-architecture) signed-by=/usr/share/keyrings/docker-archive-keyring.gpg] https://download.docker.com/linux/ubuntu $(lsb_release -cs) stable" | sudo tee /etc/apt/sources.list.d/docker.list > /dev/null
sudo apt update
sudo apt install -y docker-ce docker-ce-cli containerd.io

# 安装Docker Compose
sudo curl -L "https://github.com/docker/compose/releases/download/v2.20.0/docker-compose-$(uname -s)-$(uname -m)" -o /usr/local/bin/docker-compose
sudo chmod +x /usr/local/bin/docker-compose

# 将当前用户添加到docker组
sudo usermod -aG docker $USER

# 启用Docker服务
sudo systemctl enable docker
sudo systemctl start docker

# 配置防火墙
sudo ufw allow 22/tcp    # SSH
sudo ufw allow 80/tcp    # HTTP
sudo ufw allow 443/tcp   # HTTPS
sudo ufw allow 8080/tcp  # API
sudo ufw allow 3000/tcp  # Frontend
sudo ufw --force enable

# 配置时区
sudo timedatectl set-timezone Asia/Shanghai

# 配置系统限制
echo "* soft nofile 65536" | sudo tee -a /etc/security/limits.conf
echo "* hard nofile 65536" | sudo tee -a /etc/security/limits.conf

# 优化内核参数
echo "vm.max_map_count=262144" | sudo tee -a /etc/sysctl.conf
echo "net.core.somaxconn=65535" | sudo tee -a /etc/sysctl.conf
sudo sysctl -p

echo "Ubuntu Server 22+ 初始化完成！"
echo "请重新登录以使docker组权限生效"
```

#### 8.0.3 24小时运行服务配置
```bash
#!/bin/bash
# scripts/setup_24h_service.sh

# 创建systemd服务文件
sudo tee /etc/systemd/system/stock-trading-system.service > /dev/null <<EOF
[Unit]
Description=Stock Trading System
Requires=docker.service
After=docker.service

[Service]
Type=oneshot
RemainAfterExit=yes
WorkingDirectory=/opt/stock-trading-system
ExecStart=/usr/local/bin/docker-compose up -d
ExecStop=/usr/local/bin/docker-compose down
TimeoutStartSec=0

[Install]
WantedBy=multi-user.target
EOF

# 启用服务
sudo systemctl daemon-reload
sudo systemctl enable stock-trading-system.service

# 创建自动重启脚本
sudo tee /opt/stock-trading-system/scripts/auto_restart.sh > /dev/null <<'EOF'
#!/bin/bash
# 检查服务状态并自动重启

LOG_FILE="/var/log/stock-system-monitor.log"
DATE=$(date '+%Y-%m-%d %H:%M:%S')

# 检查Docker容器状态
check_container_health() {
    local container_name=$1
    local status=$(docker inspect --format='{{.State.Health.Status}}' $container_name 2>/dev/null)
    
    if [ "$status" != "healthy" ]; then
        echo "[$DATE] Container $container_name is unhealthy, restarting..." >> $LOG_FILE
        docker restart $container_name
        return 1
    fi
    return 0
}

# 检查关键容器
containers=("stock-backend" "stock-frontend" "stock-db" "stock-redis" "stock-celery-worker" "stock-celery-beat")

for container in "${containers[@]}"; do
    if ! docker ps --format "table {{.Names}}" | grep -q $container; then
        echo "[$DATE] Container $container is not running, starting system..." >> $LOG_FILE
        cd /opt/stock-trading-system
        docker-compose up -d
        break
    fi
done

# 检查系统资源
cpu_usage=$(top -bn1 | grep "Cpu(s)" | awk '{print $2}' | awk -F'%' '{print $1}')
memory_usage=$(free | grep Mem | awk '{printf("%.1f", $3/$2 * 100.0)}')

if (( $(echo "$cpu_usage > 90" | bc -l) )); then
    echo "[$DATE] High CPU usage: $cpu_usage%" >> $LOG_FILE
fi

if (( $(echo "$memory_usage > 90" | bc -l) )); then
    echo "[$DATE] High memory usage: $memory_usage%" >> $LOG_FILE
fi
EOF

chmod +x /opt/stock-trading-system/scripts/auto_restart.sh

# 添加到crontab (每5分钟检查一次)
(crontab -l 2>/dev/null; echo "*/5 * * * * /opt/stock-trading-system/scripts/auto_restart.sh") | crontab -

echo "24小时运行服务配置完成！"
```

#### 8.0.4 生产环境监控配置
```yaml
# monitoring/docker-compose.monitoring.yml
version: '3.8'

services:
  # Prometheus 监控
  prometheus:
    image: prom/prometheus:latest
    container_name: stock-prometheus
    ports:
      - "9090:9090"
    volumes:
      - ./monitoring/prometheus.yml:/etc/prometheus/prometheus.yml
      - prometheus_data:/prometheus
    command:
      - '--config.file=/etc/prometheus/prometheus.yml'
      - '--storage.tsdb.path=/prometheus'
      - '--web.console.libraries=/etc/prometheus/console_libraries'
      - '--web.console.templates=/etc/prometheus/consoles'
      - '--storage.tsdb.retention.time=200h'
      - '--web.enable-lifecycle'
    restart: unless-stopped

  # Grafana 可视化
  grafana:
    image: grafana/grafana:latest
    container_name: stock-grafana
    ports:
      - "3001:3000"
    environment:
      - GF_SECURITY_ADMIN_PASSWORD=admin123
    volumes:
      - grafana_data:/var/lib/grafana
      - ./monitoring/grafana/provisioning:/etc/grafana/provisioning
    restart: unless-stopped

  # Node Exporter 系统监控
  node-exporter:
    image: prom/node-exporter:latest
    container_name: stock-node-exporter
    ports:
      - "9100:9100"
    volumes:
      - /proc:/host/proc:ro
      - /sys:/host/sys:ro
      - /:/rootfs:ro
    command:
      - '--path.procfs=/host/proc'
      - '--path.rootfs=/rootfs'
      - '--path.sysfs=/host/sys'
      - '--collector.filesystem.mount-points-exclude=^/(sys|proc|dev|host|etc)($$|/)'
    restart: unless-stopped

volumes:
  prometheus_data:
  grafana_data:
