### 8.1 Docker 配置

#### 8.1.1 后端Dockerfile (FastAPI)
```dockerfile
# backend/Dockerfile
FROM python:3.11-slim

WORKDIR /app

# 安装系统依赖
RUN apt-get update && apt-get install -y \
    gcc \
    g++ \
    && rm -rf /var/lib/apt/lists/*

# 复制依赖文件
COPY requirements.txt .
RUN pip install --no-cache-dir -r requirements.txt

# 复制应用代码
COPY . .

# 端口管理脚本
COPY scripts/check_port.sh /usr/local/bin/
RUN chmod +x /usr/local/bin/check_port.sh

EXPOSE 8080

# 启动前检查端口并启动服务
CMD ["/bin/bash", "-c", "/usr/local/bin/check_port.sh && uvicorn main:app --host 0.0.0.0 --port 8080"]
```

#### 8.1.2 前端Dockerfile (React.js)
```dockerfile
# frontend/Dockerfile
FROM node:18-alpine

WORKDIR /app

# 复制package文件
COPY package*.json ./
RUN npm install

# 复制源代码
COPY . .

# 构建应用
RUN npm run build

# 使用nginx提供静态文件服务
FROM nginx:alpine
COPY --from=0 /app/dist /usr/share/nginx/html
COPY nginx.conf /etc/nginx/nginx.conf

EXPOSE 3000

CMD ["nginx", "-g", "daemon off;"]
```

#### 8.1.3 docker-compose.yml
```yaml
version: '3.8'

services:
  # 前端服务 (React.js)
  frontend:
    build: ./frontend
    ports:
      - "3000:3000"
    depends_on:
      - backend
    environment:
      - REACT_APP_API_URL=http://localhost:9000/api/v1

  # 后端服务 (FastAPI)
  backend:
    build: ./backend
    ports:
      - "8080:8080"
    environment:
      - DATABASE_URL=postgresql://stockuser:stockpass@db:5432/stock_db
      - REDIS_URL=redis://redis:6379
      - TUSHARE_TOKEN=${TUSHARE_TOKEN}
      - SECRET_KEY=${SECRET_KEY}
    depends_on:
      - db
      - redis
    volumes:
      - ./backend:/app
    restart: unless-stopped

  # PostgreSQL 数据库
  db:
    image: postgres:15
    environment:
      - POSTGRES_DB=stock_db
      - POSTGRES_USER=stockuser
      - POSTGRES_PASSWORD=stockpass
    volumes:
      - postgres_data:/var/lib/postgresql/data
      - ./init.sql:/docker-entrypoint-initdb.d/init.sql
    ports:
      - "5432:5432"
    restart: unless-stopped

  # Redis 缓存
  redis:
    image: redis:7-alpine
    ports:
      - "6379:6379"
    volumes:
      - redis_data:/data
    restart: unless-stopped

  # Celery 工作进程
  celery-worker:
    build: ./backend
    command: celery -A tasks worker --loglevel=info
    environment:
      - DATABASE_URL=postgresql://stockuser:stockpass@db:5432/stock_db
      - REDIS_URL=redis://redis:6379
      - TUSHARE_TOKEN=${TUSHARE_TOKEN}
    depends_on:
      - db
      - redis
    volumes:
      - ./backend:/app
    restart: unless-stopped

  # Celery 定时任务
  celery-beat:
    build: ./backend
    command: celery -A tasks beat --loglevel=info
    environment:
      - DATABASE_URL=postgresql://stockuser:stockpass@db:5432/stock_db
      - REDIS_URL=redis://redis:6379
      - TUSHARE_TOKEN=${TUSHARE_TOKEN}
    depends_on:
      - db
      - redis
    volumes:
      - ./backend:/app
    restart: unless-stopped

  # Nginx 反向代理 (可选)
  nginx:
    image: nginx:alpine
    ports:
      - "80:80"
    volumes:
      - ./nginx.conf:/etc/nginx/nginx.conf
    depends_on:
      - frontend
      - backend
    restart: unless-stopped

volumes:
  postgres_data:
  redis_data:
```

### 8.2 环境配置

#### 8.2.1 后端依赖 (requirements.txt)
```
# FastAPI 核心
fastapi==0.104.1
uvicorn[standard]==0.24.0

# 数据库
sqlalchemy==2.0.23
psycopg2-binary==2.9.9

#### 8.2.3 启动脚本

**后端启动脚本 (start_backend.py)**
```python
#!/usr/bin/env python3
# scripts/start_backend.py

import uvicorn
import sys
import os
sys.path.append(os.path.dirname(os.path.dirname(os.path.abspath(__file__))))

from utils.port_manager import PortManager

def main():
    port = 8080
    port_manager = PortManager(port)
    
    try:
        # 确保端口可用
        port_manager.ensure_port_available()
        
        # 启动FastAPI应用
        print(f"启动股票交易系统后端服务，端口: {port}")
        uvicorn.run(
            "main:app",
            host="0.0.0.0",
            port=port,
            reload=True,
            log_level="info"
        )
    except Exception as e:
        print(f"启动失败: {e}")
        sys.exit(1)

if __name__ == "__main__":
    main()
```

**前端启动脚本 (start_frontend.sh)**
```bash
#!/bin/bash
# scripts/start_frontend.sh

cd frontend

# 检查Node.js版本
NODE_VERSION=$(node -v | cut -d'v' -f2 | cut -d'.' -f1)
if [ "$NODE_VERSION" -lt "16" ]; then
    echo "错误: 需要Node.js 16或更高版本"
    exit 1
fi

# 安装依赖
if [ ! -d "node_modules" ]; then
    echo "安装前端依赖..."
    npm install
fi

# 启动开发服务器
echo "启动前端开发服务器，端口: 3000"
npm run dev
```

**一键启动脚本 (start_all.sh)**
```bash
#!/bin/bash
# scripts/start_all.sh

echo "=== 股票交易系统启动脚本 ==="

# 检查Docker是否运行
if ! docker info > /dev/null 2>&1; then
    echo "错误: Docker未运行，请先启动Docker"
    exit 1
fi

# 启动数据库和缓存服务
echo "启动数据库和缓存服务..."
docker-compose up -d db redis

# 等待数据库启动
echo "等待数据库启动..."
sleep 10

# 运行数据库迁移
echo "运行数据库迁移..."
cd backend
python -m alembic upgrade head
cd ..

# 启动后端服务
echo "启动后端服务..."
python scripts/start_backend.py &
BACKEND_PID=$!

# 等待后端启动
sleep 5

# 启动前端服务
echo "启动前端服务..."
bash scripts/start_frontend.sh &
FRONTEND_PID=$!

# 启动Celery服务
echo "启动Celery服务..."
docker-compose up -d celery-worker celery-beat

echo "=== 所有服务已启动 ==="
echo "前端地址: http://localhost:3000"
echo "后端地址: http://localhost:9000"
echo "API文档: http://localhost:9000/docs"

# 等待用户输入退出
read -p "按Enter键停止所有服务..."

# 停止服务
echo "停止服务..."
kill $BACKEND_PID $FRONTEND_PID
docker-compose down

echo "所有服务已停止"
```

### 8.3 生产环境部署流程

#### 8.3.1 Ubuntu Server 22+ 生产环境部署

**步骤1: 服务器初始化**
```bash
# 1. 连接到Ubuntu Server 22+
ssh root@your-server-ip

# 2. 创建部署用户
useradd -m -s /bin/bash stockuser
usermod -aG sudo stockuser
su - stockuser

# 3. 执行系统初始化脚本
wget https://raw.githubusercontent.com/your-repo/stock-system/main/scripts/ubuntu_server_init.sh
chmod +x ubuntu_server_init.sh
./ubuntu_server_init.sh

# 4. 重新登录以使docker组权限生效
exit
ssh stockuser@your-server-ip
```

**步骤2: 部署应用**
```bash
# 1. 创建应用目录
sudo mkdir -p /opt/stock-trading-system
sudo chown stockuser:stockuser /opt/stock-trading-system
cd /opt/stock-trading-system

# 2. 克隆代码仓库
git clone https://github.com/your-repo/stock-trading-system.git .

# 3. 配置环境变量
cp .env.example .env
vim .env  # 编辑配置文件

# 示例配置
cat > .env << EOF
# 数据源配置
TUSHARE_TOKEN=your_tushare_token_here
AKSHARE_ENABLED=true

# 数据库配置
POSTGRES_DB=stock_db
POSTGRES_USER=stockuser
POSTGRES_PASSWORD=your_secure_password_here
DATABASE_URL=postgresql://stockuser:your_secure_password_here@db:5432/stock_db

# Redis配置
REDIS_URL=redis://redis:6379

# 安全配置
SECRET_KEY=your_very_secure_secret_key_here
JWT_SECRET_KEY=your_jwt_secret_key_here

# 系统配置
ENVIRONMENT=production
DEBUG=false
LOG_LEVEL=INFO

# 监控配置
PROMETHEUS_ENABLED=true
GRAFANA_ADMIN_PASSWORD=your_grafana_password_here
EOF

# 4. 构建和启动服务
docker-compose build
docker-compose up -d

# 5. 等待服务启动
sleep 30

# 6. 初始化数据库
docker-compose exec backend python -m alembic upgrade head

# 7. 创建初始数据
docker-compose exec backend python scripts/init_data.py
```

**步骤3: 配置24小时运行服务**
```bash
# 1. 设置24小时运行服务
./scripts/setup_24h_service.sh

# 2. 启动系统服务
sudo systemctl start stock-trading-system.service
sudo systemctl status stock-trading-system.service

# 3. 验证服务状态
docker ps
curl http://localhost:9000/api/v1/health
curl http://localhost:3000
```

**步骤4: 配置监控和告警**
```bash
# 1. 启动监控服务
docker-compose -f monitoring/docker-compose.monitoring.yml up -d

# 2. 配置Grafana仪表板
# 访问 http://your-server-ip:3001
# 用户名: admin, 密码: 在.env中配置的密码

# 3. 导入预配置的仪表板
docker-compose exec grafana grafana-cli plugins install grafana-piechart-panel
docker restart stock-grafana

# 4. 配置告警规则
cp monitoring/alert-rules.yml /opt/stock-trading-system/monitoring/
docker restart stock-prometheus
```

#### 8.3.2 A股交易日自动化部署验证

**验证实时数据同步 (9:30启动)**
```bash
# 1. 检查定时任务配置
docker-compose exec celery-beat celery -A tasks inspect scheduled

# 2. 手动触发实时数据同步测试
docker-compose exec celery-worker celery -A tasks call tasks.start_realtime_data_sync

# 3. 检查Redis中的实时数据
docker-compose exec redis redis-cli
> KEYS stock_quotes:*
> HGETALL stock_quotes:20240101

# 4. 检查WebSocket连接
curl -i -N -H "Connection: Upgrade" \
     -H "Upgrade: websocket" \
     -H "Sec-WebSocket-Key: SGVsbG8sIHdvcmxkIQ==" \
     -H "Sec-WebSocket-Version: 13" \
     http://localhost:9000/ws/realtime
```

**验证交易结束数据处理 (15:00)**
```bash
# 1. 手动触发交易结束处理
docker-compose exec celery-worker celery -A tasks call tasks.end_of_day_data_processing

# 2. 检查数据迁移状态
docker-compose exec backend python -c "
from database import get_db
from models import StockDaily
from datetime import datetime

db = next(get_db())
today = datetime.now().strftime('%Y-%m-%d')
count = db.query(StockDaily).filter(StockDaily.trade_date == today).count()
print(f'今日数据条数: {count}')
"

# 3. 检查Redis数据清理
docker-compose exec redis redis-cli
> KEYS *:20240101
```

**验证九转选股自动执行 (16:00)**
```bash
# 1. 手动触发九转选股
docker-compose exec celery-worker celery -A tasks call tasks.nine_turn_stock_selection

# 2. 检查选股结果
docker-compose exec backend python -c "
from database import get_db
from models import NineTurnResult
from datetime import datetime

db = next(get_db())
today = datetime.now().strftime('%Y-%m-%d')
buy_signals = db.query(NineTurnResult).filter(
    NineTurnResult.signal_date == today,
    NineTurnResult.buy_signal == True
).count()
sell_signals = db.query(NineTurnResult).filter(
    NineTurnResult.signal_date == today,
    NineTurnResult.sell_signal == True
).count()
print(f'买入信号: {buy_signals}个, 卖出信号: {sell_signals}个')
"

# 3. 查看选股报告
ls -la /opt/stock-trading-system/reports/
cat /opt/stock-trading-system/reports/nine_turn_selection_$(date +%Y%m%d).json
```

#### 8.3.3 系统健康检查和维护

**每日健康检查脚本**
```bash
#!/bin/bash
# scripts/daily_health_check.sh

LOG_FILE="/var/log/stock-system-health.log"
DATE=$(date '+%Y-%m-%d %H:%M:%S')

echo "[$DATE] 开始每日健康检查..." >> $LOG_FILE

# 1. 检查容器状态
echo "检查容器状态..." >> $LOG_FILE
docker ps --format "table {{.Names}}\t{{.Status}}" | grep -E "(stock-|Exited)" >> $LOG_FILE

# 2. 检查数据库连接
echo "检查数据库连接..." >> $LOG_FILE
docker-compose exec -T backend python -c "
from database import engine
try:
    with engine.connect() as conn:
        result = conn.execute('SELECT 1')
        print('数据库连接正常')
except Exception as e:
    print(f'数据库连接失败: {e}')
" >> $LOG_FILE

# 3. 检查Redis连接
echo "检查Redis连接..." >> $LOG_FILE
docker-compose exec -T redis redis-cli ping >> $LOG_FILE

# 4. 检查API健康状态
echo "检查API健康状态..." >> $LOG_FILE
curl -s http://localhost:9000/api/v1/health | jq . >> $LOG_FILE

# 5. 检查磁盘空间
echo "检查磁盘空间..." >> $LOG_FILE
df -h | grep -E "(/$|/opt)" >> $LOG_FILE

# 6. 检查内存使用
echo "检查内存使用..." >> $LOG_FILE
free -h >> $LOG_FILE

# 7. 检查最近的错误日志
echo "检查最近的错误日志..." >> $LOG_FILE
docker-compose logs --tail=10 backend | grep -i error >> $LOG_FILE

echo "[$DATE] 每日健康检查完成" >> $LOG_FILE
echo "----------------------------------------" >> $LOG_FILE
```

**系统备份脚本**
```bash
#!/bin/bash
# scripts/backup_system.sh

BACKUP_DIR="/opt/backups/stock-system"
DATE=$(date '+%Y%m%d_%H%M%S')
BACKUP_PATH="$BACKUP_DIR/$DATE"

mkdir -p $BACKUP_PATH

# 1. 备份数据库
echo "备份数据库..."
docker-compose exec -T db pg_dump -U stockuser stock_db > $BACKUP_PATH/database_$DATE.sql

# 2. 备份Redis数据
echo "备份Redis数据..."
docker-compose exec -T redis redis-cli BGSAVE
sleep 5
docker cp stock-redis:/data/dump.rdb $BACKUP_PATH/redis_$DATE.rdb

# 3. 备份配置文件
echo "备份配置文件..."
cp .env $BACKUP_PATH/
cp docker-compose.yml $BACKUP_PATH/
cp -r monitoring/ $BACKUP_PATH/

# 4. 压缩备份文件
echo "压缩备份文件..."
cd $BACKUP_DIR
tar -czf stock_system_backup_$DATE.tar.gz $DATE/
rm -rf $DATE/

# 5. 清理旧备份（保留最近7天）
find $BACKUP_DIR -name "stock_system_backup_*.tar.gz" -mtime +7 -delete

echo "备份完成: $BACKUP_DIR/stock_system_backup_$DATE.tar.gz"
```

#### 8.3.4 故障恢复流程

**数据库故障恢复**
```bash
# 1. 停止相关服务
docker-compose stop backend celery-worker celery-beat

# 2. 备份当前数据库（如果可能）
docker-compose exec db pg_dump -U stockuser stock_db > emergency_backup.sql

# 3. 恢复数据库
docker-compose exec -T db psql -U stockuser -d stock_db < latest_backup.sql

# 4. 重启服务
docker-compose start backend celery-worker celery-beat

# 5. 验证数据完整性
docker-compose exec backend python scripts/verify_data_integrity.py
```

**Redis故障恢复**
```bash
# 1. 停止Redis容器
docker-compose stop redis

# 2. 恢复Redis数据
docker cp latest_redis_backup.rdb stock-redis:/data/dump.rdb

# 3. 重启Redis
docker-compose start redis

# 4. 验证数据恢复
docker-compose exec redis redis-cli
> KEYS *
> INFO keyspace
```

## 附录

### A. API错误码定义
- 200: 成功
- 400: 请求参数错误
- 401: 未授权
- 403: 禁止访问
- 404: 资源不存在
- 500: 服务器内部错误

详细的数据库字段说明和业务规则定义。

## 12. 前端设计详细说明

### 12.0 UI设计规范和参考模版

#### 12.0.1 股票详情页设计规范（参考同花顺APP）

基于同花顺APP的股票详情页面设计，我们的股票详情页将采用以下设计规范：

**页面布局结构：**
```
┌─────────────────────────────────────────┐
│ 顶部导航栏                                │
│ [返回] 股票名称(代码) [收藏] [分享] [更多]    │
├─────────────────────────────────────────┤
│ 股票基本信息区域                           │
│ ┌─────────────────┬─────────────────────┐ │
│ │ 当前价格 16.43   │ 涨跌幅 -0.73%       │ │
│ │ 涨跌额 -0.12     │ 成交量 300401       │ │
│ │ 开盘 16.51       │ 最高 16.59          │ │
│ │ 昨收 16.55       │ 最低 16.40          │ │
│ └─────────────────┴─────────────────────┘ │
├─────────────────────────────────────────┤
│ K线图表区域                               │
│ ┌─────────────────────────────────────┐   │
│ │ [分时] [日K] [周K] [月K] [5分] [15分] │   │
│ │                                     │   │
│ │     K线图表显示区域                   │   │
│ │                                     │   │
│ │     成交量柱状图                     │   │
│ │                                     │   │
│ │     技术指标图表(MACD/KDJ/RSI)       │   │
│ └─────────────────────────────────────┘   │
├─────────────────────────────────────────┤
│ 功能按钮区域                             │
│ [买入] [卖出] [自选] [资讯] [公告] [研报]  │
├─────────────────────────────────────────┤
│ 详细数据表格                             │
│ ┌─────────────────────────────────────┐   │
│ │ 实时五档行情                         │   │
│ │ 买五 16.44 | 卖一 16.43             │   │
│ │ 买四 16.43 | 卖二 16.44             │   │
│ │ ...                                 │   │
│ └─────────────────────────────────────┘   │
│ ┌─────────────────────────────────────┐   │
│ │ 资金流向/龙虎榜/大宗交易等详细信息     │   │
│ └─────────────────────────────────────┘   │
└─────────────────────────────────────────┘
```

**设计要点：**
1. **颜色规范**：
   - 涨：红色 (#FF4D4F)
   - 跌：绿色 (#52C41A)
   - 平：灰色 (#8C8C8C)
   - 背景：白色/深色主题切换

2. **字体规范**：
   - 主要价格：24px，加粗
   - 次要信息：14px，常规
   - 标签文字：12px，常规

3. **间距规范**：
   - 模块间距：16px
   - 内容间距：8px
   - 边距：12px

#### 12.0.2 自选股页面UI设计模版

**页面布局：**
```
┌─────────────────────────────────────────┐
│ 顶部搜索栏                               │
│ [🔍 搜索股票代码/名称]        [编辑] [+]  │
├─────────────────────────────────────────┤
│ 分组标签                                 │
│ [全部] [沪深] [港股] [美股] [自定义分组]   │
├─────────────────────────────────────────┤
│ 股票列表                                 │
│ ┌─────────────────────────────────────┐   │
│ │ 花园生物 300401                      │   │
│ │ 16.43  -0.12  -0.73%               │   │
│ │ ████████████████░░░░ 成交量          │   │
│ │ [分时图缩略图]                       │   │
│ └─────────────────────────────────────┘   │
│ ┌─────────────────────────────────────┐   │
│ │ 聚光科技 300203                      │   │
│ │ 15.10  0.00  0.00%                 │   │
│ │ ████████░░░░░░░░░░░░ 成交量          │   │
│ │ [分时图缩略图]                       │   │
│ └─────────────────────────────────────┘   │
│ ... 更多股票                             │
├─────────────────────────────────────────┤
│ 底部操作栏                               │
│ [全选] [删除] [分组] [排序] [刷新]        │
└─────────────────────────────────────────┘
```

#### 12.0.3 九转系列选股UI设计模版

**页面布局：**
```
┌─────────────────────────────────────────┐
│ 策略选择区域                             │
│ ┌─────────────────────────────────────┐   │
│ │ [九转买入] [九转卖出] [九转确认]      │   │
│ │ [自定义策略] [历史回测]              │   │
│ └─────────────────────────────────────┘   │
├─────────────────────────────────────────┤
│ 筛选条件区域                             │
│ ┌─────────────────────────────────────┐   │
│ │ 市场: [全部▼] 板块: [全部▼]          │   │
│ │ 价格区间: [5-50] 市值: [50亿以上]     │   │
│ │ 成交量: [活跃] 信号强度: [强▼]       │   │
│ │           [重置] [筛选]              │   │
│ └─────────────────────────────────────┘   │
├─────────────────────────────────────────┤
│ 选股结果列表                             │
│ ┌─────────────────────────────────────┐   │
│ │ 序号 | 股票 | 价格 | 涨跌幅 | 信号 | 操作│   │
│ │  1   花园生物 16.43 -0.73% 买入9  [+] │   │
│ │  2   聚光科技 15.10  0.00% 买入8  [+] │   │
│ │  3   美康生物 44.48 -0.67% 卖出9  [+] │   │
│ │ ...                                 │   │
│ └─────────────────────────────────────┘   │
├─────────────────────────────────────────┤
│ 统计信息区域                             │
│ ┌─────────────────────────────────────┐   │
│ │ 总计: 156只 | 买入信号: 89只          │   │
│ │ 卖出信号: 67只 | 成功率: 73.2%       │   │
│ │ 最后更新: 2024-01-15 15:30          │   │
│ └─────────────────────────────────────┘   │
└─────────────────────────────────────────┘
```

**九转信号显示规范：**
1. **买入信号**：
   - 九转买入1-9：绿色圆圈，数字1-9
   - 确认信号：绿色实心圆圈
   - 强度指示：颜色深浅表示信号强度

2. **卖出信号**：
   - 九转卖出1-9：红色圆圈，数字1-9
   - 确认信号：红色实心圆圈
   - 强度指示：颜色深浅表示信号强度

3. **信号图标设计**：
```css
.nine-turn-signal {
  display: inline-block;
  width: 24px;
  height: 24px;
  border-radius: 50%;
  text-align: center;
  line-height: 24px;
  font-size: 12px;
  font-weight: bold;
  color: white;
}

.buy-signal {
  background: linear-gradient(135deg, #52c41a, #389e0d);
  border: 2px solid #52c41a;
}

.sell-signal {
  background: linear-gradient(135deg, #ff4d4f, #cf1322);
  border: 2px solid #ff4d4f;
}

.confirmed-signal {
  box-shadow: 0 0 8px rgba(0,0,0,0.3);
  animation: pulse 2s infinite;
}
```

#### 12.0.4 响应式设计规范

**断点设置：**
- 手机端：< 768px
- 平板端：768px - 1024px
- 桌面端：> 1024px

**适配规则：**
1. **手机端**：
   - 单列布局
   - 隐藏次要信息
   - 大按钮设计
   - 手势操作支持

2. **平板端**：
   - 双列布局
   - 保留主要功能
   - 适中的按钮尺寸

3. **桌面端**：
   - 多列布局
   - 完整功能展示
   - 鼠标悬停效果

### 12.1 技术栈选择

#### 12.1.1 核心框架
- **React 18**: 前端框架，支持并发特性和自动批处理
- **TypeScript**: 类型安全的 JavaScript 超集，提供更好的开发体验
- **Vite**: 快速的构建工具和开发服务器，支持热模块替换

#### 12.1.2 状态管理
- **Redux Toolkit**: 现代化的 Redux 状态管理，简化样板代码
- **RTK Query**: 数据获取和缓存解决方案，自动处理加载状态

#### 12.1.3 UI 组件库
- **Ant Design**: 企业级 UI 设计语言和组件库
- **Ant Design Pro Components**: 高级业务组件，如 ProTable、ProForm

#### 12.1.4 图表库
- **ECharts**: 强大的数据可视化图表库，支持 K 线图
- **@ant-design/charts**: 基于 G2Plot 的 React 图表组件

#### 12.1.5 工具库
- **Axios**: HTTP 客户端，支持请求拦截和响应拦截
- **Socket.io-client**: WebSocket 客户端，支持实时数据推送
- **dayjs**: 轻量级日期处理库
- **lodash**: 实用工具库

### 12.3 核心组件设计

#### 12.3.1 应用入口组件
```typescript
// src/App.tsx
import React from 'react';
import { BrowserRouter as Router, Routes, Route, Navigate } from 'react-router-dom';
import { ConfigProvider, App as AntApp } from 'antd';
import { Provider } from 'react-redux';
import zhCN from 'antd/locale/zh_CN';

import { store } from './store';
import Layout from './components/Layout';
import Home from './pages/Home';
import StockDetail from './pages/StockDetail';
import Watchlist from './pages/Watchlist';
import NineTurn from './pages/NineTurn';
import Login from './pages/Login';
import ErrorBoundary from './components/Common/ErrorBoundary';
import { useAuth } from './hooks/useAuth';

import './styles/global.css';

const ProtectedRoute: React.FC<{ children: React.ReactNode }> = ({ children }) => {
  const { isAuthenticated } = useAuth();
  
  return isAuthenticated ? <>{children}</> : <Navigate to="/login" replace />;
};

const App: React.FC = () => {
  return (
    <Provider store={store}>
      <ConfigProvider 
        locale={zhCN}
        theme={{
          token: {
            colorPrimary: '#1890ff',
            borderRadius: 6,
          },
        }}
      >
        <AntApp>
          <ErrorBoundary>
            <Router>
              <Routes>
                <Route path="/login" element={<Login />} />
                <Route path="/" element={
                  <ProtectedRoute>
                    <Layout>
                      <Routes>
                        <Route index element={<Home />} />
                        <Route path="stock/:tsCode" element={<StockDetail />} />
                        <Route path="watchlist" element={<Watchlist />} />
                        <Route path="nine-turn" element={<NineTurn />} />
                      </Routes>
                    </Layout>
                  </ProtectedRoute>
                } />
              </Routes>
            </Router>
          </ErrorBoundary>
        </AntApp>
      </ConfigProvider>
    </Provider>
  );
};

export default App;
```

#### 12.3.2 布局组件
```typescript
// src/components/Layout/index.tsx
import React, { useState, useEffect } from 'react';
import { Layout as AntLayout, Menu, Avatar, Dropdown, Space, Badge, Button } from 'antd';
import { 
  HomeOutlined, 
  StarOutlined, 
  TrendingUpOutlined,
  UserOutlined,
  LogoutOutlined,
  SettingOutlined,
  BellOutlined,
  MenuFoldOutlined,
  MenuUnfoldOutlined
} from '@ant-design/icons';
import { useNavigate, useLocation } from 'react-router-dom';
import { useSelector, useDispatch } from 'react-redux';

import { RootState } from '../../store';
import { logout } from '../../store/slices/authSlice';
import WebSocketService from '../../services/websocket';
import { useWebSocket } from '../../hooks/useWebSocket';

const { Header, Sider, Content } = AntLayout;

interface LayoutProps {
  children: React.ReactNode;
}

const Layout: React.FC<LayoutProps> = ({ children }) => {
  const [collapsed, setCollapsed] = useState(false);
  const navigate = useNavigate();
  const location = useLocation();
  const dispatch = useDispatch();
  
  const { user } = useSelector((state: RootState) => state.auth);
  const { notifications } = useSelector((state: RootState) => state.notification);
  
  // 初始化 WebSocket 连接
  useWebSocket();

  const menuItems = [
    {
      key: '/',
      icon: <HomeOutlined />,
      label: '市场首页',
    },
    {
      key: '/watchlist',
      icon: <StarOutlined />,
      label: '自选股',
    },
    {
      key: '/nine-turn',
      icon: <TrendingUpOutlined />,
      label: '九转选股',
    },
  ];

  const userMenuItems = [
    {
      key: 'profile',
      icon: <UserOutlined />,
      label: '个人资料',
    },
    {
      key: 'settings',
      icon: <SettingOutlined />,
      label: '系统设置',
    },
    {
      type: 'divider' as const,
    },
    {
      key: 'logout',
      icon: <LogoutOutlined />,
      label: '退出登录',
      danger: true,
    },
  ];

  const handleMenuClick = ({ key }: { key: string }) => {
    navigate(key);
  };

  const handleUserMenuClick = ({ key }: { key: string }) => {
    if (key === 'logout') {
      dispatch(logout());
      navigate('/login');
    }
  };

  return (
    <AntLayout style={{ minHeight: '100vh' }}>
      <Sider 
        trigger={null} 
        collapsible 
        collapsed={collapsed}
        style={{
          background: '#fff',
          boxShadow: '2px 0 8px rgba(0,0,0,0.15)',
        }}
      >
        <div style={{ 
          height: 64, 
          display: 'flex', 
          alignItems: 'center', 
          justifyContent: 'center',
          borderBottom: '1px solid #f0f0f0'
        }}>
          <h2 style={{ margin: 0, color: '#1890ff' }}>
            {collapsed ? 'ST' : 'Stock Trader'}
          </h2>
        </div>
        <Menu
          mode="inline"
          selectedKeys={[location.pathname]}
          items={menuItems}
          onClick={handleMenuClick}
          style={{ borderRight: 0 }}
        />
      </Sider>
      
      <AntLayout>
        <Header style={{ 
          padding: '0 16px', 
          background: '#fff', 
          display: 'flex', 
          alignItems: 'center',
          justifyContent: 'space-between',
          boxShadow: '0 2px 8px rgba(0,0,0,0.15)'
        }}>
          <Button
            type="text"
            icon={collapsed ? <MenuUnfoldOutlined /> : <MenuFoldOutlined />}
            onClick={() => setCollapsed(!collapsed)}
            style={{ fontSize: '16px', width: 64, height: 64 }}
          />
          
          <Space size="middle">
#### 12.3.3 股票详情页组件（基于同花顺APP设计）

```typescript
// src/pages/StockDetail/index.tsx
import React, { useState, useEffect } from 'react';
import { useParams, useNavigate } from 'react-router-dom';
import { 
  Card, 
  Row, 
  Col, 
  Statistic, 
  Button, 
  Tabs, 
  Table, 
  Space,
  Typography,
  Tag,
  Divider,
  message
} from 'antd';
import { 
  ArrowLeftOutlined, 
  StarOutlined, 
  StarFilled,
  ShareAltOutlined,
  MoreOutlined,
  RiseOutlined,
  FallOutlined
} from '@ant-design/icons';

import KLineChart from '../../components/Charts/KLineChart';
import RealtimeQuotes from '../../components/StockDetail/RealtimeQuotes';
import TechnicalIndicators from '../../components/StockDetail/TechnicalIndicators';
import { useStockDetail, useAddToWatchlist } from '../../hooks/useStock';
import { formatPrice, formatPercent, formatVolume } from '../../utils/format';

const { Title, Text } = Typography;
const { TabPane } = Tabs;

const StockDetail: React.FC = () => {
  const { tsCode } = useParams<{ tsCode: string }>();
  const navigate = useNavigate();
  const [activeTab, setActiveTab] = useState('realtime');
  const [chartPeriod, setChartPeriod] = useState('1d');
  
  const { data: stockData, loading } = useStockDetail(tsCode!);
  const { mutate: addToWatchlist } = useAddToWatchlist();

  if (loading || !stockData) {
    return <div>加载中...</div>;
  }

  const { basic, quote, technical } = stockData;
  const isRising = quote.change >= 0;

  const handleAddToWatchlist = () => {
    addToWatchlist(tsCode!, {
      onSuccess: () => message.success('已添加到自选股'),
      onError: () => message.error('添加失败')
    });
  };

  return (
    <div style={{ padding: '0', background: '#f5f5f5', minHeight: '100vh' }}>
      {/* 顶部导航栏 */}
      <Card 
        style={{ 
          margin: 0, 
          borderRadius: 0,
          borderBottom: '1px solid #f0f0f0'
        }}
        bodyStyle={{ padding: '12px 16px' }}
      >
        <Row justify="space-between" align="middle">
          <Col>
            <Space>
              <Button 
                type="text" 
                icon={<ArrowLeftOutlined />} 
                onClick={() => navigate(-1)}
              />
              <div>
                <Text strong style={{ fontSize: '16px' }}>
                  {basic.name}
                </Text>
                <Text type="secondary" style={{ marginLeft: 8 }}>
                  {basic.ts_code}
                </Text>
              </div>
            </Space>
          </Col>
          <Col>
            <Space>
              <Button 
                type="text" 
                icon={basic.is_favorite ? <StarFilled /> : <StarOutlined />}
                onClick={handleAddToWatchlist}
              />
              <Button type="text" icon={<ShareAltOutlined />} />
              <Button type="text" icon={<MoreOutlined />} />
            </Space>
          </Col>
        </Row>
      </Card>

      {/* 股票基本信息区域 */}
      <Card style={{ margin: '8px 16px', borderRadius: '8px' }}>
        <Row gutter={[16, 16]}>
          <Col span={12}>
            <div style={{ textAlign: 'left' }}>
              <div style={{ 
                fontSize: '28px', 
                fontWeight: 'bold',
                color: isRising ? '#ff4d4f' : '#52c41a'
              }}>
                {formatPrice(quote.close)}
              </div>
              <Space>
                <Text style={{ 
                  color: isRising ? '#ff4d4f' : '#52c41a',
                  fontSize: '14px'
                }}>
                  {isRising ? '+' : ''}{formatPrice(quote.change)}
                </Text>
                <Text style={{ 
                  color: isRising ? '#ff4d4f' : '#52c41a',
                  fontSize: '14px'
                }}>
                  {formatPercent(quote.pct_chg)}%
                </Text>
              </Space>
            </div>
          </Col>
          <Col span={12}>
            <Row gutter={[8, 8]}>
              <Col span={12}>
                <Text type="secondary">开盘</Text>
                <div>{formatPrice(quote.open)}</div>
              </Col>
              <Col span={12}>
                <Text type="secondary">最高</Text>
                <div style={{ color: '#ff4d4f' }}>
                  {formatPrice(quote.high)}
                </div>
              </Col>
              <Col span={12}>
                <Text type="secondary">昨收</Text>
                <div>{formatPrice(quote.pre_close)}</div>
              </Col>
              <Col span={12}>
                <Text type="secondary">最低</Text>
                <div style={{ color: '#52c41a' }}>
                  {formatPrice(quote.low)}
                </div>
              </Col>
              <Col span={12}>
                <Text type="secondary">成交量</Text>
                <div>{formatVolume(quote.vol)}</div>
              </Col>
              <Col span={12}>
                <Text type="secondary">成交额</Text>
                <div>{formatVolume(quote.amount)}</div>
              </Col>
            </Row>
          </Col>
        </Row>
      </Card>

      {/* K线图表区域 */}
      <Card style={{ margin: '8px 16px', borderRadius: '8px' }}>
        <div style={{ marginBottom: '16px' }}>
          <Space>
            {['分时', '日K', '周K', '月K', '5分', '15分'].map(period => (
              <Button
                key={period}
                type={chartPeriod === period ? 'primary' : 'text'}
                size="small"
                onClick={() => setChartPeriod(period)}
              >
                {period}
              </Button>
            ))}
          </Space>
        </div>
        <KLineChart 
          tsCode={tsCode!} 
          period={chartPeriod}
          height={400}
        />
      </Card>

      {/* 功能按钮区域 */}
      <Card style={{ margin: '8px 16px', borderRadius: '8px' }}>
        <Row gutter={16}>
          <Col span={4}>
            <Button type="primary" danger block>买入</Button>
          </Col>
          <Col span={4}>
            <Button block>卖出</Button>
          </Col>
          <Col span={4}>
            <Button block onClick={handleAddToWatchlist}>自选</Button>
          </Col>
          <Col span={4}>
            <Button block>资讯</Button>
          </Col>
          <Col span={4}>
            <Button block>公告</Button>
          </Col>
          <Col span={4}>
            <Button block>研报</Button>
          </Col>
        </Row>
      </Card>

      {/* 详细数据标签页 */}
      <Card style={{ margin: '8px 16px', borderRadius: '8px' }}>
        <Tabs activeKey={activeTab} onChange={setActiveTab}>
          <TabPane tab="实时" key="realtime">
            <RealtimeQuotes tsCode={tsCode!} />
          </TabPane>
          <TabPane tab="资金" key="capital">
            <div>资金流向数据</div>
          </TabPane>
          <TabPane tab="龙虎榜" key="dragon">
            <div>龙虎榜数据</div>
          </TabPane>
          <TabPane tab="大宗" key="block">
            <div>大宗交易数据</div>
          </TabPane>
        </Tabs>
      </Card>
    </div>
  );
};

export default StockDetail;
```

#### 12.3.4 自选股页面组件

```typescript
// src/pages/Watchlist/index.tsx
import React, { useState, useEffect } from 'react';
import { 
  Card, 
  Input, 
  Button, 
  Tabs, 
  List, 
  Space,
  Typography,
  Row,
  Col,
  Checkbox,
  Dropdown,
  Menu,
  message
} from 'antd';
import { 
  SearchOutlined, 
  EditOutlined, 
  PlusOutlined,
  MoreOutlined,
  DeleteOutlined,
  FolderOutlined,
  SortAscendingOutlined
} from '@ant-design/icons';

import StockListItem from '../../components/Watchlist/StockListItem';
import AddStockModal from '../../components/Watchlist/AddStockModal';
import { useWatchlist, useDeleteFromWatchlist } from '../../hooks/useWatchlist';
import { formatPrice, formatPercent } from '../../utils/format';

const { Search } = Input;
const { Text } = Typography;
const { TabPane } = Tabs;

const Watchlist: React.FC = () => {
  const [activeTab, setActiveTab] = useState('all');
  const [searchKeyword, setSearchKeyword] = useState('');
  const [editMode, setEditMode] = useState(false);
  const [selectedStocks, setSelectedStocks] = useState<string[]>([]);
  const [addModalVisible, setAddModalVisible] = useState(false);
  
  const { data: watchlistData, loading } = useWatchlist();
  const { mutate: deleteFromWatchlist } = useDeleteFromWatchlist();

  const filteredStocks = watchlistData?.filter(stock => 
    stock.name.includes(searchKeyword) || 
    stock.ts_code.includes(searchKeyword)
  ) || [];

  const handleSelectStock = (tsCode: string, checked: boolean) => {
    if (checked) {
      setSelectedStocks([...selectedStocks, tsCode]);
    } else {
      setSelectedStocks(selectedStocks.filter(code => code !== tsCode));
    }
  };

  const handleDeleteSelected = () => {
    selectedStocks.forEach(tsCode => {
      deleteFromWatchlist(tsCode);
    });
    setSelectedStocks([]);
    setEditMode(false);
    message.success('删除成功');
  };

  const sortMenu = (
    <Menu>
      <Menu.Item key="price">按价格排序</Menu.Item>
      <Menu.Item key="change">按涨跌幅排序</Menu.Item>
      <Menu.Item key="volume">按成交量排序</Menu.Item>
      <Menu.Item key="name">按名称排序</Menu.Item>
    </Menu>
  );

  return (
    <div style={{ padding: '0', background: '#f5f5f5', minHeight: '100vh' }}>
      {/* 顶部搜索栏 */}
      <Card 
        style={{ 
          margin: 0, 
          borderRadius: 0,
          borderBottom: '1px solid #f0f0f0'
        }}
        bodyStyle={{ padding: '12px 16px' }}
      >
        <Row justify="space-between" align="middle">
          <Col flex="auto">
            <Search
              placeholder="搜索股票代码/名称"
              prefix={<SearchOutlined />}
              value={searchKeyword}
              onChange={(e) => setSearchKeyword(e.target.value)}
              style={{ borderRadius: '20px' }}
            />
          </Col>
          <Col>
            <Space>
              <Button 
                type={editMode ? 'primary' : 'text'}
                icon={<EditOutlined />}
                onClick={() => setEditMode(!editMode)}
              >
                {editMode ? '完成' : '编辑'}
              </Button>
              <Button 
                type="text" 
                icon={<PlusOutlined />}
                onClick={() => setAddModalVisible(true)}
              />
            </Space>
          </Col>
        </Row>
      </Card>

      {/* 分组标签 */}
      <Card style={{ margin: '8px 16px 0', borderRadius: '8px 8px 0 0' }}>
        <Tabs 
          activeKey={activeTab} 
          onChange={setActiveTab}
          size="small"
        >
          <TabPane tab="全部" key="all" />
          <TabPane tab="沪深" key="hs" />
          <TabPane tab="港股" key="hk" />
          <TabPane tab="美股" key="us" />
          <TabPane tab="自定义" key="custom" />
        </Tabs>
      </Card>

      {/* 股票列表 */}
      <Card 
        style={{ 
          margin: '0 16px', 
          borderRadius: '0 0 8px 8px',
          minHeight: 'calc(100vh - 200px)'
        }}
        bodyStyle={{ padding: 0 }}
      >
        <List
          dataSource={filteredStocks}
          loading={loading}
          renderItem={(stock) => (
            <StockListItem
              key={stock.ts_code}
              stock={stock}
              editMode={editMode}
              selected={selectedStocks.includes(stock.ts_code)}
              onSelect={handleSelectStock}
            />
          )}
        />
      </Card>

      {/* 底部操作栏 */}
      {editMode && (
        <Card 
          style={{ 
            margin: '8px 16px 0', 
            borderRadius: '8px',
            position: 'fixed',
            bottom: '16px',
            left: '16px',
            right: '16px',
            zIndex: 1000
          }}
          bodyStyle={{ padding: '12px 16px' }}
        >
          <Row justify="space-between" align="middle">
            <Col>
              <Checkbox
                checked={selectedStocks.length === filteredStocks.length}
                indeterminate={selectedStocks.length > 0 && selectedStocks.length < filteredStocks.length}
                onChange={(e) => {
                  if (e.target.checked) {
                    setSelectedStocks(filteredStocks.map(s => s.ts_code));
                  } else {
                    setSelectedStocks([]);
                  }
                }}
              >
                全选
              </Checkbox>
            </Col>
            <Col>
              <Space>
                <Button 
                  danger 
                  disabled={selectedStocks.length === 0}
                  onClick={handleDeleteSelected}
                >
                  删除 ({selectedStocks.length})
                </Button>
                <Button icon={<FolderOutlined />}>分组</Button>
                <Dropdown overlay={sortMenu}>
                  <Button icon={<SortAscendingOutlined />}>排序</Button>
                </Dropdown>
                <Button>刷新</Button>
              </Space>
            </Col>
          </Row>
        </Card>
      )}

      {/* 添加股票弹窗 */}
      <AddStockModal
        visible={addModalVisible}
        onCancel={() => setAddModalVisible(false)}
        onSuccess={() => {
          setAddModalVisible(false);
          message.success('添加成功');
        }}
      />
    </div>
  );
};

export default Watchlist;
```

#### 12.3.5 九转系列选股页面组件

```typescript
// src/pages/NineTurn/index.tsx
import React, { useState, useEffect } from 'react';
import { 
  Card, 
  Button, 
  Select, 
  InputNumber,
  Table, 
  Space,
  Typography,
  Row,
  Col,
  Statistic,
  Tag,
  Tooltip,
  message
} from 'antd';
import { 
  ReloadOutlined,
  DownloadOutlined,
  PlusOutlined,
  FilterOutlined
} from '@ant-design/icons';

import NineTurnSignal from '../../components/NineTurn/NineTurnSignal';
import FilterPanel from '../../components/NineTurn/FilterPanel';
import { useNineTurnSelection, useAddToWatchlist } from '../../hooks/useNineTurn';
import { formatPrice, formatPercent, formatDateTime } from '../../utils/format';

const { Text, Title } = Typography;
const { Option } = Select;

interface FilterParams {
  market: string;
  sector: string;
  priceRange: [number, number];
  marketCap: string;
  volume: string;
  signalStrength: string;
}

const NineTurn: React.FC = () => {
  const [strategy, setStrategy] = useState('buy');
  const [filterParams, setFilterParams] = useState<FilterParams>({
    market: 'all',
    sector: 'all',
    priceRange: [5, 50],
    marketCap: '5000000000',
    volume: 'active',
    signalStrength: 'strong'
  });
  const [selectedRowKeys, setSelectedRowKeys] = useState<string[]>([]);

  const { data: selectionData, loading, refetch } = useNineTurnSelection(strategy, filterParams);
  const { mutate: addToWatchlist } = useAddToWatchlist();

  const columns = [
    {
      title: '序号',
      dataIndex: 'index',
      key: 'index',
      width: 60,
      render: (_: any, __: any, index: number) => index + 1,
    },
    {
      title: '股票',
      dataIndex: 'name',
      key: 'name',
      width: 120,
      render: (name: string, record: any) => (
        <div>
          <div style={{ fontWeight: 'bold' }}>{name}</div>
          <Text type="secondary" style={{ fontSize: '12px' }}>
            {record.ts_code}
          </Text>
        </div>
      ),
    },
    {
      title: '价格',
      dataIndex: 'close',
      key: 'close',
      width: 80,
      render: (price: number) => (
        <Text strong>{formatPrice(price)}</Text>
      ),
    },
    {
      title: '涨跌幅',
      dataIndex: 'pct_chg',
      key: 'pct_chg',
      width: 80,
      render: (pct: number) => (
        <Text style={{ color: pct >= 0 ? '#ff4d4f' : '#52c41a' }}>
          {formatPercent(pct)}%
        </Text>
      ),
    },
    {
      title: '九转信号',
      dataIndex: 'nine_turn_signal',
      key: 'nine_turn_signal',
      width: 100,
      render: (signal: any) => (
        <NineTurnSignal 
          type={signal.type}
          count={signal.count}
          confirmed={signal.confirmed}
          strength={signal.strength}
        />
      ),
    },
    {
      title: '成交量',
      dataIndex: 'vol',
      key: 'vol',
      width: 100,
      render: (vol: number) => formatVolume(vol),
    },
    {
      title: '操作',
      key: 'action',
      width: 80,
      render: (_: any, record: any) => (
        <Button
          type="text"
          icon={<PlusOutlined />}
          onClick={() => handleAddToWatchlist(record.ts_code)}
        />
      ),
    },
  ];

  const handleAddToWatchlist = (tsCode: string) => {
    addToWatchlist(tsCode, {
      onSuccess: () => message.success('已添加到自选股'),
      onError: () => message.error('添加失败')
    });
  };

  const handleBatchAddToWatchlist = () => {
    selectedRowKeys.forEach(tsCode => {
      addToWatchlist(tsCode);
    });
    setSelectedRowKeys([]);
    message.success(`已添加${selectedRowKeys.length}只股票到自选股`);
  };

  const rowSelection = {
    selectedRowKeys,
    onChange: (keys: React.Key[]) => setSelectedRowKeys(keys as string[]),
  };

  return (
    <div style={{ padding: '16px', background: '#f5f5f5', minHeight: '100vh' }}>
      {/* 策略选择区域 */}
      <Card style={{ marginBottom: '16px', borderRadius: '8px' }}>
        <Row justify="space-between" align="middle">
          <Col>
            <Space size="large">
              <Button 
                type={strategy === 'buy' ? 'primary' : 'default'}
                onClick={() => setStrategy('buy')}
              >
                九转买入
              </Button>
              <Button 
                type={strategy === 'sell' ? 'primary' : 'default'}
                onClick={() => setStrategy('sell')}
              >
                九转卖出
              </Button>
              <Button 
                type={strategy === 'confirm' ? 'primary' : 'default'}
                onClick={() => setStrategy('confirm')}
              >
                九转确认
              </Button>
              <Button>自定义策略</Button>
              <Button>历史回测</Button>
            </Space>
          </Col>
          <Col>
            <Space>
              <Button icon={<ReloadOutlined />} onClick={() => refetch()}>
                刷新
              </Button>
              <Button icon={<DownloadOutlined />}>
                导出
              </Button>
            </Space>
          </Col>
        </Row>
      </Card>

      {/* 筛选条件区域 */}
      <Card style={{ marginBottom: '16px', borderRadius: '8px' }}>
        <FilterPanel
          params={filterParams}
          onChange={setFilterParams}
        />
      </Card>

      {/* 选股结果列表 */}
      <Card style={{ marginBottom: '16px', borderRadius: '8px' }}>
        <div style={{ marginBottom: '16px' }}>
          <Row justify="space-between" align="middle">
            <Col>
              <Title level={5} style={{ margin: 0 }}>
                选股结果
              </Title>
            </Col>
            <Col>
              <Space>
                {selectedRowKeys.length > 0 && (
                  <Button 
                    type="primary"
                    onClick={handleBatchAddToWatchlist}
                  >
                    批量添加到自选股 ({selectedRowKeys.length})
                  </Button>
                )}
              </Space>
            </Col>
          </Row>
        </div>
        
        <Table
          columns={columns}
          dataSource={selectionData?.stocks || []}
          loading={loading}
          rowKey="ts_code"
          rowSelection={rowSelection}
          pagination={{
            pageSize: 20,
            showSizeChanger: true,
            showQuickJumper: true,
            showTotal: (total) => `共 ${total} 条记录`,
          }}
          scroll={{ x: 800 }}
        />
      </Card>

      {/* 统计信息区域 */}
      <Card style={{ borderRadius: '8px' }}>
        <Row gutter={16}>
          <Col span={6}>
            <Statistic 
              title="总计" 
              value={selectionData?.statistics.total || 0}
              suffix="只"
            />
          </Col>
          <Col span={6}>
            <Statistic 
              title="买入信号" 
              value={selectionData?.statistics.buySignals || 0}
              suffix="只"
              valueStyle={{ color: '#52c41a' }}
            />
          </Col>
          <Col span={6}>
            <Statistic 
              title="卖出信号" 
              value={selectionData?.statistics.sellSignals || 0}
              suffix="只"
              valueStyle={{ color: '#ff4d4f' }}
            />
          </Col>
          <Col span={6}>
            <Statistic 
              title="成功率" 
              value={selectionData?.statistics.successRate || 0}
              suffix="%"
              precision={1}
            />
          </Col>
        </Row>
        <div style={{ marginTop: '16px', textAlign: 'center' }}>
          <Text type="secondary">
            最后更新: {formatDateTime(selectionData?.lastUpdate)}
          </Text>
        </div>
      </Card>
    </div>
  );
};

export default NineTurn;
```

#### 12.3.6 九转信号组件

```typescript
// src/components/NineTurn/NineTurnSignal.tsx
import React from 'react';
import { Tooltip } from 'antd';
import './NineTurnSignal.css';

interface NineTurnSignalProps {
  type: 'buy' | 'sell';
  count: number;
  confirmed?: boolean;
  strength?: 'weak' | 'medium' | 'strong';
}

const NineTurnSignal: React.FC<NineTurnSignalProps> = ({
  type,
  count,
  confirmed = false,
  strength = 'medium'
}) => {
  const getSignalClass = () => {
    let baseClass = 'nine-turn-signal';
    baseClass += type === 'buy' ? ' buy-signal' : ' sell-signal';
    if (confirmed) baseClass += ' confirmed-signal';
    baseClass += ` strength-${strength}`;
    return baseClass;
  };

  const getTooltipTitle = () => {
    const action = type === 'buy' ? '买入' : '卖出';
    const status = confirmed ? '确认' : '待确认';
    return `九转${action}信号 ${count} - ${status}`;
  };

  return (
    <Tooltip title={getTooltipTitle()}>
      <div className={getSignalClass()}>
        {count}
      </div>
    </Tooltip>
  );
};

export default NineTurnSignal;
```

```css
/* src/components/NineTurn/NineTurnSignal.css */
.nine-turn-signal {
  display: inline-block;
  width: 24px;
  height: 24px;
  border-radius: 50%;
  text-align: center;
  line-height: 24px;

  font-weight: bold;
  color: white;
  cursor: pointer;

}

  background: linear-gradient(135deg, #52c41a, #389e0d);
  border: 2px solid #52c41a;
}

  background: linear-gradient(135deg, #ff4d4f, #cf1322);
  border: 2px solid #ff4d4f;
}

.confirmed-signal {
  box-shadow: 0 0 8px rgba(0,0,0,0.3);
  animation: pulse 2s infinite;
}

.strength-weak {
  opacity: 0.6;
}

.strength-medium {
  opacity: 0.8;
}

.strength-strong {
  opacity: 1;
  transform: scale(1.1);
}

    box-shadow: 0 0 0 10px rgba(82, 196, 26, 0);
  }

    box-shadow: 0 0 0 0 rgba(82, 196, 26, 0);
  }
}

.sell-signal.confirmed-signal {

}

    box-shadow: 0 0 0 0 rgba(255, 77, 79, 0.7);
  }

    box-shadow: 0 0 0 10px rgba(255, 77, 79, 0);
  }
  100% {
    box-shadow: 0 0 0 0 rgba(255, 77, 79, 0);
  }
}

#### 12.3.7 股票列表项组件

```typescript
// src/components/Watchlist/StockListItem.tsx
import React from 'react';
import { List, Row, Col, Checkbox, Typography, Progress } from 'antd';
import { useNavigate } from 'react-router-dom';
import MiniChart from '../Charts/MiniChart';
import { formatPrice, formatPercent, formatVolume } from '../../utils/format';

const { Text } = Typography;

interface StockListItemProps {
  stock: any;
  editMode: boolean;
  selected: boolean;
  onSelect: (tsCode: string, checked: boolean) => void;
}

const StockListItem: React.FC<StockListItemProps> = ({
  stock,
  editMode,
  selected,
  onSelect
}) => {
  const navigate = useNavigate();
  const isRising = stock.pct_chg >= 0;

  const handleClick = () => {
    if (!editMode) {
      navigate(`/stock/${stock.ts_code}`);
    }
  };

  return (
    <List.Item
      style={{ 
        padding: '12px 16px',
        borderBottom: '1px solid #f0f0f0',
        cursor: editMode ? 'default' : 'pointer'
      }}
      onClick={handleClick}
    >
      <Row style={{ width: '100%' }} align="middle">
        {editMode && (
          <Col span={2}>
            <Checkbox
              checked={selected}
              onChange={(e) => onSelect(stock.ts_code, e.target.checked)}
              onClick={(e) => e.stopPropagation()}
            />
          </Col>
        )}
        
        <Col span={editMode ? 10 : 12}>
          <div>
            <Text strong style={{ fontSize: '16px' }}>
              {stock.name}
            </Text>
            <div>
              <Text type="secondary" style={{ fontSize: '12px' }}>
                {stock.ts_code}
              </Text>
            </div>
          </div>
        </Col>
        
        <Col span={6}>
          <div style={{ textAlign: 'right' }}>
            <div style={{ 
              fontSize: '16px', 
              fontWeight: 'bold',
              color: isRising ? '#ff4d4f' : '#52c41a'
            }}>
              {formatPrice(stock.close)}
            </div>
            <div style={{ 
              fontSize: '12px',
              color: isRising ? '#ff4d4f' : '#52c41a'
            }}>
              {isRising ? '+' : ''}{formatPrice(stock.change)} {formatPercent(stock.pct_chg)}%
            </div>
          </div>
        </Col>
        
        <Col span={6}>
          <div>
            <Progress
              percent={stock.volumePercent}
              showInfo={false}
              strokeColor={isRising ? '#ff4d4f' : '#52c41a'}
              size="small"
              style={{ marginBottom: '4px' }}
            />
            <Text type="secondary" style={{ fontSize: '10px' }}>
              成交量 {formatVolume(stock.vol)}
            </Text>
          </div>
          <div style={{ height: '40px', marginTop: '4px' }}>
            <MiniChart data={stock.minuteData} />
          </div>
        </Col>
      </Row>
    </List.Item>
  );
};

export default StockListItem;
```

### 12.4 响应式设计实现

#### 12.4.1 断点配置

```typescript
// src/utils/responsive.ts
export const breakpoints = {
  xs: 480,
  sm: 576,
  md: 768,
  lg: 992,
  xl: 1200,
  xxl: 1600,
};

export const useResponsive = () => {
  const [screenSize, setScreenSize] = useState({
    width: window.innerWidth,
    height: window.innerHeight,
  });

  useEffect(() => {
    const handleResize = () => {
      setScreenSize({
        width: window.innerWidth,
        height: window.innerHeight,
      });
    };

    window.addEventListener('resize', handleResize);
    return () => window.removeEventListener('resize', handleResize);
  }, []);

  return {
    isMobile: screenSize.width < breakpoints.md,
    isTablet: screenSize.width >= breakpoints.md && screenSize.width < breakpoints.lg,
    isDesktop: screenSize.width >= breakpoints.lg,
    screenSize,
  };
};
```

#### 12.4.3 移动端导航组件

```typescript
// src/components/Layout/MobileNavigation.tsx
import React from 'react';
import { TabBar } from 'antd-mobile';
import { useNavigate, useLocation } from 'react-router-dom';
import {
  AppOutline,
  SearchOutline,
  HeartOutline,
  UserOutline,
  UnorderedListOutline
} from 'antd-mobile-icons';

const MobileNavigation: React.FC = () => {
  const navigate = useNavigate();
  const location = useLocation();

  const tabs = [
    {
      key: '/dashboard',
      title: '首页',
      icon: <AppOutline />,
    },
    {
      key: '/watchlist',
      title: '自选',
      icon: <HeartOutline />,
    },
    {
      key: '/nine-turn',
      title: '九转',
      icon: <UnorderedListOutline />,
    },
    {
      key: '/search',
      title: '搜索',
      icon: <SearchOutline />,
    },
    {
      key: '/profile',
      title: '我的',
      icon: <UserOutline />,
    },
  ];

  return (
    <TabBar
      activeKey={location.pathname}
      onChange={(key) => navigate(key)}
      style={{
        position: 'fixed',
        bottom: 0,
        left: 0,
        right: 0,
        zIndex: 1000,
        backgroundColor: '#fff',
        borderTop: '1px solid #f0f0f0',
      }}
    >
      {tabs.map(item => (
        <TabBar.Item key={item.key} icon={item.icon} title={item.title} />
      ))}
    </TabBar>
  );
};

export default MobileNavigation;
```

#### 12.4.4 自适应布局Hook

```typescript
// src/hooks/useAdaptiveLayout.ts
import { useState, useEffect } from 'react';
import { useResponsive } from '../utils/responsive';

export const useAdaptiveLayout = () => {
  const { isMobile, isTablet, isDesktop } = useResponsive();
  
  const getGridConfig = () => {
    if (isMobile) {
      return {
        gutter: [8, 8],
        span: { xs: 24, sm: 12, md: 8, lg: 6 }
      };
    } else if (isTablet) {
      return {
        gutter: [12, 12],
        span: { xs: 24, sm: 12, md: 8, lg: 6 }
      };
    } else {
      return {
        gutter: [16, 16],
        span: { xs: 24, sm: 12, md: 8, lg: 6 }
      };
    }
  };

  const getTableConfig = () => {
    if (isMobile) {
      return {
        size: 'small' as const,
        scroll: { x: 800 },
        pagination: { pageSize: 10, simple: true }
      };
    } else if (isTablet) {
      return {
        size: 'middle' as const,
        scroll: { x: 1000 },
        pagination: { pageSize: 15 }
      };
    } else {
      return {
        size: 'middle' as const,
        pagination: { pageSize: 20 }
      };
    }
  };

  const getChartConfig = () => {
    if (isMobile) {
      return {
        height: 300,
        grid: { left: 40, right: 20, top: 20, bottom: 40 }
      };
    } else if (isTablet) {
      return {
        height: 400,
        grid: { left: 60, right: 40, top: 40, bottom: 60 }
      };
    } else {
      return {
        height: 500,
        grid: { left: 80, right: 60, top: 60, bottom: 80 }
      };
    }
  };

  return {
    isMobile,
    isTablet,
    isDesktop,
    gridConfig: getGridConfig(),
    tableConfig: getTableConfig(),
    chartConfig: getChartConfig(),
  };
};
```
